Enforcement Rules of 

KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation 

Wholly amended on October 27, 2021 

Amended on 
February 14, 2022; March 17, 2022; April 29, 2022; September 27, 2022, December 9, 2022 
March 9, 2023; December 28, 2023 
June 14, 2024; July 12, 2024 
February 27, 2025; July 3, 2025; July 9, 2025; November 24, 2025 
March 16, 2026; March 31, 2026 

This English version does not warrant or assume any liability or responsibility for the accuracy, 
completeness or usefulness of any  information contained herein. Only Korean version shall be 
deemed authentic.

CHAPTER I. GENERAL PROVISIONS 

§1. Purpose 

The purpose of these Enforcement Rules is to stipulate the terms of reference and the matters 
necessary for the enforcement of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation.   

§2. Professional Investors 

“A professional investor stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§2(1)15] of the KOSDAQ 
Market Listing Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “the Regulation”) shall refer to a person 
who falls under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Professional investors under subparagraphs 1 and 2 of Article 10(1) of the Enforcement 
Decree  of  the  Financial  Investment  Services  and  Capital  Markets  Act  (hereinafter 
referred to as “the Enforcement Decree of the Act”); 

2.  Professional investors under subparagraphs 1 through 10 and 13 through 16 of Article 
10(2) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act. Provided that, from among the financial 
investment  companies  under  subparagraph  8  of  Article  10(2)  of  the  Enforcement 
Decree of the Act,  the trust  business  entity, discretionary investment  business  entity 
and investment advisory business entity shall be excluded; 

3.  Professional investors under subparagraphs 3 and 10 through 13 of Article 10(3) of the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Enforcement Decree of the Act;   

4.  Business development collective investment vehicle under subparagraph 1 of [§85-2] 

of the Regulation; and [March 16, 2026] 

5.    As the professional investors equivalent to those noted in subparagraphs 1 through 4, 
those professional investors for whom the Korea Exchange (hereinafter referred to as 
“the  Exchange”)  deems  it  appropriate  to  exclude  the  shares  held  by  them  when 
calculating the number of shares owned the largest shareholder under [§2(1)13] of the 
Regulation (hereinafter referred to as “the largest shareholder”) in consideration of the 
nature of the relevant investors and the purpose of their shareholding, etc. (Amended 
on March 16, 2026) 

§3. Stocks Issued by Capital Increase without Consideration 

“The  stocks  issued  by  capital  increase  without  consideration  specified  in  the  Enforcement 
Rules” in the latter part of [§2(1)18] of the Regulation shall refer to capital increase without 
consideration in accordance with any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on March 17) 

1. The capitalization of reserve pursuant to Article 461 of the Commercial Act; and 

2. The transfer into capital pursuant to Article 30 of the Assets Revaluation Act.   

§4. Determination Criteria for Foreign Holding Company and Foreign Holding 
Company Located in Korea 

The aggregated value of stocks of the foreign subsidiaries and the total assets of foreign holding 
companies or foreign holding companies located in Korea under [§2(1)25 and §2(1)26] of the 
Regulation shall be based on the aggregated value and the total assets as the end of the latest 
business year. Provided that, in cases where documents that confirm the current value of stocks 
and the total assets are submitted after the end of the latest business year, the aggregated value 
and the total assets as of the date of the concerned documents may be accepted in lieu thereof. 

§5. Eligible Foreign Securities Markets 

“An  overseas  securities  market  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  [§2(1)33]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to any of the following securities markets: 

1.  NYSE (New York Stock Exchange); 

2.  NASDAQ Stock Market; 

3.  Euronext; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4.  Tokyo Stock Exchange;     

5.  London Stock Exchange;   

6.  Deutsche Börse; 

7.  Hong Kong Exchanges and Clearing; 

8.  Singapore Exchange; 

9.  Australian Securities Exchange; 

10. Toronto Stock Exchange; and 

11. Other overseas securities markets that are recognized by the Exchange in view of such 

factors as the reliability, liquidity, and transparency of the market. 

§6. Calculation Methods of Base Market Capitalization 

“The amount determined according to the methods stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” under 
[§2(1)34(b)] of the Regulation shall refer to the amount calculated by the method in each of 
the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Case  of  listing  stocks  or  DRs  of  foreign  stocks  issued  by  a  company  listed  on  an 
overseas securities market: The amount obtained by multiplying the arithmetic average 
of the closing prices for the past ninety (90) days from the listing application date of 
the stocks (referring to the underlying stocks for DRs of foreign stocks) listed on the 
overseas securities market by the total number of outstanding shares as of the listing 
application date. 

2.  Case of listing by making public offering both in Korea and abroad at the same time: 
The amount determined by multiplying the lower price between the primary offering 
price and the secondary offering price by the number of stocks to be listed as of the 
listing application date; and   

3.  Other cases: The amount determined by the methods that the Exchange sets separately. 

§7. Provincial Venture Companies 

“Venture  companies  located  in  the  provinces  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the 
proviso  to  [§2(1)38(a)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  venture  companies  whose  head 
offices and places of main business are located in the areas other than Seoul Metropolitan City, 
Incheon Metropolitan City and Gyeonggi Province. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§8. Accounting Standards for Foreign Subsidiaries 

(1) “The matters set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§3(3)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
the matters specified in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Details  of  the  differences  between  the  accounting  standards  adopted  by  the  foreign 
subsidiaries and the accounting standards noted in each subparagraph of [§3(2)] of the 
Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the “comparative accounting standards” in this 
paragraph); 

2.  Effects of the details noted in subparagraph 1 on the financial statements of the foreign 

subsidiaries; and 

3.  Financial statements of the latest business year prepared in the format of comparison 

by applying the comparative accounting standards to the foreign subsidiaries.   

(2) The listing applicant shall submit to the Exchange a document stating the matters noted in 
each  subparagraph  of  paragraph  (1)  along  with  the  audit  report  of  the  foreign  subsidiaries 
concerned. 

§9. Financial Documents 

“Financial statements specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the former part of [§6(3)] of the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  financial  documents  among  the  documents  for  applying  for  the 
preliminary listing review in [Annex 1]. 

§10. Notification of Result of Preliminary Listing Review   

(1)  In  accordance  with  the  proviso  to  [§6(4)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  cases  where  any  of  the 
followings  occurs,  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  result  of  preliminary  listing  review  within 
thirty (30) days (based on business days; hereinafter the same shall apply in this Article) from 
the  date  when  the  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  is  received.  Provided  that,  this 
provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  listing  applicant  pursuant  to  [§6(4)2]  of  the  Regulation. 
(Amended on December 28, 2023) 

1.  Preliminary listing reviews for prompt-transfer companies pursuant to [§31(1)] of the 

Regulation; 

2.  Preliminary  listing  reviews  for  large-sized  corporations  pursuant  to  [§32(1)]  of  the 

Regulation;   

3.  Preliminary listing reviews for listing after merger pursuant to [§75(4)]; and 

4.  Preliminary  listing  reviews  for  innovative  technology  companies  falling  under 

[§28(1)1(a)(v)]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) “Cases specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§6(5)3] of the Regulation shall refer to any 
of the following cases: (Amended on March 9, 2023) 

1.  Case where  an official challenge has been filed  against a member of the KOSDAQ 

Market Listing Committee (hereinafter referred to as “the Listing Committee”) 

2.  Case  where  additional  data  is  requested  and  reviewed  to  confirm  important  matters 
related  to  financial  status,  business  activities,  governance  structure,  internal  control 
system, etc. of applicants for preliminary listing review; 

3.  Case where the number of applicants for preliminary listing review sharply increases 
in a short period of time, where the deliberation of the Listing Committee is extended, 
or where it is necessary to finalize the financial statements; 

4.  Case  where,  considering  the  deliberation  schedule  of  the  Listing  Committee,  the 
Exchange determines that it is difficult to secure a sufficient time for review during the 
period between the application date for preliminary listing review and the meeting date 
of the Listing Committee. In such cases, the notification of the result of preliminary 
listing review may be postponed within a period of fifteen (15) days. (Amended on 
July 9, 2025) 

5.  Case where a listing sponsor of a foreign company or foreign holding company located 
in Korea, to which a quantitative cause of delisting or a cause of delisting subsequent 
to  the  listing  maintenance  review  has  occurred  within  one  (1)  year  from  the  initial 
listing  date,  makes  an  arrangement  for  initial  listing  of  stocks  of  another  foreign 
company or foreign holding company located in Korea within one (1) year from the 
day when the concerned cause for delisting was confirmed through public disclosures, 
etc. (based on the application date for preliminary listing review). In such cases, the 
notification of the result of preliminary listing review may be postponed within a period 
of one (1) month. 

(3) Outstanding export companies and any registered or designated corporations in the K-OTC 
Market which are prioritized for the review pursuant to [§6(6)] of the Regulation shall be as 
follows: (Amended on April 29, 2022) 

1.  Outstanding export companies: Venture companies whose exports account for 50/100 

or more of its total sales as of the end of the latest business year; and 

2.  Registered or designated corporations in K-OTC Market: Corporations that meet the 

requirement of each subparagraph of [§26(5)]. 

(4) Pursuant to [§6(6)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall preferentially review the listing 
applicant  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs  within  the  scope  specified  in  each 
subparagraph. Provided that, this provision shall not apply to the cases where the notification 
of the result of preliminary listing review may be made within the period mentioned in [§6(4)] 
of the Regulation: 

1.  Registered or designated corporations in K-OTC Market pursuant to paragraph (3)2: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Within 10/100 of the corporations subject to the following review; and 

2.  Provincial venture companies pursuant to [§7] or outstanding export companies under 
paragraph (3)1: Within 20/100 of the corporations subject to the following review. 

§11.  Selection  of  Specialized  Assessment  Institution  and  Specialized  Assessment 
Procedures, etc. 
(Amended on December 28, 2023) 

(1) The Exchange shall appoint a  specialized assessment institution with expertise to assess 
technical capacity, etc. of listing applicants pursuant to [§7(1)] of the Regulation. 

(2) A company that falls under any of the following subparagraphs shall undergo an assessment 
for  technology,  etc.  by  the  specialized  assessment  institution  designated  by  requesting  the 
designation of a specialized assessment institution to the Exchange: (Amended on December 
28, 2023) 

1.  A company that wishes to be listed as an innovative technology company (excluding 
the innovative technology companies falling under [§28(1)2] and [§67(1)2]). In such 
cases,  the  company  shall  go  through  an  assessment  by  the  specialized  assessment 
institution before the application date of preliminary listing review; and 

2.  Other  companies  that  the  Exchange  deems  that  an  assessment  by  the  specialized 

assessment institution is necessary for the purpose of listing review. 

(3) The service fees to be paid to the specialized assessment institution shall be borne by the 
concerned company in the case of paragraph (2)1, and by the Exchange in the case of paragraph 
(2)2. 

(4) Only in the case where the company that has gone through the assessment for technology, 
etc. pursuant to paragraph (2)1 applies for the preliminary listing review within six (6) months 
from the date of notification on the assessment result, the result of concerned assessment shall 
be valid. 

(5) In addition to the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (4), the matters necessary for the 
selection  of  specialized  assessment  institutions,  specialized  assessment  procedures  and 
assessment ratings shall be established separately by the Exchange. 

§12. Operation of Expert Meeting, etc. 
(Amended on December 28, 2023) 

(1)  Pursuant  to  [§7(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Exchange  may  establish  and  operate  expert 
meetings  for  the  purpose  of  carrying  out  a  technical  analysis  of  the  industry  to  which  the 
applicant  for  preliminary  listing  review  belongs,  obtaining  professional  and  objective 
information on the concerned industry and reflecting review opinions. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) In cases where  it deems  necessary to  obtain advice on technological  prowess  or growth 
potential, etc. of a listing applicant, the Exchange may convene an expert meeting. 

(3)  The  Exchange  shall  separately  specify  the  matters  necessary  for  the  establishment  and 
operation of the expert meeting pursuant to paragraph (1). (Amended on December 28, 2023) 

§13. Invalidation of Result of Preliminary Listing Review 

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§8(1)7] of the Regulation shall refer to any 
of the following: 

1.  Case of issuing stocks, etc. by a third-party allotment from the application date for the 
preliminary listing review to the day before the listing day. Provided that, this provision 
shall not apply to cases where the listing sponsor intends to acquire stocks to fulfill the 
investment obligations pursuant to [§13(5)] of the Regulation; and 

2.  Other  cases  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  for  public  interest  and  investor 

protection. 

(2) In cases where a listing applicant re-applies  for a preliminary listing review pursuant to 
[§8(4)] of the Regulation, the application form for each listing type specified in [Annex 1] and 
attachments thereto shall be submitted. Provided that, the submission of such documents may 
be omitted in case where the documents are identical to those submitted for the preliminary 
listing review. 

§14. Procedures for Filing an Objection to Result of Preliminary Listing Review, etc. 

(1) A  listing  applicant  who  raises  an  objection  to  the  result  of  preliminary  listing  review 
pursuant to [§10(1)] of the Regulation shall submit the following documents to the Exchange 
through its listing sponsor: 

1.  A statement of grounds for objection to the decision of the Exchange and documentary 

evidence; 

2.  An opinion letter of the listing sponsor; and 

3.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the objection. 

(2) The Exchange shall convene the KOSDAQ Market Committee (hereinafter referred to as 
“the Market Committee) within fifteen (15) days (based on business days; hereinafter the same 
shall apply in this Article) from the date when the documents pursuant to paragraph (1) were 
submitted.  In  such  cases,  the  Exchange  shall  grant  at  least  one  (1)  opportunity  to  the 
representative of the concerned listing applicant to express his/her opinion. (Amended on July 
9, 2025) 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) The Exchange shall notify the listing applicant of the outcome of deliberation within three 
(3) days from the date of deliberation and decision by the Market Committee under paragraph 
(2). In such cases, the listing applicant may not file another objection to the decision of the 
Market Committee. 

§15. Fulfillment of Obligations of Listing Sponsors, etc.   

(1) In the process of corporate due diligence pursuant to [§13(1)] of the Regulation, a listing 
sponsor  shall  receive  a  confirmation  letter,  which  proves  that  the  financial  situation  of  the 
listing  applicant  has  been  stated  in  a  true  and  accurate  manner  based  on  facts,  from  the 
representative director, etc. of the listing applicant. 

(2) A listing sponsor who has arranged an initial listing (limited to an initial listing of common 
stocks or foreign stocks), backdoor listing, or listing after merger pursuant to the main sentence 
of  [§13(4)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  submit  a  business  analysis  report  of  the  concerned 
KOSDAQ-listed corporation to the Exchange at least once for each half-year period for three 
(3)  years  from  the  date  of  listing  and  post  the  report  on  the  website  of  the  listing  sponsor. 
Provided that, in cases where the period from the listing date to the last day of the semi-annual 
period to  which  the listing date belongs is less than two (2) months, this provision  shall be 
applied from the first day of the following half-year period of the semi-annual period to which 
the date of listing belongs. 

(3) In cases where the Exchange confirmed that a listing sponsor has violated the obligation 
under paragraph (2), the Exchange may post such fact on the website, etc. of the Exchange. 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  listing  sponsor  acquires  stocks  (including  DRs  of  foreign  stocks; 
hereinafter the same shall apply in this paragraph) pursuant to [§13(5)] of the Regulation, the 
requirements in each of the following subparagraphs shall be satisfied: 

1.  Acquisition method: The stocks issued by way of private placement shall be acquired; 

2.  Acquisition  time:  The  relevant  stocks  shall  be  acquired  during  the  period  from  the 
application date for preliminary listing review to the application date for initial listing; 
and 

3.  Acquisition quantity: In cases where the listing sponsor acquires a remaining quantity 
in accordance with the underwriting agreement entered into with the listing applicant 
as no one acquired some stocks offered for primary offering or secondary offering, such 
acquisition quantity shall be included. 

(5) “In the case where the listing sponsor falls under the reasons prescribed by the Enforcement 
Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§13(5)1(b)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  case  where  a 
technology growth company for which the listing sponsor arranged listing within the past three 
(3) years as of the date of application for preliminary listing review has been designated as an 
investment attention issue or administrative issue within two (2) years after listing or the case 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
where the technology growth company falls under formal requirements for delisting or a reason 
for delisting due to the listing maintenance review. [December 28, 2023] (Previous paragraph 
(5) moved to paragraph (6) on December 28, 2023) 

(6)  Pursuant  to  [§13(8)]  of  the  Regulation,  a  listing  sponsor  shall  post  a  business  model 
evaluation report on the websites, etc. of the Exchange and the listing sponsor within seven (7) 
days from the date of notification on the approval for the preliminary listing review. Provided 
that,  any  confidential  matters,  etc.  of  the  concerned  company,  which  are  included  in  the 
business model evaluation report, may be excluded from the posting in consultation with the 
Exchange.  (Moved  from  paragraph  (5),  Previous  paragraph  (6)  moved  to  paragraph  (7)  on 
December 28, 2023) 

(7) Pursuant  to  [§13(9)  of the Regulation,  a listing sponsor shall post a report on corporate 
continuity in [Annex Form 10-2] on the websites, etc. of the Exchange and the listing sponsor 
within seven (7) days from the date of notification on the approval for the preliminary listing 
review. In such cases, the proviso  to  paragraph (6) shall apply  mutatis mutandis. [April 29, 
2022] (Moved from paragraph (6) on December 28, 2023) 

§16. Qualifications for Auditors of Foreign Companies 

(1) “A person who meets the requirements set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§15(1)1] of 
the Regulation shall refer to a person who meets all of the requirements noted in each of the 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  Five (5) years have elapsed since the incorporation; 

2.  Number of affiliated certified public accountants shall be at least fifty (50); 

3.  The sales amount of latest business year shall be KRW 10 billion or more; 

4.  Any of the following requirements shall be met: 

(a)  The sum of the reserve for damage compensation under Article 28 of the Certified 
Public Accountant Act and the joint fund for damages under Article 32 of the Act 
on  External  Audit  of  Stock  Companies  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “Act  on 
External Audit”) shall be at least KRW 2 billion; or 

(b) The compensation liability insurance policy under Article 38(1) of the Enforcement 
Decree of the Act on External Audit of Stock Companies (hereinafter referred to as 
the “Enforcement Decree of the Act on External Audit”) shall have been purchased. 

5.  Among foreign accounting auditors pursuant to Article 169(3) of the Act (hereinafter 
referred  to  as  the  “foreign  accounting  auditor”  in  this  Article),  an  agreement  for 
management of audit quality shall have been entered into with the foreign accounting 
auditor who satisfies all of the following items:   

(a)  Member companies shall be distributed in at least thirty (30) countries; and 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Number of certified public accounts affiliated with the member companies shall be 

at least 2,000. 

6.  There shall have been no such incident where the Securities and Futures Commission 
has recommended the  cancellation of business  registration or  ordered  suspension of 
business in part or in entirety during the last three (3) years. 

        7. The corporation shall be registered as an auditor of listed companies in accordance with 

Article 9-2 of the External Audit Act. [November 24, 2025] 

(2) “A person who meets the requirements set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§15(1)2] of 
the Regulation shall refer to a person who meets any of the requirements noted in each of the 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  Case where the applicant of initial listing is not a company listed on a foreign securities 

exchange: A person who meets all of the following requirements 

(a)  All requirements under subparagraphs 1 through 3 of paragraph (1) shall be met; 

and 

(b) All of the following requirements are satisfied or an agreement for management of 
audit quality shall have been entered into with the foreign accounting auditor who 
satisfies all of the following requirements: 

(i) Member companies shall be distributed in at least one hundred (100) countries; 

and 

(ii) Number of certified public accountants affiliated with the member companies 

shall be at least 100,000. 

2.  Case where the applicant of initial listing is a company listed on a foreign securities 

exchange: A person who meets all of the following requirements 

(a)  All requirements under subparagraphs 1 through 3 of paragraph (1) shall be met; 

and 

(b) All of the following requirements are satisfied or an agreement for management of 
audit quality shall have been entered into with the foreign accounting auditor who 
satisfies all of the following requirements: 

(i) Member companies shall be distributed in at least thirty (30) countries; and 

(ii) Number of certified public accounts affiliated with the member companies shall 

be at least 2,000. 

(3) “A person who meets the requirements set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§15(2)1] of 
the Regulation shall refer to a person who meets all of the requirements noted in each of the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  All requirements under each subparagraph (excluding subparagraph 5) of paragraph (1) 

shall be met; and (Amended on November 24, 2025) 

2.  An agreement for management of audit quality shall have been entered into with the 

foreign accounting auditor who satisfies all of the following requirements: 

(a)  Member companies shall be distributed in  at  least  one hundred (100) countries; 

and 

(b) Number of certified public accountants affiliated with the member companies shall 

be at least 100,000. 

(4) “A person who meets the requirements set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in [§15(2)2] of 
the Regulation shall refer to a person who meets all of the requirements in items (a) and (b) of 
paragraph (2)1. 

§17. Exceptions to Mandatory Holding, etc. 

(1) “Case specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§16(1)2] of the Regulation shall refer to any 
of  the  merger  and  acquisition,  etc.  under  of  the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
December 9, 2022) 

1. Case where it is required for improving the technical capability and product quality, cost 

reduction and enhancement of efficiency; 

2. Case where the amount of investment in research and development is excessive or it is 

required for risk diversion; 

3. Case where it is required for securing the transparency of corporate governance such as 

the appointment of professional manager; 

4.  Case where it is required for rationalizing the trading terms and conditions; and 

5.  Other cases where the Exchange deems that the effects expected from the merger or 
acquisition  is  greater  than  that  of  restricting  the  sales  of  shares  held  by  largest 
shareholders, etc. 

(2)  The  Exchange  shall,  when  reviewing  the  cases  falling  under  each  subparagraph  of 
paragraph (1), take into account the analysis of business management and the relevant opinion 
statements  by  external  assessment  institutions  prescribed  in  Article  176-5(8)  of  the 
Enforcement Decree of the Act. 

(3) The Exchange shall, in the case of accepting an exception to the mandatory holding for the 
largest shareholder, etc. pursuant to [§16(1)1 and 2] of the Regulation, disclose the relevant 
details in the form of market notice. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4)  “Other  cases  where  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules  as  deems  necessary  to  grant  an 
exception to the mandatory holding” in [§16(1)3] of the Regulation shall refer to the case where,   
as  a  case  where  the  listing  applicant  was  established  by  a  spin-off  of  a  KOSDAQ-listed 
corporation or a KOSPI-listed corporation, the Exchange recognizes that a shareholder of the 
parent  company  (referring  to  a  parent  company  pursuant  to  the  Article  342-2(1)  of  the 
Commercial Act; hereinafter the same in this paragraph) acquires the stocks, etc. in accordance 
with a shareholder protection plan, etc. for the shareholders of the parent company of the listing 
applicant. [December 9, 2022] 

(5) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§16(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to any 
of the following cases: Provided that, in cases where the events specified in subparagraphs 1 
through 4 occur with respect to stocks, etc., which are electronically registered pursuant to the 
Act on Electronic Registration of Stocks, Bonds, etc., an approval from the Exchange may not 
be obtained. 

1.  Case of exchanging for new stocks subsequent to a stock split or reverse stock split; 

2.  Case of exchanging for new stocks subsequent to a merger, split-off, or merger after 

split-off; 

3.  Case of exercising the rights over convertible stocks, convertible bonds, redeemable 

stocks, or bonds with warrants (including certificates of the subscription right); 

4.  Case of redemptions of convertible stocks, convertible bonds, redeemable stocks, or 

bonds with warrants; 

5.  Case of establishing a right of pledge for any of the following purposes to the financial 
institutions under Subparagraphs 1 through 11 Article 61(2) of the Enforcement Decree 
of the Corporate Tax Act or the securities finance companies under Article 9(17)3 of 
the Act: 

(a)  Loans to finance the operation of the issuing company (excluding special purpose 

acquisition companies); and 

(b) Loans to finance a participation in paid-in capital increase of the issuing company 
(excluding the capital increase through public offering or third-party allotment) 

6.  Case  where  the  right  of  pledge  established  under  subparagraph  5  is  changed  or 

terminated; and 

7.  Other cases where the Exchange deems that it is inevitable to withdraw the stocks, etc. 
and establish or terminate pledges, etc. in order to comply with statutory obligations. 

§18. Measures against Violations of Mandatory Holding, etc. 

(1)  In  case  of  falling  under  any  of  the  subparagraphs  of  [§17(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the 
Exchange may extend the mandatory holding period for one (1) year for each violation. In such 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
cases, the stocks, etc. whose mandatory holding period is extended shall include stocks, etc. 
that  are  mandatorily  held  by  the  person  subject  to  the  mandatory  holding,  stocks  whose 
ownership has been changed or repurchased pursuant to paragraph (2), and stocks that have 
been sold effectively by the methods noted in subparagraphs of [§17(1)] of the Regulation. 

(2) Pursuant to [§17(3)] of the Regulation, the Exchange may have the relevant corporation 
or the largest shareholder comply with the measures in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  The ownership of the stocks held under a borrowed name shall be changed; 

2.  The stocks sold among the stocks held under a borrowed name shall be repurchased. 
In such cases, the quantity sold shall be repurchased, but in cases where the amount 
repurchased is less than the amount sold, the number of stocks equivalent to the 
amount sold shall be purchased back; and 

3.  Stocks, etc. subject to mandatory holding shall be deposited with the Korea Securities 

Depository to enforce the measure of the mandatory holding. 

§19. Suspension and Resumption of Trading, etc.   

(1) The period of trading suspension under [§18(1)] of the Regulation shall be the period noted 
in each of the following subparagraphs. In such cases, the calculation of the trading suspension 
period shall be based on trading days (including the trading suspension days of the concerned 
issue)  in  each  subparagraph  of  [§4(3)]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  Regulation 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Business Regulation”): 

1.  Cases falling under [§18(1)1] of the Regulation: The day of confirming the cause (not 
applicable to cases where the cause for designation as an administrative issue is added). 
Provided that, the period of trading suspension may be extended if the Exchange deems 
it  necessary,  and  in  case  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following  items,  the  period  of 
trading suspension shall be governed by the concerned item: 

(a)  Case of having been designated as an administrative issue due to a non-submission 
of annual report pursuant to [§53(1)6] of the Regulation: The period from the date 
of being designated as an administrative issue to the submission date of the annual 
report concerned;     

(b) Case of having been designated as an administrative issue due to an application for 
commencement  of  rehabilitation  procedure  pursuant  to  [§53(1)10]  of  the 
Regulation: The period from the date of confirming the concerned cause to the date 
when  the  court  makes  its  decision  on  the  commencement  of  rehabilitation 
procedure. Provided that, in cases when the Exchange deems it necessary for public 
interest and investor protection, the trading suspension may not be lifted; 

(c)  Case of having been designated as an administrative issue due to an application for 
bankruptcy pursuant to [§53(1)11] of the Regulation: The period from the date of 
confirming the concerned cause to the date of confirming the resolution of the cause 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
for  the  designation  as  an  administrative  issue.  Provided  that,  in  cases  when  the 
Exchange deems it necessary, the trading suspension may be lifted; and 

(d) Case  where  stocks  of  a  special  purpose  acquisition  company  are  designated  as 
administrative  issues  pursuant  to  [§72(2)3  and  §72(2)4]  of  the  Regulation:  The 
period  from  the  date  of  being  designated  as  administrative  issues  to  the  date  of 
being released from such designation subject to resolution of the concerned cause. 

(e)  Case of having been designated as an administrative issue pursuant to [§85-9(1)4 
or §85-16(1)4] of the Regulation: The period from the date of being designated as 
an administrative issue to the date of release form the designation as an 
administrative issue due to the relevant cause; [March 16, 2026] 

2.  Cases falling under  [§18(1)2] of the Regulation (excluding the cause resulting from 
being listed on the KOSPI Market or merged into a KOSDAQ market-listed or KOSPI 
market-listed  corporation):  The  period  from  the  date  of  confirming  the  cause  of 
delisting (including the case of confirming that the concerned stock is subject to the 
listing maintenance review) to the day when the cause of delisting has been resolved. 
Provided that, in  the case of falling  under any of the following items,  the period of 
trading suspension shall be governed the concerned item: 

(a)  Case  where  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Corporate  Review  Committee  (hereinafter 
referred to as “the Corporate Review Committee”) or the Market Committee, which 
has  granted  an  improvement  period,  deliberated  and  decided  to  lift  the  trading 
suspension during the improvement period: The trading suspension shall be lifted 
for  a  period  specified  by  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  or  the  Market 
Committee; and 

(b) Cases falling under the cause of delisting of subscription warrants or subscription 
right certificates under [§85] of the Regulation: The trading shall be suspended 
from the date of confirming the relevant cause and the day after the date of 
confirmation. 

3.  Cases falling under [§18(1)3] of the Regulation: The period specified in each of the 

following items: 

(a)  Cases falling under the proviso to the part other than each item of [§54(1)1] of the 
Regulation: Until the time when the decision on delisting is made after confirming 
the audit opinion on the financial statements of the latest business year. 

(b) Cases where there is a report on a merger or an all-inclusive stock swap (limited to 
cases  where  the  unlisted  corporation  or  the  KONEX  market-listed  corporation 
becomes a  wholly-owned subsidiary) with  an unlisted corporation or a KONEX 
market-listed  corporation  pursuant  to  [§6]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Disclosure 
Regulation  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Disclosure  Regulation”):  From  the 
reporting date to the date of notification on whether or not it is a backdoor listing. 

(c) Cases where there is a report under [§6] of the Disclosure Regulation with respect 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
to  business  acquisition  or  asset  acquisition  stated  as  backdoor  listing  in  the 
confirmation statement (including the case where it is scheduled to be stated) in 
[Annex 17] through [Annex 20]: From the reporting date to the date of notification 
on whether or not it is a backdoor listing. 

(d) Cases where there is a report under [§6] of the Disclosure Regulation with respect 
to    an issuance of stocks through investment in-kind, which is stated as a backdoor 
listing in the confirmation statement in [Annex 21]: From the reporting date to the 
date of notification on whether or not it is a backdoor listing. 

(f)  Cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  to  confirm  whether  or  not  it  is  a 
backdoor listing even if the confirmation statement in [Annex 17] through [Annex 
21] does not state that it is a backdoor listing: From the reporting date pursuant to 
[§6] of the Disclosure Regulation to the date of notification on whether or not it is 
a backdoor listing. 

(g) Cases where the Exchange deems it necessary for investor protection and market 
management  after  the  court’s  decision  on  the  commencement  of  rehabilitation 
procedures: From the date of the decision on the trading suspension (including the 
trading  suspension  under  the  proviso  to  paragraph  (1)1(b))  to  the  date  of 
confirmation  when the cause for the trading  suspension is  deemed to  have been 
resolved. 

(h) Cases  of  confirming  that  the  cause  for  listing  maintenance  review  under  any  of 
subparagraphs  of  [§56(1)]  of  the  Regulation  has  occurred:  From  the  date  of 
confirming that the cause for listing maintenance review has occurred to the date 
on  which  the  decision  is  made  on  whether  or  not  to  be  subject  to  the  listing 
maintenance review pursuant to [§57(1)] of the Regulation. Provided that, in the 
case of a resolution or decision on a cancellation of spin-off or merger after spin-
off  stated  in  [§56(1)10]  of  the  Regulation,  it  shall  be  the  date  of  resolution  or 
decision on the cancellation. 

(i)  Cases where a decision on whether or not to be subject to the listing maintenance 
review is made in accordance with (g): From the date on which it is decided to be 
subject to the listing maintenance review to the date on which it is decided whether 
or  not  to  delist.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  of  a  resolution  or  decision  on  a 
cancellation  of  spin-off  or  merger  after  spin-off  mentioned  in  [§56(1)10]  of  the 
Regulation, it shall be the date of resolution or decision on the cancellation. 

(j)  Cases  where  a  corporation  conducts  a  listing  change  or  a  supplementary  listing 
pursuant to [§44] of the Regulation due to an increase or decrease of capital such 
as capital reduction, reverse stock split, etc., and the number of circulating stocks 
(referring  to  the  number  of  shares  calculated  by  subtracting    those  held  by  the 
largest shareholder, etc. from the number of floating stocks as    confirmed by the 
Table of Status of Circulating Stocks in [Annex: Form No. 2]; hereinafter the same 
shall apply in this item) falls short of 2/100 of the total number of common stocks 
of  the  concerned  KOSDAQ  market-listed  corporation  or  one  hundred  thousand 
(100,000)  shares:  The  period  from  the  date  of  the  relevant  listing  change  or 
supplementary listing to the date when the following reasons for release from the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
trading suspension were confirmed. In such cases, the date when the reasons for 
release from the trading suspension were confirmed shall refer to the date when it 
was confirmed pursuant to    == the Table of Status of Circulating Stocks in [Annex: 
Form No. 2] submitted by the relevant corporation for such reasons as expiration 
of the period of mandatory holding: 

(i) Case where the trading was suspended since the number of circulating stocks 
was less than 2/100 of the total number of common stocks: When the number of 
circulating  stocks  has  become  5/100  or  more  of  the  total  number  of  common 
stocks; 

(ii)  Case where the trading was suspended since the number of circulating stocks 
was  less  than  one  hundred  thousand  (100,000)  shares:  When  the  number  of 
circulating stocks has become three hundred thousand (300,000) shares or more; 
and 

(iii) Case where the trading was suspended since the number of circulating stocks     
was less than 2/100 of the total number of common stocks and at the same time 
less  than  one  hundred  thousand  (100,000)  shares:  When  the  number  of 
circulating stocks has become 5/100 or more of the total number of common 
stocks and three hundred thousand (300,000) shares or more. 

(k) Cases  where  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  or  the  Market  Committee 
deliberated  and  decided  to  terminate  the  trading  suspension  pursuant  to 
subparagraph 2(a): From the end of period for the termination of trading suspension 
specified by the Corporate Review Committee or the Market Committee to the date 
on which the cause for delisting was resolved. 

(l)  Cases  where  a  special  purpose  acquisition  company  reports  its  resolution  or 
decision  on  a  merger  with  a  corporation  pursuant  to  [§6(1)3(a)(viii)]  of  the 
Disclosure Regulation: From the reporting date to the date specified in any of the 
followings: 

(i) Case where the corporation that is the counterparty to the merger is subject to     
the eligibility review for listing after merger pursuant to [§74] of the Regulation: 
Until the date of notification on the result of the  eligibility  review for listing 
after merger. Provided that, in cases where the result of the eligibility review 
turned out ineligible, it shall be the date of resolution or decision to suspend the 
merger. 

(ii) Case where the corporation that is the counterparty to the merger is not subject 
to  the  eligibility  review  for  listing  after  merger  pursuant  to  [§74]  of  the 
Regulation and falls under any of the causes for delisting under [§73(2)9(a)(ii) 
through §73(2)9(a)(iv)] and [§73(2)9(b) or §73(2)9(c)] of the Regulation: The 
date  of  resolution  or  decision  to  suspend  the  merger.  Provided  that,  in  cases 
where it is confirmed that the corporation does not fall under any of the causes 
for delisting under [§73(2)9(a)(ii) through §73(2)9(a)(iv)] and [§73(2)9(b) or 
§73(2)9(c)] of the Regulation based on the details of a report and a confirmation 
statement at the time of the report, the trading suspension may not take place. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(m) Other cases where a trading suspension is deemed necessary for investor protection: 
One (1) day. Provided that, it may be extended in cases where the Exchange deems 
it necessary. 

(2) The provisions of paragraph (1) shall not apply during the trading period pursuant to [§23] 
of the Regulation. 

(3) In cases where the trading of a stock is suspended pursuant to paragraph (1), the Exchange 
may  suspend  the  trading  of  subscription  warrants  or  subscription  right  certificates  whose 
underlying asset is the concerned stock. 

(4)  The  Exchange  may  provide  information  on  trading  suspension  to  a  multilateral  trading 
company  when  necessary  for  investor  protection  and  market  management.  (Amended  on 
February 27, 2025) 

§20. Submission of Operation Report on Internal Accounting Management System 

(1) “Documents stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the main sentence of [§19(3)] of the 
Regulation  shall  refer  to  a  written  report  on  operation  of  internal  accounting  management 
system  in  [Annex:  Form  No.  34],  which  has  been  verified,  reviewed  and  signed  by  the 
representative director concerning the operation of the internal accounting management system, 
and contain the matters noted in each of the following subparagraphs. Provided that, in case of 
operating the internal accounting management system under the laws and regulations of home 
country,  etc.,  it  shall  refer  to  the  Korean  translation  of  the  report  on  internal  accounting 
management system prepared under the concerned laws and regulations: (Amended on April 
29, 2022) 

1.  The regulation on internal accounting management system and the matters concerning   
organizations that manage and operate the internal accounting management system; 

2.  Operating status of the internal accounting management system, which was reported 
by the internal accounting manager (referring to a standing officer who is responsible 
for management and operation of the internal accounting management system) of the 
internal accounting system to the board of directors and audit committee (referring to 
the auditor, in cases where the auditor has been appointed; hereinafter the same shall 
apply in this paragraph); 

3.  The  details  that  the  audit  committee  has  reported  to  the  board  of  directors  upon 

reviewing the documents noted in subparagraph 2; 

4.  The review and audit opinions of the auditor on the document noted in subparagraph 
2. In such cases, the auditor shall be the auditor of the financial statements of the latest 
business  year,  but  in  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  unavoidable,  the  member 
companies  of  the  relevant  auditor  noted  in  [§16(2)1(b)]  or  [§16(2)2(b)]  may  be 
included; and 

5.  Other  matters  recognized  as  necessary  by  the  Exchange  with  respect  to  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
establishment of an internal accounting management system and the appropriateness 
of its operation. 

(2) “Foreign subsidiaries specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§19(3)] of the 
Regulation shall refer to foreign subsidiaries that fall under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Subsidiaries whose sole purpose is to own the stocks of other companies; and 

2.  Subsidiaries whose total assets at the end of the latest business year are less than 10/100 

of the total assets of the holding company at the end of the latest business year. 

§21. Application Documents for Delisting, etc.   

(1) The application for delisting pursuant to the main sentence of [§22(1)] of the Regulation 
shall mean attached [Annex: Form No. 1] and the supplementary documents shall be as follows:   

1.  A  copy  of  the  minutes  on  special  resolution  of  general  meeting  of  shareholders 
concerned with the delisting. Provided that, in case of an application for delisting of 
different  class  of  shares  (including  foreign  different  class  of  shares;  hereinafter  the 
same  shall  apply  in  this  paragraph),  it  shall  be  a  copy  of  the  minutes  on  special 
resolution of general meeting of shareholders of the different class of shares; and 

2.  A copy of the listing sponsor’s consent on delisting. Provided that, this provision shall 

not apply to an application for delisting of different classes of shares. 

(2)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (1),  in  cases  where  a  delisting  has  been  requested  for  the 
purpose of listing on the KOSPI Market pursuant to [§54(1)9] of the Regulation, the application 
for delisting in [Annex: Form No. 1] and the minutes of general meeting of shareholders, which 
made  the  decision  on  delisting,  shall  be  submitted  to  apply  for  delisting.  (Amended  on 
December 9, 2022) 

(3)  The  Exchange  shall  hold  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  pursuant  to  the  proviso  to 
[§22(2)] of the Regulation within fifteen (15) days (based on business days) from the date of 
receiving an application for delisting unless there are any special reasons. 

(4) The Corporate Review Committee pursuant to the proviso to [§22(2)] of the Regulation 
shall deliberate and decide whether to delist the concerned stocks (including depository receipts 
of foreign stocks; the same shall apply in this Article) in consideration of the matters noted in 
each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Whether the largest shareholder, etc. (including the joint holders under Article 141(1) 
of the Enforcement Decree of the Act, while excluding the relevant KOSDAQ-listed 
corporation;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this  Article)  have  faithfully  observed  the 
procedures  for  shareholder  protection  by  such  means  of  acquiring  stocks  from  the 
shareholders  who  held  the  concerned  stocks  before  the  application  for  delisting 
(including  tender  offers  and  other  means  equivalent  thereto),  or  guaranteeing  the 
acquisition of the concerned stocks for a specified period after the delisting; and 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Whether the matters necessary for the realization of public interests and protection of 
investors, such as the shareholding ratios of the largest shareholder, etc. (referring to 
the ratios calculated based on the number of stocks excluding treasury stocks from the 
total number of issued stocks) and conditions for tender offer, have been satisfied. 

(5)  The  Exchange  shall,  within  three  (3)  days  (based  on  business  days)  from  the  date  of 
deliberation or resolution of the Corporate Review Committee under paragraph (4), notify the 
concerned  KOSDAQ  market-listed  corporation  in  writing  whether  the  concerned  stock  is 
delisted or not. 

CHAPTER IⅠ. LISTING AND LISTING MANAGEMENT OF COMMON STOCKS 

Section 1. Listing Requirements and Procedures 

§22. Application Documents for Preliminary Listing Review, etc. 

The  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  and  supplementary  documents  in  the  main 
sentence of [§25(1)] of the Regulation shall be specified in [Annex 1]. 

§23. Exceptions to Mandatory Holding of Initial Listing   

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§26(1)1] of the Regulation 
shall refer to any of the following subparagraphs:   

1.  Case  where  a  specially  related  person  (referring  to  a  specially  related  person  under 
[§2(1)13(b)] of the Regulation; hereinafter the same shall apply) who holds less than 
5/100 of the total number of common stocks as of the application date for listing falls 
under any of the following items:   

(a)  Where it is difficult to discover the whereabouts of the concerned specially related 

person; 

(b) Where the concerned specially related person and the largest shareholder do not 

have common interests; and 

(c)  Where the number of stocks held by the relevant specially related person is less 

than one hundred (100) shares. 

2.  Case attributable to the fulfillment of statutory obligations or court rulings. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2)  In  the  case  of  paragraph  (1)1,  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  of  the  listing  applicant  shall 
acquire the same number of stocks, etc. held by the specially related person from a person other 
than the largest shareholder, etc. on behalf of the specially related person and hold it for the 
same period as the mandatory holding period of the specially related person. Provided that, in 
cases where the Exchange deems it unavoidable, a person other than the largest shareholder, 
etc. may hold the stocks, etc. mandatorily on behalf of the concerned specially related person. 

(3) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§26(1)2] of the Regulation 
shall refer to any of the following cases: (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

1.  Case  of  an  acquisition  by  employees  who  are  members  of  the  employee  stock 

ownership association; 

2.  Where the largest  shareholder, etc.  acquires the same number of stocks, etc. from  a 
person  other  than  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  on  behalf  of  the  person  subject  to 
mandatory holding and holds it mandatorily for the relevant period. Provided that, in 
cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  unavoidable,  a  person  other  than  the  largest 
shareholder, etc. may hold the same number of stocks, etc. mandatorily on behalf for 
the relevant period;   

3.  Where  the  concerned  corporation  is  a  KONEX  market-listed  corporation  and  falls 

under any of the following items:   

(a)  Case  of  acquiring  stocks,  etc.  from  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  in  the  KONEX 

Market; and 

(b) Case of selling the stocks, etc., which were acquired before the date of listing on 

the KONEX Market, in the KONEX Market. 

4.  Case where, as a case where the listing applicant was established by a spin-off through 
carving-out  of  a  KOSDAQ-listed  corporation  or  a  KOSPI-listed  corporation,  the 
Exchange recognizes that a shareholder of the parent company (referring to a parent 
company pursuant to the Article 342-2(1) of the Commercial Act; hereinafter, the same 
in  this  subparagraph)  acquires  the  stocks,  etc.  in  accordance  with  a  shareholder 
protection plan, etc. for the shareholders of the parent company of the listing applicant. 

5.  Case attributable to the fulfillment of statutory obligations or court rulings. 

(4) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§26(1)3] of the Regulation 
shall refer to any of the following cases: 

1.  Case of acquisition by employees who are members of the employee stock ownership 

association; 

2.  Case of acquisition by a venture capital or a professional investor; 

3.  Case of acquisition by a foreign investor pursuant to the Foreign Investment Promotion 
Act, and the relevant acquired stocks, etc. have not been disposed of for one (1) year 
from the date of acquisition; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
4.  Where the largest  shareholder, etc.  acquires the same number of stocks, etc. from  a 
person  other  than  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  on  behalf  of  the  person  subject  to 
mandatory holding and holds it mandatorily for the relevant period. Provided that, in 
cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  unavoidable,  a  person  other  than  the  largest 
shareholder, etc. may hold the same number of stocks, etc. mandatorily on behalf for 
the relevant period 

5.  Where  the  concerned  corporation  is  a  KONEX  market-listed  corporation  and  falls 

under any of the following items: 

(a)  Case of acquiring stocks, etc. issued through a third-party allotment method during 

the period listed on the KONEX Market; and 

(b) Case of selling the stocks, etc., which were acquired before the date of listing on 

the KONEX Market, in the KONEX Market. 

6.  Case attributable to the fulfillment of statutory obligations or court rulings. 

(5) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§26(1)4] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  the  cases  where  the  relevant  corporation  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on April 29, 2022) 

1.  Among technology growth companies, registered or designated corporations in K-OTC 

Market that meet the requirements under [§26(5)]; 

2.  Large corporations, which are domestic enterprises; and 

3.  KONEX market-listed corporations that have been listed on the KONEX Market for at 
least one (1) year based on the date of preliminary listing review. Provided that, in cases 
where a venture capital or a professional investor acquired stocks, etc. at the KONEX 
Market  or  sold  stocks,  etc.,  which  were  acquired  before  the  listing  on  the  KONEX 
Market,  in  the  KONEX  Market,  KONEX  market-listed  corporations  that  have  been 
listed on the KONEX Market for less than one (1) year may be included.   

(6) The disparate ratio between the acquisition price and the public offering price under the 
proviso  to  [§26(1)5]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  calculated  in  accordance  with  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  Acquisition price: The arithmetic average of the acquisition prices of the stocks, etc. of 
the applicant for initial listing by weighting the number of stocks, etc. acquired by the 
listing  sponsor  during  six  (6)  months  before  the  date  of  application  for  preliminary 
listing review. In such cases, acquisition price of securities that do not correspond to 
stocks, such as convertible bonds, bonds with warrants, etc., may be calculated (based 
on the date of calculation for the acquisition price) by taking into account the number 
of shares or exercise prices in the event of conversion, listing, etc.   

2.  Public  offering  price: The  price  under Article  5(1)  of  the  Regulations  on  Securities 

Underwriting Business, etc. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3.  Disparate ratio between the acquisition price and the public offering price: The ratio 

calculated by the following formula: 

Disparate ratio between the public offering price and the acquisition price = (Public 
offering price – Acquisition price)  ÷  Acquisition price  ×  100 

§24. Criteria for Paper Companies   

(1) “A paper company stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” under the main sentence of [§26(2)] 
of the Regulation shall refer to a company that meets each of the following requirements:   

1.  It shall not be a stock-listed corporation under Article 9(15)3 of the Act or a company 

that has listed foreign stocks, etc. on the eligible overseas securities markets; 

2.  As  of  the  end  of  the  latest  business  year,  the  aggregated  value  of  stocks  of  other 
companies owned by the relevant company (hereinafter referred to as an “investment 
target company” in this Article) shall be at least 50/1000 of the total asset. Provided 
that, in the case of submitting documents that can confirm the relevant fact based on 
the current stock price and the total asset after the end of the latest business year, such 
documents may be used for the calculation; 

3.  The sales amount from profit-making activities other than those falling under any of 
the following items shall be less than 30/100 of the total sales amount based on the 
income statement of the latest business year: 

(a)  Business management of an investment target company; 

(b) Activities  related  to  funds  raising,  such  as  the  listing  and  issuance  of  stocks  or 

bonds;   

(c)  Activities that are generally required for the operation of a company, including the 
preparation  and  implementation  of  budget,  recruitment  and  administration  of 
human resources, development and operation of computer systems, etc.; and 

(d) Activities incidental to those specified in items (a) through (c). 

      4.  It  shall  not  be  a  business  development  investment  company  under  [§85-2(2)]  of  the 

Regulation. [March 16, 2026] 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1), in cases where the Exchange determines that it is necessary 
to mandatory hold the stocks, etc. held by the largest shareholder, etc. of the relevant company 
for public interests and investor protection, the relevant company may be regarded as a paper 
company even if the requirements in each subparagraph of paragraph (1) are not satisfied. 

(3)  Whether  or  not  the  company  meets  the  requirements  noted  in  each  subparagraph  of 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
paragraph (1) shall be determined based on the written confirmation on paper company and 
attached documents pursuant to [Annex: Form No. 13]. 

§25. Application Documents for Initial Listing   

The  application  for  initial  listing  and  supplementary  documents  pursuant  to  [§27(1)]  of  the 
Regulation shall be as set forth in [Annex 2]. 

§26. Application Methods for Formality Review Requirements 

(1)  “Cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  under  [§28(1)1(a)(i)]  and  [§28(2)1]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the case where, of the shares held by venture capitals and professional 
investors that are subject to the calculation of the total number of shares held by the minority 
shareholders (excluding those who hold less than 1/100 of total number of outstanding shares), 
those shares fall under the shares other than the common shares with voting rights. 

(2) “Cases where the Exchange deems it necessary in the Enforcement Rules” in [§28(1)2(a)(i)] 
of the Regulation  shall refer to  a case where, through prior consultation  with  the Exchange 
before filing a request for review, a valuation loss related to financial products subsequent to 
the conversion of class stocks has been confirmed in Annex Form No. 43. In this case, the profit 
from continuing operations before corporate tax may be calculated by applying the adjusted 
financial details according to the Confirmation of Valuation Loss Related to Financial Products 
in the format in Annex Form No. 43. [July 9, 2025] 

(3)  The  average  daily  trading  value  under  [§28(1)2(b)(vi)ⓑ]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be 
calculated by dividing the trading value for one (1) year through the KONEX Market by the 
number  of  trading  days  of  the  relevant  issue.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  the  number  of 
trading  days  of  the  concerned  issue  is  less  than  1/2  of  the  number  of  trading  days  on  the 
KONEX Market, it is deemed that the requirement is not met. [April 29, 2022] 

(4) The par value per share pursuant to [§28(1)5] of the Regulation shall be KRW 100, KRW 
200, KRW 500, KRW 1,000, KRW 2,500, and KRW 5,000. 

(5) “Equity shares stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” under [§28(2)1] of the Regulation shall 
refer to the case of subscribing for new common shares (including common stocks converted 
or  issued  by  the  exercise  of  conversion  rights  or  subscription  rights).  In  such  cases,  the 
capitalization portion of reserves for the concerned new shares transferred to equity shall be 
included. 

(6) “The corporation that meets the requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the 
main sentence of [§28(2)2] of the Regulation shall refer to a listing applicant who meets each 
of the following requirements:   

1.  The period registered pursuant to Article 7 of the Regulation on the Operation of the 
K-OTC Market or designated pursuant to Article 14 of the said Regulation shall be at 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
least one (1) year from the application date for preliminary listing review; 

2.  There shall be no record of a designation having been made pursuant to Article 49(1) 
of the Regulation on the Operation of the K-OTC Market as an unfaithful disclosure 
corporation  for  the  one  (1)-year  period  prior  to  the  application  date  for  preliminary 
listing review; and   

3.  The annual turnover ratio, calculated by dividing the trading volume for the one (1)- 
year  period  prior  to  the  application  date  for  preliminary  listing  review  by  the  total 
number of outstanding shares as of the application date of preliminary listing review, 
shall be 5/100 or higher. 

§27. Application Methods for Qualitative Review Requirements 

(1) “The qualitative review requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the former 
part of [§29(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to the qualitative review requirements in [Annex 
6]. 

(2) “The qualitative review requirements for each industry specified in the Enforcement Rules” 
in the latter part of [§29(2)] of the Regulation shall refer to the qualitative review requirements 
for each type of industry in [Annex 7]. 

(3) In cases where the contribution to the national economy is taken into account pursuant to 
[§29(3)] of the Regulation, the review may reflect the effort of the KONEX-listed corporation 
to improve shareholder value during the listing period on the KONEX Market. [April 29, 2022] 

§28. Special Cases for Technology Growth Companies   

(1) “Cases recognized for the technological prowess and growth potential in accordance with 
the Enforcement Rules” in the part other than each subparagraph of [§30(1)] of the Regulation 
shall refer to any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on April 29, 2022; December 28, 
2023) 

1.  An assessment has taken place six (6) months before the application date of preliminary 
listing review by a specialized assessment institution and the assessment result satisfies 
the following items: 

(a)  Corporations  under  [§30(1)1]  of  the  Regulation: Among  the  assessment  grades 
from  two  (2)  specialized  assessment  institutions, the  higher  grade  shall  be A  or 
higher  and  the  lower  grade  shall  be  BBB  or  higher.  Provided  that,  companies 
falling  under  any  of  the  followings  shall  have  an  A  grade  or  higher  from  a 
specialized  assessment  institution  (in  the  case  of  assessments  by  two  (2) 
specialized assessment institutions, it shall be the higher grade): 

(i) 

Companies with a base market capitalization of KRW 500 billion or more; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
or 

(ii) 

Specialized corporations for materials, components, and facilities pursuant 
to Article 2, Subparagraph 5 of the Act on Special Measures to Strengthen 
Competitiveness  of  Materials,  Components,  and  Facility  Industries  and 
Stabilize Supply Chain. 

(iii)  KONEX-listed corporations that meet all of the followings: 

ⓐ  At  least  one (1) year shall be passed from  the listing on  the KONEX 

Market; and 

ⓑ  There shall be a recommendation from the designated advisor (limited 
to the cases where the period of designation is at least six (6) months) of 
the relevant corporation 

(iv)  A  corporation  that  possesses  national  strategic  technology  (hereinafter 
referred  to  as  the  “national  strategic  technology”  in  this  Article)  under 
Subparagraph  1  of  Article  2  of  the  Special  Act  on  Fostering  of  National 
Strategic  Technology  or  national  high-tech  strategic  technology  (hereinafter 
referred to as the “national high-tech strategic technology” in this Article) under 
Subparagraph 1 of Article 2 of the Act on Special Measures for Strengthening 
and Protecting Competitiveness of National High-tech Strategic Industries and 
meet all of the followings; 

                      ⓐ  The base market capitalization shall be KRW 100 billion or more; and 

                      ⓑ  The total amount of investment [referring to investment under Paragraph 
2 of Article 2 of the Act on special Measures for Promotion of Venture 
Businesses (hereinafter referred to as the “Venture Company Act”)] made 
through venture capital financing over the last five (5) years as of the date 
of request for designation of a specialized assessment institution to the 
Exchange pursuant to [§11(2)] shall be KRW 10 billion or more. 

(v) A corporation that filed the application for preliminary listing review pursuant 
to [§30(1)1] of the Regulation but received the notification of non-approval in 
the  preliminary  listing  review  and  requested  for  designation  of  a  specialized 
assessment institution pursuant to [§11(2)] within six (6) months from the date 
of  notification  of  non-approval.  Provided  that  cases  where  the  preliminary 
listing review is not approved due to the failure to meet the qualitative review 
requirements under [§29(1)1] shall be excluded. 

(b) Corporations under [§30(1)1(a)] of the Regulation: The assessment grades from 

two (2) specialized assessment institutions shall be A or higher. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Corporations  with  a  base  market  capitalization  of  KRW  1  trillion  or  more  and  the 
technological  prowess  or  business  feasibility  is  recognized  by  examining  the 
qualitative review requirements pursuant to [§29] of the Regulation. 

(2)  “The  requirements  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  under  [§30(1)1(a)]  of  the 
Regulation  shall refer to  all of the following requirements. [December 28, 2023] <Previous 
paragraph (2) moved to paragraph (3) on December 28, 2023> 

1.  It shall be a corporation that possesses a national strategic technology or national high-

tech strategic technology; 

2.  The  largest  shareholder  under  Article  3(1)2(b)  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of 
Framework Act  on  Small  and  Medium  Enterprises  or  a  controlling  company  under 
Article 3-2(1) of the same Decree shall have held 30/100 or more of the total number 
of shares issued by the listing applicant for three (3) years or more;   

3.  The largest shareholder shall not be a company belonging to a company group subject 
to disclosure pursuant to Article 31(1) of the Monopoly Regulation and Fair Trade Act; 
and 

      4. The shares held by the largest shareholders shall be less than 50/100 of the total number 

of shares issued by the listing applicant. 

(3)  “The  requirements  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  under  [§30(1)2(b)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to all of the following requirements. Provided that, the requirements in 
each of the following subparagraphs shall not apply to a listing sponsor who is not a managing 
underwriter pursuant to the Regulation on Securities Underwriting Business, etc.: (Amended 
on  February  14,  2022;  March  9,  2023;  December  28,  2023)  <Moved  from  paragraph  (2). 
Previous paragraph (3) moved to paragraph (4) on December 28, 2023> 

1.  There shall be a record  of having  sponsored the listing of an innovative technology 
company within the past three (3) years from the date of application for preliminary 
listing review. Provided that this provision shall not apply in cases when the Exchange 
deems it inevitable due to a sudden change in market situations or economic conditions; 
and 

2.  The  foreign  holding  company  located  in  Korea  or  the  KOSDAQ-listed  foreign 
corporation whose listing was sponsored within the past three (3) years from the date 
of  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  shall  not  have  been  designated  as  an 
investment attention issue or an administrative issue pursuant to the Regulation, or not 
have fallen under a cause for delisting due to failure to meet the formality requirements 
or a cause for delisting as a result of listing maintenance review within two (2) years 
after the listing. 

(4) “The requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the former part other than each 
subparagraph  of  [§30(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  all  of  the  following  requirements.   
Provided that, the requirements in  each of the following subparagraphs shall not  apply  to  a 
listing sponsor who is  not  a managing  underwriter pursuant  to  the Regulation on Securities 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Underwriting Business, etc.: (Amended on February 14, 2022) <Moved from paragraph (3). 
Previous paragraph (4) moved to paragraph (5) on December 28, 2023> 

1.  There  shall  be  a  record  of  having  sponsored  the  listing  of  a  KOSDAQ-listed 
corporation within the past one (1) year from the date of application for preliminary 
listing review; 

2.  The KOSDAQ-listed corporation whose listing was sponsored within the past three (3) 
years from the date of application for preliminary listing review shall not have been 
designated  as  an  investment  attention  issue  or  an  administrative  issue,  or  not  have   
fallen under a cause for delisting due to failure to meet the formality requirements or a 
cause for delisting as a result of listing maintenance review within two (2) years after 
the listing; and 

3.  In addition, a listing sponsor shall not be the listing sponsor whose qualification was 

limited by the Exchange for investor protection. 

(5) In accordance with the latter part other than each subparagraph of [§30(2)] of the Regulation, 
when a listing sponsor recommends a business model company, the listing sponsor shall submit 
to the Exchange a business model company evaluation report in [Annex Form No. 10], which 
includes  the  evaluation  results  of  the  unique  business  model  and  growth  potential  of  the 
relevant corporation and the grounds therefore. (Amended on December 28, 2023) <Moved 
from paragraph (4) on December 28, 2023> 

§29. Special Cases for Prompt-Transfer Companies 

(1) The average daily trading value under [§31(1)3(f)(ii)] of the Regulation shall be calculated 
by dividing the trading value for one (1) year on the KONEX Market by the number of    trading 
days  of  the  relevant  issue.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  the  number  of  trading  days  of  the 
concerned issue is less than 1/2 of the number of trading days of the KONEX Market, it is 
deemed that the requirement is not satisfied. 

(2) The corporate continuity report pursuant to [§31(1)3(f)(iv)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
[Annex Form 10-2]. 

(3) “Requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” under [§31(1)4] of the Regulation shall 
refer to the following requirements:   

1.  There  has  not  been  any  disciplinary  measure  (excluding  cases  designated  as  an 
unfaithful  disclosure  corporation  due  to  ordinary  negligence  or  minor  negligence 
according to the KONEX Market Disclosure Regulation) from the Financial Services 
Commission or the Exchange for the past one (1) year due to a violation of the financial 
laws and regulations or the regulations of the Exchange; and 

2.  In addition, it is deemed that the realization of public interest and investor protection 

are not harmed. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Wholly amended on April 29, 2022] 

§30. Criteria for Changes in Management Rights 

(1) “The change in management right as stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the part other 
than each subparagraph of [§33(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to a case where a key investor 
(referring to a person falling under any of the subparagraphs of paragraph (2); hereinafter the 
same shall apply) of the backdoor listing target company becomes the largest shareholder of a 
common-stock-listed corporation in accordance with any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Mergers  under  [§33(1)1(a)]  of  the  Regulation  and  all-inclusive  share  swaps  under 
[§33(1)1(b)] of the Regulation: Case of becoming the largest shareholder by the merger 
ratio or exchange ratio stated in the report on material facts of the merger or the all-
inclusive share swap, or becoming the largest shareholder within one (1) year before 
the submission date of such report on material facts;   

2.  Significant business transfers under [§33(1)1(c)] of the Regulation and acquisitions of 
material assets under [§33(1)2(a)] of the Regulation: Case where, from one (1) year 
before the submission date of the report on material facts of the significant business 
transfer or the acquisition of material asset to six (6) months after the submission date, 
the  common-stock-listed  corporation  issues  stocks,  etc.  to  the  key  investor  of  the 
backdoor listing target company by way of third-party allotment or the key investor of 
the backdoor listing target company makes transactions such as contracting of trades 
and/or trading  reservation for stocks of the common-stock-listed corporation, which 
requires the reporting of a change in the largest shareholder pursuant to [§6(1)3(a)(i)] 
of the Disclosure Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the “stock transfer”) during the 
same period, and the key investor becomes the largest shareholder in accordance with 
any of the following items: 

(a)  Case of becoming the largest shareholder by acquiring the stocks issued by way of 

third-party allotment or becoming the largest shareholder through the stock transfer;   

(b) In cases where stocks, etc. are issued by way of third-party allotment or the stock 
transfer is conducted within one (1) year prior to the submission of the report on 
material  facts,  the  case  of  becoming  the  largest  shareholder  within  one  (1)  year 
prior to the submission of the report on material facts; and 

(c)  In cases where stocks, etc. are issued by way of third-party allotment or the stock 
transfer is conducted within six (6) months after the submission of the report on 
material  facts  (including  where  it  is  stated  that  such  event  is  scheduled  in  the 
confirmation statement of the backdoor listing), the case of becoming the largest 
shareholder from one (1) year prior to the submission of the report on material facts 
to the date of the issuance of stocks, etc. or the date of the reporting on the change 
in the largest shareholder pursuant to [§6(1)3(a)(i)] of the Disclosure Regulation. 

3.  Investment in kind under [§33(1)2(b)] of the Regulation: Pursuant to [§33(1)2(b)] of 
the Regulation, the common-stock-listed corporation becomes the largest shareholder 
by acquiring stocks issued by way of third-party allotment method, or it becomes the 
largest shareholder from one (1) year prior to the date of reporting on the issuance of 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the relevant stocks pursuant to [§6] of the Disclosure Regulation.   

4.  Transactions under [§33(1)3] of the Regulation: In the case where the Exchange deems 
that  it  is  equivalent  to  the  change  of  the  largest  shareholder  as  stipulated  in  the 
provisions of subparagraphs 1 through 3 in consideration of the nature and procedures 
of the transaction. 

(2) “A key investor of the backdoor listing target company specified in the Enforcement Rules” 
in [§33(1)2)] of the Regulation shall refer to a person who falls under any of the following 
subparagraphs: 

1.  The largest shareholder, etc. of a backdoor listing target company (in the case where 
the backdoor listing target company issued equity securities rather than stocks, it refers 
to the largest investor, etc. In such cases, the criteria for the largest shareholder, etc. 
under [§2(1)13] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis mutandis to the decision whether 
or not a person is the largest investor, etc.;   

2.  A person who holds 5/100 or more of the total number of issued stocks (referring to 
investment  shares  in  the  case  of  a  corporation  issuing  equity  securities  rather  than 
stocks) of the backdoor listing target company. 

(3) In the case of determining a change of the largest shareholder pursuant to paragraph (1), the 
stocks falling under each of the following subparagraphs shall be included in the calculation of 
the number of stocks: 

1.  Stocks  to  be  received  pursuant  to  the  transactions  falling  under  any  of  the 

subparagraphs of [§33(1)] of the Regulation; and 

2.  Stocks to be increased subsequent to the exercise of rights of equity-related bonds that 
are not exercised as of the date specified in each of the following items. In such cases, 
it  shall  be  based  on  the  conversion  price,  etc.  on  the  date  specified  in  each  of  the 
following items: 

(a)  Mergers and all-inclusive share swaps pursuant to paragraph (1)1: The submission 

date of the report on material facts; 

(b) Significant  business  transfers  and  acquisitions  of  material  assets  pursuant  to 
paragraph (1)2: The date on which a decision on whether the largest shareholder 
has been changed in accordance with each item of paragraph (1)2 is made;   

(c)  Investment in kind pursuant to paragraph (1)3: The issuance date of shares issued 

by way of third-party allotment; and 

(d) Transactions  pursuant  to  paragraph  (1)4:  The  date  separately  specified  by  the 

Exchange. 

3.  Stocks and equity-related bonds (based on the number of stocks to be increased as a 
result of exercise of rights) that are subject to delivery claim according to the provisions 
of  relevant  laws,  trading,  or  other  contracts  as  of  the  date  specified  in  each  item  of 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
subparagraph 2. 

§31. Effect of Listing, etc. 

(1) “Cases where there is an effect of listing the equity securities of a backdoor listing target 
company” in the part other than each subparagraph of [§33(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to 
any of the following subparagraphs:
