1.  Mergers under [§33(1)1(a)] of the Regulation: Case where the common-stock-listed 

corporation survives after the merger; 

2.  All-inclusive  share  swaps  under  [§33(1)1(b)]  of  the  Regulation:  Case  where  the 
common-stock-listed  corporation  owns  the  total  number  of  stocks  issued  by  the 
backdoor listing target company as a result of the all-inclusive share swap;   

3.  Significant  business  takeover  under  [§33(1)1(c)]  of  the  Regulation:  Case  where  the 
assets or sales of the business segment to be taken over are at least 30/100 s of the total 
assets or sales of the backdoor listing target company as of the end of the latest business 
year; 

4.  Acquisitions of material assets under [§33(1)2(a)] of the Regulation:    Case where, as 
a result of the acquisition of material asset, the common-stock-listed corporation owns 
50/100 or more of the total number of stocks issued (in the case of a corporation that 
issues equity securities other than stocks, it refers to investment shares; hereinafter the 
same shall apply in this Article) by the backdoor listing target company, or owns more 
than 30/100 thereof with the highest share ownership ratio;   

5.  Investment in kind under [§33(1)2(b)] of the Regulation: Case where, as a result of the 
investment in kind, the common-stock-listed corporation owns 50/100 or more of the 
total number of stocks issued by the backdoor listing target company, or owns more 
than 30/100 thereof with    the highest share ownership ratio; 

(2)  “The  amount  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§33(1)2(b)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the case of not less than 10/100 of the total assets of the common-
stock-listed corporation as of the end of the latest business year (referring to the end of the 
business year immediately preceding the latest business year in case where the report under 
[§6(1)2(e)(i)] of the Disclosure Regulation has not been filed yet). 

(3) “Transactions specified in the Enforcement Rules” under [§33(1)3] of the Regulation shall 
refer to any of the following transactions:   

1.  Case where the backdoor listing target company merges with the common-stock-listed 
corporation after spin-off, and there is a change in management rights of the common-
stock-listed corporation pursuant to [§30(1)1]; and 

2.  Other cases where the Exchange deems that a review for backdoor listing is necessary 

in terms of public interests and investor protection. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4) The backdoor listing under paragraph (3) shall be applied in accordance with each of the 
following subparagraphs: 

1.  Backdoor  listing  under  paragraph  (3)1:  The  review  methods  and  procedures  for 
backdoor listing as a result of a merger under [§33(1)1] or [§33(2)] of the Regulation 
shall apply  mutatis mutandis, and the review  requirements for backdoor listing  as a 
result of a business transfer under [§33(1)1(c)] of the Regulation shall apply mutatis 
mutandis; and   

2.  Backdoor  listing  under  paragraph  (3)2:  The  review  methods,  requirements,  and 

procedures separately specified by the Exchange shall be followed. 

(5) The review requirements under paragraph (4)1 shall apply based on the financial statements 
of the latest business year and the audit report of the backdoor listing target company. In such 
cases,  the  provisions  of  [§33(2)]  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis  with  regards  to  the  financial 
statements.   

(6) Matters concerning the financial details of the common-stock-listed corporation pursuant 
to [§33(2)] of the Regulation shall apply based on the financial statements of the latest business 
year for which the audit opinion is “unqualified” or “qualified” (limited to “qualified opinion” 
due to uncertainties over the ability to continue as a going concern; hereinafter the same shall 
apply in this paragraph). Provided that, in cases where the audit opinion for the latest business 
year is  not  “unqualified” or  “qualified”, it shall  be based on the financial  statements of the 
business year closest to the latest business year for which the audit opinion is “unqualified” or 
“qualified”. 

§32. Submission of Documents for Backdoor Listing Review   

(1) The common-stock-listed corporation shall, unless there is an unavoidable reason, consult 
with  the  Exchange  in  advance  concerning  whether  the  relevant  trades  fall  under  backdoor 
listing and the review requirements and procedures for backdoor listing before the submission 
date of the report on material facts about the transactions under each subparagraph of [§33(1)] 
and [§33(2)] of the Regulation (in the case of an investment in kind under [§33(1)2(b)] of the 
Regulation, it refers to the date on which the report is made pursuant to [§6] of the Disclosure 
Regulation regarding the issuance of the relevant shares),. 

(2)  Pursuant  to  [§34(1)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  case  of  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraph, the confirmation statement on backdoor listing and supplementary documents 
specified in [Annex 15] through [Annex 21] shall be submitted by the date specified in each of 
the following subparagraphs: (Amended on December 28, 2023) 

1.  Case where the common-stock-listed corporation merges with an unlisted corporation 
(including a corporation that issues equity securities other than stocks; hereinafter the 
same shall apply in this paragraph) or a KONEX-listed corporation pursuant to Article 
522 of the Commercial Act: The submission date of the report on material facts of the 
merger; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Case  where  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  intends  to  make  an  unlisted 
corporation or a KONEX-listed corporation its wholly owned subsidiary through all-
inclusive  share  swaps  pursuant  to Article  360-2(2)  of  the  Commercial Act  with  the 
unlisted  corporation  or  the  KONEX-listed  corporation:  The  submission  date  of  the 
report on material facts of the all-inclusive share swaps; 

3.  Case where the common-stock-listed corporation makes a significant business takeover, 
which requires a submission of the report on material facts pursuant to Article 161(1)7 
of  the  Act,  from  an  unlisted  corporation  or  a  KONEX-listed  corporation:  The 
submission date of the report on material facts of the significant business transfer; 

4.  Case  where  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  acquires  material  assets,  which 
requires a submission of a report on material facts pursuant to Article 161(1)17 of the 
Act, from major shareholders of an unlisted corporation or a KOEX-listed corporation 
(limited  to  cases  where  the  assets  to  be  acquired  are  equity  securities  issued  by  the 
unlisted  corporation  or  the  KONEX-listed  corporation): The  submission  date  of  the 
report on material facts regarding    the acquisition of material assets; 

5.  Case where the common-stock-listed corporation issues stocks, etc. by way of third-
party allotment within six (6) months from the submission date of the report on material 
facts under subparagraphs 3 or 4, or there is a stock transfer: The date on which the 
resolution or decision is made concerning the issuance of the stocks, etc., or the date 
of  reporting  on  the  stock  transfer.  Provided  that,  the  cases  subject  to  the  backdoor 
listing review due to the submission of the report on material facts under subparagraphs 
3 or 4 shall be excluded; 

6.  Case where the common-stock-listed corporation issues stocks by way of third-party 
allotment,  and  the  payment  for  the  stocks  is  made  through  the  investment  in  kind 
pursuant to Article 422 of the Commercial Act (limited to the cases where the property, 
which is the object of the investment in kind, is equity securities issued by an unlisted 
corporation or a KONEX-listed corporation, and the amount of the investment in kind 
is  at  least  the  amount  stipulated  in  [§31(2)]):  The  date  on  which  the  resolution  or 
decision is made concerning the issuance of the stocks. In such cases, in cases where 
there is a correction report on the report pursuant to [§6] of the Disclosure Regulation 
regarding the issuance of the concerned stocks due to a change in the value of equity 
securities, which is the object of the investment in kind, the confirmation statement and 
supplementary  documents  on  backdoor  listing  shall  be  submitted  again,  but  such 
submission  may  be  omitted  if  the  details  of  the  statement  and  the  documents  are 
identical to those already submitted; and 

7.  Other cases similar to the trades stipulated in subparagraphs 1 through 6 and recognized 
as necessary by the Exchange for the public interests and investor protection: The date 
specified by the Exchange. 

(3) The Exchange shall determine whether the trades under each subparagraph of paragraph (2) 
fall  under  backdoor  listing  and  notify  such  result  to  the  common-stock-listed  corporation 
without delay. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(4) The common-stock-listed corporation, which has been notified that it falls under backdoor 
listing pursuant to paragraph (3), shall submit without delay the review documents on backdoor 
listing  stipulated  in  [Annex  3]  and  the  backdoor  listing  report  separately  specified  by  the 
Exchange. 

(5) The common-stock-listed corporation, which has been notified that it falls under backdoor 
listing pursuant to the former part of [§34(2)] of the Regulation, shall submit, in cases when 
the  Exchange  requests  it,  the  financial  statements  and  the  documents  containing  other 
information  about  financial  data  about  the  corporate  merger  pursuant  to  [§12-8-6]  of  the 
Guideline  for  Preparation  of  Corporate  Disclosure  Forms  established  by  the  Financial 
Supervisory Service within the two (2) weeks from the date on which the documents pursuant 
to  paragraph  (4)  are  submitted.  In  such  cases,  the  financial  information  to  be  additionally 
submitted shall include all of the following matters: 

1.  The estimated financial position statement as of the date of business combination such 

as the merger date ; 

2.  The  estimated  financial  date  for  the  business  year  in  which    the  date  of  business 

combination such as the merger date falls and the following business year ; and 

3.  The confirmation statement regarding the statement and the data in subparagraphs 1 
and 2 issued by the accounting firm under subparagraph 7(a) of Article 2 of the External 
Audit Act. 

(6) In cases where a change occurs in the confirmation statement on backdoor listing and the 
supplementary documents submitted pursuant to paragraph (2) before the merger, all-inclusive 
share swaps, significant business transfer, acquisitions of material assets or investment in kind 
is completed, the common-stock-listed corporation shall immediately notify the Exchange of 
such change. 

(7) Pursuant to [§34(4)] of the Regulation, in cases where the backdoor listing target company 
meets  the  requirements  under  [§33(3)2],  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  result  of  the  review 
within thirty (30) days (based on business days) from the date on which the review documents 
are received. Provided that, this provision shall not apply if backdoor listing target company is 
a  foreign  holding  company  located  in  Korea  or  a  foreign  company  that  is  not  listed  on  an 
eligible overseas securities market. 

(8) The  listing  specification  under  [§34(5)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  mean  attached  [Annex: 
Form No. 41]. 

§33. Application Method of Requirements for Backdoor Listing Review 

(1) In cases where the latest business year of a backdoor listing target company is less than six 
(6) months, the requirements for backdoor listing in [§35(1) and §35(2)] of the Regulation shall 
also apply to the business year immediately preceding the latest business year. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2)  “The  financial  statements  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  former  part  of 
[§35(2)3]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  selling  corporation’s  financial  statements 
annotated  with  the  asset  amount,  liability  amount,  sales  amount  and  income  from  ongoing 
business before tax of the business sector acquired by the common-stock-listed corporation. 
Provided that, in cases where the auditor’s confirmation letter (referring to the auditor of the 
relevant financial statement) about the relevant asset amount, liability amount, sales amount 
and  income  from  ongoing  business  before  tax  is  submitted,  it  shall  be  deemed  that  the 
annotation on the relevant matters is provided. 

(3)  In  accordance  with  [§35(3)]  of  the  Regulation,  in  the  case  of  falling  under  any  of  the 
following  subparagraphs,  the  qualitative  review  requirements  under  [§29(1)1]  of  the 
Regulation shall be deemed to be satisfied. Provided that, this provision shall not apply where 
the Exchange deems an exception is necessary such as a significant slowdown in business: 

1.  The common-stock-listed corporation shall meet all of the following requirements, and 
the backdoor listing target company shall not engage in the businesses that are deemed 
to  undermine  the  balanced  development  of  the  national  economy  and  the  efficient 
fundraising function    of the capital market or to run counter to good morals and other 
social orders: 

(a)  As of the submission date of report on material facts (in the case of backdoor listing 
as a result of investment in kind under [§33(1)2(b)] of the Regulation, it refers to 
the date of reporting on the stock issuance under [§6] of the Disclosure Regulation; 
hereinafter the same shall apply in this paragraph),  three (3) years have  elapsed 
since its listing (excluding listing change and supplementary listing); 

(b) There shall be no record of having been designated as an administrative issue, an 
investment attention issue, or an unfaithful disclosure corporation within the past 
two (2) year from the submission date of report on material facts; 

(c)  There shall be no capital impairment as of the end of the latest business year (in 
cases where the semi-annual report has been finalized as of the submission date of 
the review documents on backdoor listing, it shall be the end of the semi-annual 
period). In such cases, during the business year in which the submission date of 
report on material facts falls, the amount to be transferred to equity as a result of 
paid-in  capital  increases,  exercises  of  subscription  rights,  conversion  rights  or 
stock options and revaluations of assets shall be reflected;   

(d) The sales amount shall  be at least  KRW 20 billion and there shall be operating 

profits in the latest business year; and 

(e)  As of the submission date of report on material facts, there shall be no record of 
having  been  subject  to  the  listing  maintenance  review  pursuant  to  each 
subparagraph  of  [§56(1)]  of  the  Regulation  during  the  past  two  (2)  years. 
(Amended on July 9, 2025) 

2.  The backdoor listing target company shall meet all of the following requirements, and 
the common-stock-listed corporation shall have no record of having been subject to the 
listing maintenance review pursuant to each subparagraph of [§56(1)] of the Regulation 
in the past two (2) years from the submission date of report on material facts: (Amended 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  The backdoor listing target company shall have been registered in the KRX M&A 
intermediary  network  (referring  to  the  intermediary  network  established  by  the 
Exchange to carry out intermediary services for mergers and acquisitions of small 
and medium-sized enterprises and venture companies; hereinafter the same shall 
apply)  within  one  (1)  year  before  the  submission  date  of  the  documents  for 
backdoor listing review; 

(b) At least one (1) month shall have elapsed since the backdoor listing target company 
was registered in the KRX M&A intermediary network from the submission date 
of the review documents on backdoor listing; 

(c)  The sales amount  shall  be at least  KRW 10 billion and there shall be operating 

profits in the latest business year;   

(d) There shall be a recommendation from the M&A professional institution (referring 
to  the  institution  selected  by  the  Exchange  to  register  M&A  information  in  the 
KRX M&A intermediary network; hereinafter the same), which has registered the 
backdoor listing target company in the KRX M&A intermediary network; and 

(e)  The backdoor listing target company shall not  engage in the businesses that are 
deemed to undermine the balanced development of the national economy and the 
efficient fundraising function of the capital market or to run counter to good morals 
and other social orders. 

§34. Mandatory Holding Due to Backdoor Listing, etc. 

(1) “A person specified in the Enforcement Rules” under [§36(1)1] of the Regulation shall refer 
to a person falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  The  largest  shareholder,  etc.  of  the  backdoor  listing  target  company  pursuant  to 
[§30(2)1]. In such cases, officers of the backdoor listing target company shall include 
persons falling under each subparagraph of Article 401-2(1) of the Commercial Act; 
and 

2.  A person who becomes the largest shareholder of the common-stock-listed corporation 
pursuant to each subparagraph of [§30(1)] among the key investors of the backdoor 
listing target company. 

(2)  “The  cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§36(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(3)]. 

(3)  “The  cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§37(1)3]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(4)]. 

(4)  “The  cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§37(1)4]  of  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(5)]. In such 
cases,  “the  date  of  application  for  preliminary  listing  review”  shall  be  construed  as  “the 
submission date of the report on material facts.” 

(5) “The date stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” under [§36(2)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the date noted in any of the following dates or in cases where the closing date of backdoor 
listing review (referring to the date on which the result of backdoor listing review is notified) 
arrives  later  than  the  date  specified  in  each  of  the  following  subparagraphs,  it  shall  be  the 
closing date of backdoor listing review: (Amended on March 17, 2022) 

1.  In  the  case  of  backdoor  listing  as  a  result  of  the  significant  business  transfer  under 
[§33(1)1(c)]  of  the  Regulation  or  backdoor  listing  as  a  result  of  the  acquisition  of 
material assets under [§33(1)2(a)] of the Regulation, it shall be the date according to 
each of the followings: 

(a) 
Case where within one (1) year before the submission date of the report on 
material facts, the common-stock-listed corporation issues stocks, etc. to a key investor 
of  the  backdoor  listing  target  company  by  way  of  third-party  allotment,  or  the  key 
investor of the backdoor listing target company participates in the stock transfer during 
the same period: The completion date of the business transfer or the acquisitions of 
material assets (referring to the date when the implementation of the business transfer 
or the asset acquisition agreement is completed); and 

(b) 
Case where within six (6) months after the submission date of the report on 
material facts, the common-stock-listed corporation issues stocks, etc. to a key investor 
of the backdoor listing target company participates in the stock transfer during the same 
period: The date of supplementary listing (referring to the issuing date in case of no 
supplementary listing; hereinafter the same shall apply in this paragraph) or the date of 
report on a change in the largest shareholder. 

2.  In the case of backdoor listing as a result of the investment in-kind under [§33(1)2(b)] 
of  the  Regulation,  it  shall  be  the  date  of  supplementary  listing  subsequent  to  the 
investment in-kind. 

(6) Deleted on March 17, 2022. 

(6) “The date specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§37(1)3] of the Regulation shall refer to 
the dates under each subparagraph of paragraphs (5). (Amended on March 17, 2022) 

§35. Publication of Backdoor Listing 

Pursuant to [§38] of the Regulation, the Exchange may mark “backdoor listing” on the market 
price table of securities information terminals, etc. from the date noted in any of the following 
subparagraphs to the statutory deadline for the submission of annual report for the business 
year after the business year in which the concerned date falls: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1.  Case  of  backdoor  listing  subsequent  to  the  mergers  pursuant  to  [§33(1)1(a)]  and 
[§33(2)] of the Regulation, the all-inclusive share swaps pursuant to [§33(1)1(b)] of 
the  Regulation  or  the  backdoor  listing  through  investment  in  kind  pursuant  to 
[§33(1)2(b)]  of  the  Regulation:  The  date  of  supplementary  listing  (in  case  of  no 
supplementary  listing,  it  refers  to  the  day  after  the  issuing  date  of  the  securities: 
hereinafter the same shall apply in this Article). Provided that, in the case of exchanging 
with the old stocks of the common-stock-listed corporation subject to an all-inclusive 
share swap, it shall be the date of stock swap; and 

2.  Case  of  backdoor  listing  due  to  the  significant  business  takeover  pursuant  to 
[§33(1)1(c)] of the Regulation or the acquisition of material assets under [§33(1)2(a)] 
of the Regulation: The date under any of the following items: 

(a) 
Case where the supplementary listing or the stock transfer is completed after 
the completion of the business takeover or the acquisition of assets (referring to the 
date  when  the  implementation  of  the  business  transfer  or  the  asset  acquisition 
agreement is completed; hereinafter the same shall apply in this item), it shall be the 
date of supplementary listing or the day after the date of report on the stock transfer; 
or 

(b) 
Case  where  the  implementation  due  to  the  business  takeover  or  the  asset 
acquisition is completed after the date of supplementary listing or the day after the date 
of  report  on  the  stock  transfer,  it  shall  be  the  day  after  the  completion  date  of  the 
business takeover or the asset acquisition. 

§36. Application Documents for Re-Preliminary Listing Review 

The application for re-preliminary listing review and the supplementary documents pursuant 
to the latter part of [§40(1)] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 1]. 

§37. Mandatory Holding Due to Re-listing 

(1)  “The  cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§41(2)1]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any subparagraph of [§23(3)]. 

(2)  “The  cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§41(2)2]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any subparagraph of [§23(4)]. 

§38. Application Documents for Re-listing   

The application for re-listing and the supplementary documents in the former part of [§42(1)] 
of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 4]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§39. Application Documents for Listing Change and Supplementary Listing   

(1) The applications for listing change or supplementary listing and the documents attached 
thereto pursuant to [§44(1)] of the Regulation and the submission period shall be stipulated in 
[Annex 5]. 

(2) “The value stipulated in  the Enforcement Rules” under  [§44(3)] of the Regulation  shall 
refer to the value under [§26(3)]. (Amended on April 29, 2022) 

§40. Application Documents for Shelf-listing 

(1) The application for shelf-listing pursuant  to the latter part of [§45(1)] of the Regulation 
shall mean attached [Annex 22]. 

(2) A  notice  on  issuance  of  new  stocks  pursuant  to  [§45(2)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  mean 
attached [Annex: Form No. 23], and the supplementary documents are as follows: 

1.  Certificate of registration of issuance;   

2.  A certified copy of corporate register. In such cases, it may be submitted within seven 

(7) days after the registration of change 

3.  A copy of request to issue new stocks or, a copy of conversion request, or a document 

proving the exercise of stock options; and   

4.  Other documents recognized as necessary by the Exchange. 

§41. Deferment of Listing Change and Supplementary Listing     

(1)  “The  cases  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§46(1)1]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Case where there is a court decision or ruling pending on the validity of issuance of 
new stocks, etc., and the Exchange deems that there is little or no possibility of    the 
validity of issuance of such new stocks being refuted; and 

2.  Case  where  the  Exchange  acknowledges  that  the  listing  change  or  supplementary 
listing  is  unlikely  to  undermine  the  safety  of  transactions  given  the  causes  for  the 
lawsuit filed in relation to the validity of issuance of new stocks. 

(2) “The supplementary documents stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the main sentence 
of  [§46(1)4]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  details  of  use  of  funds  and  the  documents 
evidencing such details submitted in the case of paid-in capital increase by way of third-party 
allotment  among  the  application  documents  for  listing  change  and  supplementary  listing 
pursuant to [Annex 5]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3)  “The  cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to  [§46(1)4]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the case where the company category in which the applicant for the 
listing change or supplementary listing is included is the premier company category. 

(4) In cases where an applicant for listing change or supplementary listing files an objection 
pursuant to [§46(3)] of the Regulation, the applicant shall submit the objection form in [Annex” 
Form No. 24] along with the documents noted in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Documents related to the lawsuit on the validity of new stock issuance; 

2.  Opinion  letters  of  experts  in  the  concerned  fields,  such  as  lawyers,  certified  public 

accounts and appraisers; and 

3.  Other  documents  that  the  Exchange  deems  necessary  in  relation  to  the  filing  of 

objection. 

(5) Upon receiving an objection noted in paragraph (4), unless there is an inevitable reason, the 
Exchange shall hold  a  meeting of  Listing  Committee for the deliberation and  resolution  on 
whether or not to postpone the listing change or supplementary listing, within fifteen (15) days 
(based on business days) from the date of receiving the objection. In such cases, the Exchange 
may provide the representative of the applicant for the listing change or supplementary listing 
with an opportunity to present his/her opinion. 

(6) The Exchange shall notify in writing the decision on whether or not to postpone the listing 
change or supplementary listing within three (3) days (based on business days) from the date 
of deliberation and resolution of the Listing Committee under paragraph (5). 

(7) An applicant for the listing change and supplementary listing may not file another official 
objection to the decision on whether or not to postpone the listing change and supplementary 
listing made pursuant to paragraph (5). 

Section 2. Administration of Listed Issues 

§42. Prerequisites for Assigning Company Category, etc.     

(1) “Companies that meet the requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” in [§47(2)1] 
of the Regulation shall refer to companies that meet each of the following requirements: 

1.  Business size: Companies shall meet any of the following items as of the base date of 
periodic  review  (referring  to  the  statutory  submission  deadline  for  annual  report  of 
companies whose business year ends in December: hereinafter the same shall apply in 
this Article): 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(a)  The equity capital in the financial statement of the latest business year shall be at 

least KRW 70 billion; and 

(b) The average market capitalization for the past six (6) months shall be at least KRW 

100 billion. 

2.  Financial requirements: As of the base date of periodic review, companies shall meet 

all of the following requirements: 

(a)  There shall be no capital impairment based on the financial statements of the latest 

business year; 

(b) The average return on equity for the past three (3) business years shall be at least 
5/100, or the average net income for the past three (3) business years shall be KRW 
3 billion or more; and 

(c)  The  average  sales  amount  for  the  past  three  (3)  years  shall  be  at  least  KRW  50 

billion. 

3.  Soundness of corporate management: As of the base date of periodic review, companies 

shall meet all of the following requirements: 

(a)  For the past two (2) years, there shall be no record of having been subject to the 

listing maintenance review pursuant to [§57(1)] of the Regulation; 

(b) Total  demerit  points  imposed  subsequent  to  the  designation  as  an  unfaithful 
disclosure corporation pursuant to [§32] of the Disclosure Regulation for the past 
two (2) years shall be four (4) points or less; and 

(c)  For the past two (2) years, the number of changes in the largest shareholder noted 

in [§6(1)3(a)(i)] of the Disclosure Regulation shall be two (2) or less. 

(2)  “Corporations  that  meet  the  requirements  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  under 
[§47(2)3(a)] of the Regulation shall refer to companies that meet all of the requirements noted 
in each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Business size: Companies shall meet any of the following items as of the base date of 

periodic review: 

(a)  The equity capital in the financial statement of the latest business year shall be at 

least KRW 30 billion; and 

(b) The average market capitalization for the past six (6) months shall be at least KRW 

50 billion 

2.  Financial requirements: As of the base date of periodic review, companies shall meet 

all of the following requirements: 

(a)  There shall be no capital impairment based on the financial statements of the latest 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
business year; and 

(b) There shall have been net income for at least two (2) of the last three (3) business 

years. 

3.  Growth potential: As of the base date of periodic review, the average growth rate of 
sales amount compared to the respective immediately preceding year for each of the 
two (2) latest business years shall be at least 20/100; 

(3) “Corporations recognized for their technological prowess by the methods specified in the 
Enforcement  Rules” in  [§47(2)3(b)] of the Regulation  shall refer to  venture companies that 
meet any of the following requirements: (Amended on June 14, 2024) 

1.  The green certificate under Article 60 of the Framework Act on Carbon Neutrality and 
Green Growth  for Coping with  Climate Crisis  (hereinafter  referred to  as  “the green 
certificate”) shall be obtained; 

2.  All of the following items shall be met: 

(a)  Cases  falling  under  [§2(1)38(a)  or  §2(1)38(b)]  of  the  Regulation  (hereinafter 

referred to as the “venture certificate”); and 

(b) Cases falling under [§2(1)38(c)] of the Regulation (hereinafter referred to as the 

“inno-biz certificate”). 

3.  As of the base date of periodic review, the ratio of R&D expense to sales in the financial 

statements of the latest business year is 5/100 or higher. 

(4) “Corporations stipulated in the Enforcement Rules in consideration of market share, etc.” 
in [§47(2)3(c)] of the Regulation shall refer to corporations that the Exchange selects by taking 
into  consideration  such  factors  as  the  market  share,  profitability,  technology  prowess,  and 
growth potential (hereinafter referred to as the “rising star”). 

(5)  “Initially  listed  or  re-listed  corporations  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  under 
[§47(2)4(b)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  corporations  for  which  the  first  base  date  of 
periodic review (the next base date of periodic review if the period from the initial listing date 
or re-listing date to the first base date of periodic review is less than six (6) months) has not yet 
arrived after the initial listing or re-listing. Provide that, the technology growth companies, the 
companies with unrealized profits, and the prompt-transfer companies pursuant to [§31(1)] of 
the Regulation shall be excluded. 

§43. Review and Change of Company Category     

(1) The Exchange shall examine the requirements noted in [§42(1), §42(2) and §42(3)3] based 
on the audit reports for the latest business year or the recent three (3) business years, submitted 
as of the base date of periodic review (referring to the statutory submission deadline for annual 
report of companies whose business year ends in December: hereinafter the same shall apply 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
in this Article). Provided that, in cases where the audit reports could not be submitted by the 
statutory deadline due to    the occurrence of any event provided for in any subparagraph of 
[§52(1)], the base date of periodic review and the dates of assignment and change of company 
category may be separately determined by the Exchange. 

(2) “The cause for the change in the company category specified in the Enforcement Rules” in 
[§47(4)] of the Regulation shall refer to the cases noted in any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Acquisition, cancellation or expiration of the green certificate, venture certificate or 

inno-biz certificate;   

2.  Selection of or release from the rising star; 

3.  Case of being released from a designation as an administrative issue or an investment 

attention issue; and   

4.  Other cases where the Exchange deems necessary. 

(3)  In  the  event  of  changing  the  company  category  due  to  causes  provided  for  in  each 
subparagraph of paragraph (2), the Exchange shall change and assign the company category of 
a corporation falling under [§42(3)1 and §42(3)2] and [§42(4)] to the respective corresponding 
company category and change and assign the company category of a corporation falling under 
other cases to the standard company category. 

(4)  In  the  event  of  changing  and  assigning  the  company  category  under  paragraph  (2),  the 
change and designation of company category for corporations falling under causes noted in 
paragraph (2)2 and paragraph (2)3 shall be made on the day when the  concerned cause for 
change is applied, and the change and assignment of company category for corporations falling 
under  other  causes  shall  be  made  on  the  trading  day  following  the  day  of  confirming  the 
concerned cause. 

(5)  In  the  event  where  a  company  is  found  to  fall  under  two  (2)  or  more  of  the  company 
categories as a result of review conducted pursuant to [§47(3) and §47(4)] of the Regulation,, 
it shall be re-assigned in the order of the premier company category, venture company category, 
and standard company category. 

(6) Notwithstanding [§42(5)] of the Regulation, in cases where an initially listed corporation 
or a re-listed corporation falls under [§42(3)1 and §42(3)2] or [§42(4)] as of the listing date or 
before the concerned base date of periodic review from the listing date, such company shall be 
assigned or re-assigned to the concerned company category. 

(7) In the case of a company categorized into the technology growth company under [§47(2)2] 
of the Regulation, the change of company category may be permitted from the base date of 
periodic review that arrives three (3) years after the date of the first assignment of company 
category. Provided that, the prompt-transfer companies under [§31(1)] of the Regulation and 
the  prompt  listing-after-merger  companies  in  [§75(4)1]  of  the  Regulation  may  change  their 
company category from the base date of periodic review that arrives one (1) year after the date 
of the first assignment of company category. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(8) The first change of the company category for technology growth companies and companies 
with unrealized profits shall be limited to the change to the premier company category only, 
and  once  changed  to  the  premier  company  category,  it  shall  be  prohibited  from  being  re-
categorized to the technology growth company category. 

(9) Any other matters necessary for the assignment and the change of company category other 
than those set forth in the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (8) shall be separately specified 
by the Exchange. 

§44. Mandatory Holding Due to Mergers and All-inclusive Stock Swaps     

“The cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§48(1)3] of the Regulation 
shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(5)]. In such cases, “the 
date of application for preliminary listing review” shall be construed as “the submission date 
of the report on material facts.”   

§45. Mandatory Holding Due to Acquisitions of Assets, Etc.       

In cases where a change in the largest shareholder takes place pursuant to any of the following 
subparagraphs  in  relation  to  the  acquisitions  of  material  assets  or  investment  in  kind  under 
[§49(4)] of the Regulation, the largest shareholder, etc. of an unlisted corporation or a KONEX-
listed corporation who acquired the stocks, etc. issued by way of third-party allotment    by a 
common-stock-listed corporation shall mandatorily hold the allocated stocks, etc. for six (6) 
months from the date of supplementary listing: 

1.  Case  where  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  acquires  material  assets  from  the 
unlisted corporation or the KONEX-listed corporation and the largest shareholder, etc. 
of  the  unlisted  corporation  or  the  KONEX-listed  corporation  acquires  stocks,  etc. 
issued by way of third-party allotment by the common-stock-listed corporation within 
six (6) months from the submission date of the report on material facts of the concerned 
acquisition  of  the  material  assets:  Case  of  becoming  the  largest  shareholder  of  the 
common-stock-listed corporation by acquiring the relevant stocks, etc., or becoming 
the largest shareholder of the common-stock-listed corporation from the date of one (1) 
year before the submission date of report on material facts to the date before the issuing 
date of the stocks, etc. Provided that, it shall be limited to the cases where the acquired 
assets shall not be equity securities issued by the concerned unlisted corporation or the 
KONEX-listed corporation; or 

2.  Case where the payment for the stocks issued by the common-stock-listed corporation 
by  way  of  third-party  allotment  for  the  unlisted  corporation  or  the  KONEX-listed 
corporation is made through an implementation of an investment in kind pursuant to 
Article  422  of  the  Commercial Act,  and  the  largest  shareholder,  etc.  of  the  relevant 
unlisted corporation or the KONEX-listed corporation becomes the largest shareholder 
of the common-stock-listed corporation by acquiring stocks, etc. or becomes the largest 
shareholder  of  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  from  the  date  of  one  (1)  year 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
before the date of reporting on the issuance of the stocks under [§6] of the Disclosure 
Regulation to the date before the issuing date. Provided that, it shall be limited to the 
cases where the properties, which are the object of the investment in kind, shall not be 
equity securities issued by the unlisted corporation or the KONEX-listed corporation, 
and the value of the investment in kind shall be 10/100 or more of the total assets of 
the common-stock-listed corporation as of the end of the latest business year. 

§46. Mandatory Holding Due to Paid-in Capital Increase through Third-party 
Allotment       

“The cases resulted from the handling of unclaimed stocks stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” 
in [§50(1)1] of the Regulation shall refer to the case of allotting unclaimed stocks to a third-
party when there are any unclaimed stocks as a result of non-subscription of new stocks or a 
failure to deliver the subscription payment at the time of paid-in capital increase through rights 
offering or paid-in capital increase through a third-party allotment. 

§47. Mandatory Holding Due to Change of Largest Shareholder     

(1) “A change of the largest shareholder set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in the part other 
than each subparagraph of [§51(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the cases where the change 
of the largest shareholder is disclosed pursuant to [§6(1)3(a)(i)] of the Disclosure Regulation. 
Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  cases  where  the  largest  shareholder  is 
changed according to any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Gifts or inheritance; 

2.  Disposal of the stocks, etc. by the largest shareholder, etc. before the change; 

3.  Dissolution of the association that is the largest shareholder before the change; and 

4.  Other  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  that,  given  such  factors  as  the  patterns  of 
acquisition of the stocks, etc., the largest shareholder after the change has no intention 
of  becoming  the  largest  shareholder  of  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  or 
exercising the de facto control over the corporation. 

(2) “The persons set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in the part other than each subparagraph 
of  [§51(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  persons  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs: (Amended on December 28, 2023) 

1.  Case  where  the  largest  shareholder  after  the  change  is  a  corporation: A  corporation 
whose  sales  amounts  (it  shall  be  the  sales  amount  in  the  consolidated  financial 
statements  for  a  corporation  with  subsidiaries;  the  same  hereinafter  in  this 
subparagraph) for any of the first quarter, semi-annual period, third quarter, or annual 
period,  as  confirmed  by  the  documents  falling  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs (limited to the documents prepared or published within the recent one 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1)  year  based  on  the  date  of  disclosure  under  [§6(1)3(a)(i)]  of  the  Disclosure 
Regulation), are less than KRW 300 million: (Amended on November 24, 2025) 

(a)  Financial  statements  prepared  in  accordance  with  the  Korean  International 
Financial Reporting Standards under [§5(1)1] of the Act on External Audit. In such 
cases, it shall be limited to the cases where the audit or review opinion with respect 
to such financial statements is ‘unqualified’; 

(b) Financial statements submitted to the head of the tax office having authority over 
the  place  of  tax  payment  with  respect  to  the  payment  of  corporate  tax,  the  tax 
settlement invoice and the certificate of tax payment issued by tax authorities; 

(c)  The certificate of tax base of value-added tax and the certificate of tax payment 
issued by tax authorities with respect to the payment of value-added tax. Provided 
that, in case of value-added tax-free business operators, it shall be the certificate of 
income amount for value-added tax-free business operators; and 

(d) In the event where it is impossible to submit the documents provided for in items 
(a)  through  (c),  a  written  review  confirmation  verifying  the  sales  amount  of  the 
concerned corporation prepared by an accounting firm. 

2.  Case where the largest shareholder after the change is an organization or association: 
An  organization  or  association  that  does  not  fall  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs: 

(a)  The Korea Venture Fund in accordance with the Venture Company Act; 

(b) The  Small  or  Medium  Enterprise  Establishment Association  in  accordance  with   

the Support for Small and Medium Enterprise Establishment Act; 

(c)  The  New  Technology  Venture  Investment  Association  in  accordance  with  the 

Special Credit Finance Business Act; or 

(d) Any  other  organization  or  association  recognized  by  the  Exchange  that  it  is 
established  or  formed  under  the  permission  or  authorization  of  the  competent 
authorities or is registered with the competent authorities under the relevant statutes 
(except for the case of applying for registration to the head of the competent tax 
office). 

3.  Other foreign companies and organizations recognized by the Exchange as equivalent 

to subparagraphs 1 and 2. 

(3)  Notwithstanding  paragraph  (2),  a  person  who  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs  shall  not  be  deemed  to  fall  under  the  persons  specified  in  paragraph  (2): 
(Amended on September 27, 2022) 

1.  The State; 

2.  The Bank of Korea; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3.  Any person falling  under any of  subparagraphs  of Article  10(2) of the Enforcement 

Decree of the Act; 

4.  Any person falling under any of subparagraphs 1 through 4, 9 through 14 and 18 of 

Article 10(3) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act; 

5.  The private equity funds under Article 9(19) of the Act (including the private equity 
funds for institutional investors only for improving corporate structure under Article 
20 of the Industrial Development Act) and the special purpose company for investment 
in which the relevant private equity funds have invested pursuant to the Act (including 
the  special  purpose  company  for  investment  in  which  the  relevant  special  purpose 
company for investment has invested); and 

6.  Other person recognized by the Exchange as not falling under any of the subparagraphs 
of paragraph (2) for the purpose of enhancing management efficiency and improving 
corporate governance. 

(4) In cases where the largest shareholder of a common-stock-listed corporation changes to a 
corporation,  an  association  or  an  organization,  the  concerned  corporation  shall  submit  the 
documents noted in each of the following subparagraphs to the Exchange within three (3) days 
(based  on  business  days)  from  the  disclosure  date  on  which  the  change  of  the  largest 
shareholder is disclosed pursuant to [§6(1)3(a)(i)] of the Disclosure Regulation. Provided that, 
in cases where the Exchange deems that there is an unavoidable reason for not being able to 
submit the documents by the deadline, the deadline for submission may be extended: 

1.  A written confirmation under [Annex: Form No. 26] and accompanying documents on 
whether the largest shareholder after the change falls under any of the subparagraphs 
of paragraph (2); and 

2.  In  cases  where  the  largest  shareholder  after  the  change  falls  under  any  of  the 
subparagraphs of paragraph (2), the written affirmation on mandatory holding by the 
person  subject  to  mandatory  holding  and  a  document  certifying  mandatory  holding 
issued by the Korea Securities Depository. 

(5) Notwithstanding paragraph (4), in cases where the largest shareholder after the change is 
unable  to  submit  the  document  specified  in  items  (a)  through  (c)  of  paragraph  (2)1,  it  may 
submit an agreement concluded with an accounting firm for the examination and confirmation 
of  the  sales  amount  until  the  period  specified  in  the  part  other  than  each  subparagraph  of 
paragraph  (4).  In  such  cases,  the  relevant  common-stock-listed  corporation  shall  submit 
following documents within three (3) weeks from the date of the agreement set forth in the 
main sentence of this paragraph was submitted: 

1.  A written confirmation of sales amount under [Annex: Form No. 27]; and 

2.  Documents under subparagraphs 1 and 2 of paragraph (4). 

(6) “The date of submitting documents set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in the part other 
than  each  subparagraph  of  [§51(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  the  date  on  which  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
documents under paragraph (4) or the latter part of paragraph (5) are submitted. 

§48. Designation as Investment Attention Issues and Release Therefrom   

(1)  The  criteria  for  identification  of  corporate  insolvency  risks  under  [§52(1)1]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to the criteria set forth in [Annex 8] (hereinafter referred to as the “criteria 
for identification of corporate insolvency risks). 

(2) The criteria for identification of corporate insolvency risks shall apply in accordance with 
each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  It  shall  judge  based  on  the  financial  information  on  the  audit  report  of  the  latest 
business year and disclosures, etc. submitted by the statutory deadline of the annual 
report of a corporation which closes accounts in December. Provided that, in the case 
where it is impossible to submit the annual report by the statutory deadline due to a 
reason which falls any of the subparagraphs of [§52(1)], the Exchange may determine 
the  reference  date  to  judge  whether  the  corporation  falls  under  the  criteria  for 
identification of corporate insolvency risks and the timing of designation as and release 
from an investment attention issue. 

2.  It  shall  not  apply  to  a  common  stock-listed  corporation  where  it  is  confirmed  that 
reason  of  delisting  by  formality  review  of  [§54]  of  the  Regulation  (excluding 
distribution of share ownership not up to standards of [§54(1)5], restriction of transfer 
of stocks of [§54(1)8], and corporate governance not up to standards of [§54(1)11]), 
of  [§52(1)],  of  [§52(1)]  occurs,  or  else,  there  is  a  fact  that  falls  under  any  of  each 
subparagraph of [§56(1)]. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(3) The reason  of timely designation pursuant  to  [§52(1)2] of the Regulation shall apply  in 
accordance with each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Reasons of [§52(1)2(a),(d),(g) through (j)] of the Regulation: The timely designation 
shall  apply  based  on  the  review  or  audit  reports  that  are  reported  pursuant  to 
[§56(1)2(e)(i)] of the KOSDAQ Market Disclosure Regulation. In such cases, cases 
where  there  is  a  revised  report  to  the  concerned  report,  the  designation  as  or  the 
released from an investment attention issue shall be made on the next day of the day 
of the report based on the content of the revised report. 

2.  Reasons  of  [§52(1)2(g)  through  (i)]  of  the  Regulation:  In  a  case  where  a  common 
stock-listed corporation had made a spin-off to convert to a shareholdings company 
but  has  not  completed  the  conversion  to  a  shareholdings  company,  the  timely 
designation shall not apply to the business year to which the spin-off date belongs and 
the next business year. 

3.  Reason  of  [§52(1)2(g)]  of  the  Regulation:  The  timely  designation  shall  apply  in 

accordance with each of the following items: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
a.  Notwithstanding  the  Regulation  [§3(7)2],  in  cases  excluding  a  corporation 
specified in the Regulation [§3(7)1], the timely designation shall be based on the 
individual financial statements. 

b.  The timely designation shall not apply in cases where the business year is less than 
six  (6)  months  due  to  change  of  fiscal  year,  etc.  of  a  common  stock-listed 
corporation. 

(4)  “Technology  growth  company  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  proviso  to 
[§52(1)2(g)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  mean  a  technology  growth  company  whose  company 
category has not changed to the premier company category. 

(5) The timings of the designation as an investment attention issue and the release therefrom 
pursuant to [§52(3)] of the Regulation shall be specified in [Annex 9]. 

(6) In addition to the provisions of paragraphs (1) through (5), the designation as an investment 
attention  issue  and  the  release  from  such  designation  and  other  necessary  matters  shall 
separately be stipulated by the Exchange. 

(Wholly amended on December 9, 2022) 

§49. Methods of Applying Causes for Sales Not Up To Standards     

(1) “A technology growth companies specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the main sentence 
of [§53(1)1(a) and (b)] and the main sentence of [§53(1)2(b)] of the Regulation shall refer to a 
technology growth company whose company category has not changed to the premier company 
category. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(2) “The requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§53(1)1(b)] of the Regulation 
shall  refer  to  the  cases  where  a  confirmation  of  outstanding  corporation  in  R&D    in 
accordance with Annex Form No. 29 has been filed and recognized by the Exchange. In such 
cases,  such  confirmation  shall  be  submitted  within  sixty  (60)  days  from  the  end  of  each 
business year (limited to the cases of submitting it before the submission date of annual reports). 

(3) “Method  prescribed  by the Enforcement Rules”  in  [§53(1)1(c)]  of the Regulations  shall 
refer to the arithmetic average of the closing prices on trading days during the latest fiscal year, 
excluding days on which trading was suspended, multiplied by the number of listed shares. 
Provided  that,  if  a  closing  price  is  not  available,  subparagraph  of  [§51]  shall  apply  mutatis 
mutandis. [July 9, 2025] 

(4) The designation as an administrative issue and the release therefrom due to the sales amount 
not up to standards under [§53(1)1] of the Regulation and the loss from continuing operations 
before tax under [§53(1)2] of the Regulation shall apply based on the review or audit report 
reported pursuant to [§6(1)2(e)(i) or §6(1)2(e)(ii)] of the Disclosure Regulation. In such cases, 
in  cases  where  there  is  a  correction  report  for  the  concerned  report,  a  designation  as  an 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
administrative issue or a release from such designation shall take place on the day after the date 
of report based on the corrected and reported details. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(5)  In  cases  where  an  administrative  issue  is  designated  pursuant  to  [§53(1)1&2]  of  the 
Regulation and any event in each of the following subparagraphs occurs, the business years 
specified in the relevant subparagraphs shall be excluded from the business years in which the 
sales amount not up to standards and the loss from continuing operations before tax occurred: 
(Amended on December 9, 2022) 

1.  Case  where  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  split  off  to  convert  into  a  holding 
company,  but  the  conversion  into  a  holding  company  has  not  been  completed: The 
business year to which the date of split-off belongs and the following business year     

2.  Case where the business year of the common-stock-listed corporation is less than six 
(6) months due to a change in the accounting period: The concerned business year   

(6)  “Amount  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  main  sentence  of  [§53(1)2]  of  the 
Regulation shall mean the financial debt evaluation loss that is confirmed by [Annex Form No. 
42]  Confirmation  of  Evaluation  Loss  Relating  to  Refixing  Option  Financial  Instruments, 
confirmed by the auditor, in cases where such form is submitted. [ December 9, 2022] 

(7) In the case where the loss from continuing operations before corporate tax under [§53(1)2] 
of  the  Regulation  occurs,  notwithstanding  the  latter  part  of  the  part  other  than  each 
subparagraph of [§3(7)] of the Regulation, non-controlling interests are not excluded as well 
when calculating the equity capital based on consolidated financial statements. [December 9, 
2022] 

§50. Methods of Applying Capital Impairment, etc.     

(1) The reasons of capital impairment under [§53(1)3] and equity capital not up to standards 
under [§53(1)4] of the Regulation shall apply based on the review or audit report filed pursuant 
to [§6(1)2(e)(i) or §6(1)2(e)(ii)] of the Disclosure Regulation. In such cases, in cases where 
there is a correction report for the concerned report, a designation as an administrative issue or 
a release from such designation shall take place based on the corrected and reported details on 
the day after the date of report. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(2)  In  cases  where  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  split  off  to  convert  into  a  holding 
company, but the conversion into a holding company has not been completed, the provisions 
of [§53(1)3 and 4] of the Regulation shall not apply to the business year to which the date of 
split-off belongs and the following business year. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(3) [Deleted on December 9, 2022]   

(4) [Deleted on December 9, 2022]   

§51. Methods of Applying Market Capitalization not up to Standards   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
The market capitalization not up to standards under [§53(1)5] of the Regulation shall apply in 
accordance with the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Case without a closing price: It shall apply based on the base price of the relevant issue 

on the day; and   

2.  [Deleted on July 9, 2025] 

§52. Methods of Applying Non-submission of Regular Reports   

(1) In cases where a common-stock-listed corporation requests an extension of the deadline for 
submitting  its  annual  report,  semi-annual  report  or  quarterly  report  due  to  any  of  the 
following causes, the Exchange may postpone the designation as an administrative issue 
and release therefrom pursuant to [§53(1)6] of the Regulation for the period specified in 
the  concerned  subparagraph.  Provided  that,  in  the  case  where  the  relevant  cause  occurs 
three (3) months before the statutory deadline for the submission of the regular reports, this 
paragraph  shall  be  applicable  only  when  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  provides 
justification as to    the cause of non-submission and the Exchange deems it necessary: 

1.  Case where an auditor of the common-stock-listed corporation (including subsidiaries 
of the relevant corporation) is unable to carry out an audit due to any causes under the 
subparagraphs of Article 13(2) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on External Audit: 
A period not exceeding three (3) months from the statutory deadline for submission of 
the concerned report 

2.  Other unavoidable circumstances where it is not possible for the common-stock-listed 
corporation to submit the annual, semi-annual, or quarterly report within the statutory 
submission  deadline  and  the  case  is  acknowledged  through  approval,  etc.  by  the 
Financial Services Commission or the Securities and Futures Commission: The period 
from  the  statutory  submission  deadline  for  the  report  to  the  date  determined  by  the 
Financial  Services  Commission  or  the  Securities  and  Futures  Commission  through 
approval, etc.   

(2)  In  the  case  of  a  corporation  exempted  from  the  submission  of  annual  reports  under  the 
proviso to Article 159(1) of the Act, it shall not be designated as an administrative issue under 
[§53(1)6] of the Regulation. 

§53. Methods of Applying Corporate Governance not up to Standards   

(1) “The efforts set forth in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to the part other than each 
subparagraph of [§53(1)7] of the Regulation shall refer to each of the followings: 

1.  Introduction of an electronic voting system;   

2.  Solicitation to exercise voting rights by proxy;   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
3.  Request for exercises of voting rights to institutional investors, etc.; and 

4.  Other actions taken to establish the general meeting of shareholders.   

(2) In the case of applying the provisions of [§53(1)7] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall 
reflect the result of the general meeting of shareholders of the common-stock-listed corporation 
and examine the qualifications of outside director and the audit committee based on the written 
confirmations submitted by the concerned corporation. 

(3) In cases where a common-stock-listed corporation has failed to appoint its outside director 
or establish an audit committee due to unavoidable reasons such as death, the provisions of 
[§53(1)7] of the Regulation shall not apply. 

(4) In cases where the deadline for submitting regular reports is extended pursuant to [§52(1)] 
of the Regulation, a designation as an administrative issue under [§53(1)7] of the Regulation 
may be postponed for the period specified in each subparagraph of [§52(1)]. 

§54. Methods of Applying Trading Volume not up to Standards 

(1) The average monthly trading volume in a quarter under [§53(1)8] of the Regulation shall 
refer to the quantity calculated by dividing the total trading volume for the concerned quarter 
of  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  in  the  KOSDAQ  Market  (including  trading  at 
multilateral trading companies) by three (3). In such cases, if there is a trading suspension for 
the concerned issue during the quarter, the average monthly trading volume shall be calculated 
and  applied  by  conversion  based  on  the  trading  volume  and  the  trading  days  excluding  the 
period of trading suspension. (Amended on February 27, 2025) 

(2) In the cases of calculating  the average monthly  trading  volume in  a quarter pursuant  to 
paragraph (1), if the number of floating stocks has changed during the quarter, the quarterly 
turnover ratio shall be calculated by aggregating the daily turnover ratio that was calculated by 
dividing the daily trading volume by the number of floating stocks of the day, and the average 
monthly turnover ratio shall be calculated by dividing the quarterly turnover ratio by three (3). 

(3) In the case of falling under any of the following subparagraphs, the relevant company shall 
not be designated as an administrative issue due to the trading volume not up to standards under 
[§53(1)8] of the Regulation: 

1.  Case where the agreement for liquidity provision pursuant to [§12-3(1)] of the Business 

Regulation has been entered into as of the end of the quarter; or 

2.  Case where the number of trading days for the concerned issue during the quarter is 
less than 1/2 of the number of trading days in the KOSDAQ Market during the quarter. 

(4)  In  cases  where  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  that  has  submitted  a  tender  offer 
statement under Article 134(2) of the Act (limited to the case where such fact is stated in the 
tender  offer  statement)  for  the  purpose  of  being  delisted  falls  under  any  of  the  following 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
subparagraphs, the corporation shall not be designated as an administrative issue due to the 
trading volume not up to standards in [§53(1)8] of the Regulation during the period set forth in 
the respective subparagraph. Provided that, in cases where the number of shares owned by the 
minority shareholders at the end of the latest business year falls below 5/100 of the total number 
of common stocks even while the designation as an administrative issue is suspended pursuant 
to the main sentence, the corporation shall be designated as an administrative issue pursuant to 
[§53(1)8] of the Regulation: 

1.  Where  the  number  of  common  stocks  acquired  through  tender  offers  [including  the 
stocks acquired through tender offers for the purpose of being delisted within the three 
(3) year prior to the date of submission of the post tender offer report (referring to the 
post tender offer report under Article 143 of the Act; hereinafter the same shall apply) 
as confirmed by the post tender offer report] is equal to or more than 30/100 of the total 
number of common stocks: From the quarter in which    the submission date of the post 
tender offer report falls to the end of the three (3) consecutive business years following 
the  business  year  which  includes  the  relevant  quarter.  In  such  cases,  if  there  is  a 
correction for the post tender offer report and such correction is reported, the date of 
filing such correction report shall be deemed as the date of submission. 

2.  Where  the  number  of  treasury  stocks  that  the  common-stock-listed  corporation 
acquired (including the treasury stocks acquired through tender offers for the purpose 
of being delisted within the three (3) year prior to the date of submission of the post 
tender offer report as confirmed by the post tender offer report) is equal to or more than 
30/100  of  the  total  number  of  common  stocks:  From  the  quarter  in  which    the 
submission date of the post tender offer report falls to the end of the first quarter of the 
business year following the business year in which the number of shares held by the 
largest shareholder, etc. at the end of the concerned business year exceeds 95/100 of 
the total number of common stocks. In such cases, the latter part of subparagraph 1 
shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(5)  “Minority  shareholders  stipulated  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  former  part  of 
[§53(1)8(c)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  any  of  the  following  persons:  (Amended  on 
September 27, 2022)   

1.  A person who holds less than 1/100 of the total number of common stocks. Provided 

that the largest shareholders, etc. are excluded; 

2.  Professional investors who do not fall under the largest shareholder, etc.; 

3.  Funds under Article 3(3) of the Enforcement Decree of the Venture Business Act; 

4.  Venture capitals; 

5.  Foreign investment companies; 

6.  Investment companies (referring to an investment company under Article 9(18)2 of the 

Act); and 

7.  Any  other  foreign  companies  that  have  acquired  stocks  of  a  common-stock-listed 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
corporation for investment purposes and are equivalent to professional investors. 

§55. Methods of Applying Stock Distribution not up to Standards   

(1) With respect to the designation as an administrative issue due to a stock distribution not up 
to standards under [§53(1)9] of the Regulation, a common-stock-listed corporation shall submit 
the  summarized  register  of  shareholders  in  [Annex:  Form  No.  30]  and  documents  that  are 
recognized as necessary by the Exchange within five (5) days from the statutory deadline for 
submission of annual reports. In such cases, the common-stock-listed corporation may submit 
via the electronic disclosure system under [§54(1)] of the Disclosure Regulation. 

(2) In  cases  where  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  that  has  submitted  a  tender  offer 
statement under Article 134(2) of the Act (limited to the case where such fact is stated in 
the tender offer statement) for the purpose of being delisted falls under any of the following 
subparagraphs,  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  shall  not  be  designated  as  an 
administrative issue pursuant to the stock distribution not up to standards in [§53(1)9] of 
the Regulation during the period set forth in the respective subparagraph. Provided that, in 
cases where the number of stocks held by minority shareholders at the end of the latest 
business  year  is  less  than  5/100  of  the  total  number  of  common  stocks  even  while  the 
designation as an administrative issue is postponed under the main sentence, the common-
stock-listed corporation shall be designated as an administrative issue pursuant to [§53(1)9] 
of the Regulation:   

1.  Where  the  number  of  common  stocks  acquired  through  tender  offers  (including  the 
stocks acquired through tender offers for the purpose of being delisted within the three 
(3) years prior to the date of submission of the post tender offer report and confirmed 
by the post tender offer report) is equal to or more than 30/100 of the total number of 
common  stocks:  From  the  business  year  in  which    the  submission  date  of  the  post 
tender offer report falls (in cases where the post tender offer report is submitted within 
the statutory deadline for submission of annual reports for the latest business year, it 
shall be deemed that the post tender offer report has been submitted during the latest 
business  year;  hereinafter  the  same  shall  apply  in  this  paragraph),  to  the  end  of  the 
following two (2) consecutive business years. In such cases, if there is a correction for 
the  post  tender  offer  report  and  such  correction  is  reported,  the  date  of  filing  such 
correction report shall be deemed as the date of submission. 

2.  Where  the  number  of  treasury  stocks  that  the  common-stock-listed  corporation 
acquired (including the treasury stocks acquired through tender offers for the purpose 
of being delisted within the three (3) year prior to the date of submission of the post 
tender offer report and confirmed by the post tender offer report) is equal to or more 
than 30/100 of the total number of common stocks: From the business year in which 
the submission date of the post tender offer report falls to the end of the business year 
in which the number of shares held by the largest shareholder, etc. at the end of the 
concerned business year does not exceed 95/100 of the total number of common stocks. 
In such cases, the latter part of subparagraph 1 shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(3) “The minority shareholders specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the former part other 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
than each subparagraph in [§53(1)9] of the Regulation shall refer to persons falling under any 
subparagraph of [§54(5)]. 

§56. Methods of Applying Bankruptcy Filing 

“The cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§53(1)11] of the Regulation 
shall refer to any the following cases: 

1.  Case where a creditor has filed for bankruptcy and the Exchange deems that the need 
for a designation as an administrative issue is low as the case falls under any of the 
following items: 

(a)  Where the total credit amount subject to the bankruptcy filing within six (6) months 
from the date of the bankruptcy filing is less than 10/100 of the equity capital (5/100 
for a large-sized corporation under [§2(27)] of the Disclosure Regulation) and less 
than KRW two (2) billion; and 

(b) Where it is confirmed that the common-stock-listed corporation has deposited the 
total  credit  amount  subject  to  the  bankruptcy  filing  in  the  court  within  six  (6) 
months from the date of the bankruptcy filing. 

2.  Other cases where the Exchange deems that the risk of harming public interests and 
investor  protection  is  low  considering  the  abuse  of  rights  in  connection  with  the 
bankruptcy filing and the claim-obligation relationship.   

§57. Objection to Designations of Administrative Issues   

(1)  “The  causes  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  former  part  of  [§53(4)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to any of the following causes:   

1.  Corporate governance not up to standards pursuant to [§53(1)7] of the Regulation; 

2.  Stock distribution not up to standards pursuant to [§53(1)9] of the Regulation; 

3.  Application for commencement of rehabilitation procedures pursuant to [§53(1)10] of 

the Regulation; and 

4.  Application for bankruptcy pursuant to [§53(1)11] of the Regulation. 

(2) Upon receiving an official objection noted in [§53(4)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall 
finalize the decision on the objection through the deliberation and resolution of the Corporate 
Review Committee within ten (10) days (based on business days) from the date of receiving 
the objection unless there is any special reason,. 

(3) In the case of accepting an objection as a result of the deliberation and resolution made 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
pursuant to paragraph (2), it shall be deemed that the designation as an administrative issue has 
lost its validity as of the date of accepting the objection. Provided that, in applying the cause 
of delisting by formality review under [§54(1)] of the Regulation, it shall be deemed that the 
validity is lost retroactively from the concerned designation date. 

§58. Designations as Administrative Issues and Release therefrom   

(1) The timing of designating administrative issues and releasing therefrom pursuant to [§53(8)] 
of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 10]. 

(2) The provisions of paragraph (1) shall not apply during the trading period under [§23] of the 
Regulation. 

Section 3. Delisting   

§59. Methods of Applying Formality Condition for Delisting 

(1) “The confirmation letter of the auditor specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso 
to the part other than each subparagraph of [§54(1)1] of the Regulation shall mean attached 
[Annex: Form No. 31]. 

(2)  In  cases  where  a  common  stock-listed  corporation  spins  off  to  convert  into  a  holdings 
company but the conversion has not been completed, the reason of entire capital impairment 
of [§54(1)6] of the Regulation shall not apply to the business year which includes the date of 
the spin-off and the following business year. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(3) In cases where a corporation fails to submit the annual, semiannual or quarterly report by 
the statutory deadline due to cases falling under each subparagraph in [§52(1)], the provision 
of [§52(1)] shall apply mutatis mutandis, so that the respective period under each subparagraph 
of [§52(1)] shall be added to the statutory submission deadlines for the relevant report under 
subparagraphs 1, 1-2, 6 and 7 of [§54(1)] of the Regulation. (Amended on December 9, 2022; 
July 9, 2025) 

§60. Objection to Delisting by Formality Review, etc.   

(1) “Documents specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the part other than each subparagraph 
of [§55(1)] of the Regulation shall refer to the following documents: (Amended on December 
9, 2022) 

1.  An application for official objection in [Annex: Form No. 28]; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  An improvement plan that includes a plan to resolve the causes for delisting. In such 
cases,  if  the  causes  for  delisting  fall  under  any  of  the  following  items,  the  matters 
specified in each item shall be included: 

(a)  Case of falling under the main sentence of the part other than each subparagraph of 
[§54(1)1]  of  the  Regulation:  The  improvement  plan  to  resolve  the  causes  for 
delisting by revising the audit opinion on the relevant audit report or to receive an 
“unqualified” audit opinion on the audit report of the next fiscal year; and 

(b) Case  of  falling  under  the  proviso  to  the  part  other  than  each  subparagraph  of 
[§54(1)1]  of  the  Regulation:  The  improvement  plan  to  resolve  the  cause  for 
delisting by revising the audit opinion on the relevant half-year audit report or to 
receive an “unqualified” audit opinion on the audit report of the relevant business 
year (referring to the business year in which the relevant cause for delisting has 
occurred). 

3.  Opinion statements issued by experts in the relevant fields, including lawyers, certified 

public accountants, appraisers, etc.; and 

4.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to the official objection. 

(2) When an official objection pursuant to [§55(1)] of the Regulation has been received, unless 
there  is  a  special  reason,  the  Exchange  shall  hold  a  meeting  of  the  Corporate  Review 
Committee under [§55(2)] of the Regulation within twenty (20) days (based on business days) 
from the date of receiving the concerned objection and make a deliberation and resolution on 
the  following  matters.  In  such  cases,  the  Exchange  shall  grant  the  representative  of  the 
concerned common-stock-listed corporation an opportunity to state his/her opinion: 

1.  Whether or not to delist the concerned stock; 

2.  Feasibility of the improvement plan, whether or not to grant the improvement period, 

and if granted, the length of improvement period; and 

3.  Whether or not to suspend the trading of concerned stock and if suspended, the period 

of trading suspension. 

(3) In cases where an improvement period is granted pursuant to [§55(2)] of the Regulation, 
the  improvement  period  may  not  exceed  six  (6)  months  unless  there  is  a  special  reason. 
Provided that, in the case where a cause for delisting corresponds to audit opinion not up to 
standards of [§54(1)1] of the Regulation, the improvement period may not exceed one (1) year 
unless there are special reasons. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(4) The Exchange may examine whether the improvement plan is implemented based on the 
annual report, semi-annual report, quarterly report, etc. 

(5) In cases where the improvement period granted pursuant to [§55(2)] of the Regulation is 
expired,  the  common-stock-listed  corporation  shall  submit  the  following  documents  within 
fifteen (15) days (based on business days) after the end of the improvement period. Provided 
that, in case where the concerned common-stock-listed corporation files an application before 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the  end  of  the  improvement  period  pursuant  to  [§55(3)3]  of  the  Regulation,  the  following 
documents shall be submitted on the relevant application date:   

1.  An improvement plan implementation statement; 

2.  A written confirmation on the outcome of implementation of the improvement plan 
issued by experts in the relevant fields such as lawyers, certified public accountants or 
appraisers; and 

3.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the review of implementation 

of the improvement plan. 

(6) The Exchange shall hold the Corporate Review Committee under [§55(3)] of the Regulation 
within twenty (20) days (based on business days) from the date of submitting the documents 
under  paragraph  (5)  unless  there  is  a  special  reason.  In  such  cases,  the  Corporate  Review 
Committee shall make a deliberation and resolution on whether to delist or not by reflecting 
the implementation of the improvement plan. 

(7) The Exchange shall notify the relevant common-stock-listed corporation of the result of the 
deliberation and resolution in writing within three (3) days (based on business days) from the 
date of the deliberation and resolution by the Corporate Review Committee pursuant to [§55(2) 
and §55(3)] of the Regulation. 

(8) Notwithstanding paragraphs (2) and (6), in cases where an event that may have a significant 
effect  on  the  deliberation  of  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  such  as  court  judgments  or 
decisions on lawsuits, submissions of audit reports, etc. is scheduled to occur after the period 
during which the Corporate Review Committee is to be held under paragraph (2) or (6), the 
Exchange may extend the period for holding the Corporate Review Committee within twenty 
(20) days (based on business days).
