(9)  A  common-stock-listed  corporation  may  not  file  another  objection  to  the  decision  on 
delisting pursuant to [§55(2) and (3)] of the Regulation.   

(10) In cases where, before the deliberation and resolution of the Corporate Review Committee 
noted in [§55(3)] of the Regulation on whether or not to delist in relation to a delisting cause 
under any of the following subparagraphs that has already occurred, an official objection is 
filed as a delisting cause occurs additionally, the Corporate Review Committee under [§55(3)] 
of the Regulation shall make a combined deliberation and resolution for the delisting cause that 
occurred later. Provided that, this provision shall not apply when the Exchange deems that the 
combined deliberation is not appropriate considering the circumstances of the deliberation or 
other situations. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

1.  Delisting cause due to auditor’s opinion not up to standards pursuant to [§54(1)1] of the 

Regulation 

2.  Delisting cause due to failure of submitting regular report pursuant to [§54(1)7] of the 

Regulation 

(11)  In  cases  where  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  conducts  a  combined  deliberation 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
pursuant to the main sentence of paragraph (10), the date of filing the objection against the 
delisting cause that occurred later shall be regarded as the date of filing the objection pursuant 
to  [§55(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  and  the  procedures  noted  in  [§55(2)  through  §55(4)]  of  the 
Regulation  and  paragraphs  (2)  through  (9)  of  this  Article  shall  apply  mutatis  mutandis. 
(Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(12)  In  cases  where  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  conducts  a  combined  deliberation 
pursuant  to  the  main  sentence  of  paragraph  (10),  the  Exchange  shall  notify  the  relevant 
common-stock-listed corporation in writing without delay. 

(13) “Cases where the Enforcement Rules stipulates that the Corporate Review Committee’s 
deliberation and resolution is deemed not necessary” in [§55(4)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs: (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

1. Case  that  falls  under  any  of  the  following  items,  as  a  case  where  a  cause  of  auditor’s 

opinion not up to standards under [§54(1)1] of the Regulation occurs: 

(a)  Where the Exchange grants an improvement period until the tenth (10th) day from the 
next day of the statutory submission deadline of annual report of the following business 
year (refers to the business year that includes half-year period in which the cause of 
delisting occurs, in the case of the proviso to the part other than each item of [§54(1)1] 
of  the  Regulation;  hereinafter  the  same  in  this  subparagraph)  in  accordance  with  a 
formal objection. Provided that, in the case where there is a change in the concerned 
audit opinion during the improvement period or unqualified opinion on the audit report 
of the following business year, the improvement period is deemed to have been granted 
by the day of submission of that audit report pursuant to Disclosure Regulation. 

(b)  Where  a  corporation  falls  under  the  cause  of  listing  maintenance  review  under 
[§56(1)13] of the Regulation as the concerned cause of delisting is resolved through a 
change of audit opinion on the concerned audit report or by having unqualified opinion 
on the audit report of the following business year. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

2. Case where, as a  case where the improvement period was granted by filing  an official 
objection  for  a  cause  due  to  failing  to  submit  regular  report  under  [§54(1)7]  of  the 
Regulation, the Exchange recognizes that the cause of delisting is resolved by submitting 
all the unsubmitted regular reports within the improvement period.   

§60-2. Postponement of Delisting 

(1) The auditor's opinion (hereinafter referred to as the "auditor's opinion" in this Article) noted 
in  [§55-2(1)3]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  prepared  by  the  auditor  in  accordance  with  the   
Annex Form No. 31-2. 

(2) Unless there are special circumstances, the Exchange shall convene the Corporate Review 
Committee noted in the main sentence of [§55-2(1)] of the Regulation within 20 days (based 
on business days) from the date of receipt of the auditor's opinion noted in paragraph (1). 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) If a listed company fails to submit an auditor's opinion within the deadline stipulated in   
[§55-2(1)3] of the Regulation, or if the Corporate Review Committee noted in paragraph (2) 
determines that there is no need to postpone delisting, the Exchange shall proceed with delisting 
procedures such as final trading, etc. 

[July 9, 2025] 

§61. Methods of Applying Criteria for Listing Maintenance Review   

(1) “The specific criteria for judgment, etc.” in the latter part other than each subparagraph of 
[§56(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  refer  to  any  of the  following  subparagraphs:  (Amended  on 
December 9, 2022; June 14, 2024; July 9, 2025) 

1.  Circumvention  of  the  causes  of  delisting  according  to  formality  review  or  listing 
maintenance review noted in [§56(1)3] of the Regulation: Cases falling under any of 
the followings: (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  Where  it  is  recognized  that  the  cause  of  delisting  such  as  impairment  of  entire 
capital under [§54(1)6] of the Regulation, loss from continuing operations before 
tax under [§56(1)16] of the Regulation, capital impairment under [§56(1)17] of the 
Regulation  and  equity  capital  not  up  to  standards  under  [§56(1)18]  of  the 
Regulation  has  been  resolved  through  overestimating  of  the  investment  in-kind 
under Article 422 of the Commercial Act; (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(b) Where the suspicion of disguised payment under [§6(1)2(d)(ix)] of the Disclosure 
Regulation has been recognized and it is recognized that the cause of delisting such 
as  impairment  of  entire  capital  under  [§54(1)6]  of  the  Regulation,  loss  from 
continuing  operations  before  tax  under  [§56(1)16]  of  the  Regulation,  capital 
impairment  under  [§56(1)17]  of  the  Regulation  and  equity  capital  not  up  to 
standards  under  [§56(1)18]  of  the  Regulation  has  been  resolved  through  the 
relevant disguised payment; (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(c)  Where it is recognized that the cause of delisting due to sales not up to standards 
under  [§56(1)15]  of  the  Regulation  has  been  resolved  through  arbitrary  or 
temporary sales; (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(d) Where it is recognized that the cause for delisting due to a loss from continuing 
operations  before  tax  under  [§56(1)16]  of  the  Regulation  has  been  resolved  by 
accounting for the spin-off or sales of business units, etc. as a discontinuation of 
business; and (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(e)  Other  cases  where  the  Exchange  recognizes  that  the  causes  for  delisting  due  to 
formality review or the causes to be subject to the listing maintenance review have 
been circumvented. 

2.  Disclosures of embezzlement or breach of duty pursuant to [§56(1)4] of the Regulation, 
etc.: Case where an allegation of embezzlement or breach of duty on a scale set forth 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
in [§6(1)2(d)(vi)] of the Disclosure Regulation (in the case of officers, 3/100 or more 
of equity capital or at least KRW 1 billion) have been confirmed through a disclosure, 
etc.; (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

3.  A  serious  violation  of Article  5(3)  of  the  External Audit Act  under  [§56(1)5]  of  the 
Regulation,  etc.:  Cases  falling  under  any  of  the  followings  due  to  a  violation  of 
accounting standards, etc.: 

(a) Cases where a violation of the accounting standards has been  confirmed through 
the annual report, correction of annual report, details of accusation by the prosecutor 
and result of investigation by the Securities and Futures Commission, and in the event 
of reflecting the details of such violation, it constitutes the cause of delisting due to 
formality review under [§54] of the Regulation or the cause for listing maintenance 
review under [§56(1)3(o)through(r)] of the Regulation; (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(b) Where it is confirmed that the Financial Services Commission or the Securities and 
Futures  Commission  has  made  a  resolution  to  file  an  accusation  or  inform  the 
prosecutor’s office of the violation of accounting standards committed by a common-
stock-listed corporation or its officers (including former and current officers) noted in 
Article 2, Subparagraph 6 of the External Audit Act. Provided that, this excludes cases 
where the Financial Services Commission or the Securities and Futures Commission 
decides that measures for listing management of the Exchange are not necessary while 
making a resolution on filing a complaint with or notifying to prosecutor’s office; and 

(c)  Where  it  is  confirmed  that  a  common-stock-listed  corporation  which  has  been 
designated as an administrative issue or investment attention issue has been subject to 
a penalty surcharge by the Financial Services Commission or the Securities and Futures 
Commission for violation of the accounting standards. 

4.  Suspension  of  main  business  under  [§56(1)6]  of  the  Regulation:  Cases  where  it  is 
difficult to carry out an operation with the remaining business units due to falling under 
any of the followings. In such cases, the main business is judged based on the sales 
amount, but in cases where the Exchange deems it necessary, the added value amount 
may be used as the basis for such judgment. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a) Case where the production and sales activities of main business are discontinued. 
In the event where the discontinuation is caused by labor dispute or natural disaster,   
it shall be limited to cases where the production and sales activities are suspended for 
at least six (6) months; 

(b) Case where the permit or license related to main business is canceled or returned; 

(c) Case where the main business has been taken over or has been transferred to the 
company established through a spin-off or merger after spin-off (including the physical 
spin-off or merger after physical spin-off; hereinafter the same shall apply in this item). 
Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  be  applicable  to  cases  where  the  spin-off  or 
merger after spin-off has been carried out for the purpose of a conversion into a holding 
company (including a financial holding company under Article 2(1)1 of the Financial 
Holding  Companies  Act;  hereinafter  the  same  shall  apply  in  this  item)  and  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
establishment of the holding company was completed at the time of or after the spin-
off or merger after spin-off;   

(d) Case where the sales amount during the latest quarter is less than KRW 300 million 
or the sales amount during the latest semi-annual period is less than KRW 700 million. 
Provided  that,  this  provision  shall  not  apply  to  the  cases  falling  under  any  of  the 
followings: 

(i) Corporations that belong to the sector of financial and insurance industry in the 
industry classification specified in [Annex 11]; 

(ii)  Corporations  that  does  not  apply  the  criteria  for  designation  as  an 
administrative issue due to sales not up to standards pursuant to each paragraph of   
[§53(1)1] of the Regulation. In this case, “the latest fiscal year” in [§53(1)1(c)] of 
the Regulation shall be deemed as “the latest quarter” or the latest half-year”; and   

(iii)  Case  where  a  corporation  has  spun  off  in  order  to  convert  into  a  holding 
company but the conversion process has not been completed. Provided that, this 
shall apply only to the business year in which the date of spin-off belongs and the 
following business year. 

(e)  Case  where  a  foreign  holding  company  located  in  Korea  sells  the  entire  or 
significant  parts  of  the  equity  of  its  main  foreign  subsidiary,  and  the  main  foreign 
subsidiary loses the status of foreign subsidiary;   

(f)  Case  where  a  foreign  holding  company  located  in  Korea  transfers  the  entire  or 
significant parts    of the business of its main foreign subsidiary, and business activities 
of the main foreign subsidiary are practically halted as a result of the transfer; and 

(g) Other cases where the Exchange deems that the main business has been de facto 
discontinued. 

5.  Impairment  loss  under  [§56(1)8]  of  the  Regulation:  Case  where  an  amount  of 
impairment  loss  falling  under  [§6(1)2(d)(viii)]  of  the  Disclosure  Regulation  in 
receivables  other  than  trade  receivables  is  confirmed  through  disclosures,  etc.; 
(Amended on July 9, 2025) 

6.  Changes in management rights under [§56(1)9(a)] of the Regulation: Case where the 
change of the largest shareholder has been disclosed pursuant to [§6(1)3(a)(i)] of the 
Disclosure  Regulation,  or  the  conclusion  of  a  stock  purchase  agreement  or  an 
agreement  for  the  purpose  of  making  any  change  in  management  rights  under 
[§6(1)3(a)(ix)ⓐ] of the Disclosure Regulation has been disclosed; (Amended on July 
9, 2025) 

7.  A  decline  in  sales  under  [§56(1)11]  of  the  Regulation:  Case  where  it  is  confirmed 
through disclosures, etc. that the sales amount during the latest three (3) business years 
(counting from the business years to which the listing date belongs, but in cases where 
the period from the listing date to the end of the relevant business year is less than six 
(6)  months,  it  shall  be  counted  from  the  next  business  year)  falls  under  all  of  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
followings: (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  Where the annual sales are less than KRW 500 million; and 

(b) Where the annual sales decreased by 50/100 or more compared to the previous year. 

8.  Imposition of the demerit points related to the disclosure pursuant to [§56(1)12] of the 
Regulation: In cases where the designation as an administrative issue due to the cause 
subject to the listing maintenance review under [§56(1)12] of the Regulation has been 
released during the past one (1) year, the demerit points from the date on which the 
designation as an administrative issue was released shall be aggregated. (Amended on 
July 9, 2025) 

9.  “Amount specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the latter part of [§56(1)16] of the 
Regulation  shall  mean  the  financial  debt  evaluation  loss  that  is  confirmed  via  the 
[Annex Form No. 42] which is confirmed by the auditor, in a case where such form is 
submitted. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(2)  In  cases  where  a  corporation  becomes  subject  to  the  listing  maintenance  review,  the 
Corporate Review Committee or the Market Committee shall review whether to delist or not 
based on the following criteria: 

1. In the case of [§56(1)1] of the Regulation, the review shall be conducted by the criteria 
in the following items and items in subparagraph 3: (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  Reasons  for  turning  down  the  application  for  commencement  of  rehabilitation 

procedures, etc.; and 

(b) Whether the concerned common-stock-listed corporation is likely to continue as a 

going concern. 

2.  In the case of [§56(1)2] of the Regulation, the review shall be conducted by the criteria 

in the following items and items in subparagraph 3: (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  The significance of the falsely stated matters in the listing review and the listing 

maintenance review and their impact on investors; and 

(b) Whether or not the common-stock-listed corporation made the false statement, etc. 

by intent or gross negligence. 

3.  In the case of each item of [§56(1)3 through 19] of the Regulation, the review shall be 

conducted by the following criteria: (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(a)  Whether normal business activities are possible considering sales and profit/loss 

structure; 

(b) Whether the financial position would deteriorate due to the size of loan, contingent 

liability, embezzlement, etc.; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(c)  Whether the management transparency has been damaged due to embezzlements 
and poor corporate governance caused by frequent changes of largest shareholder, 
etc.; 

(d) Whether the details of violation of the disclosure obligations including violations 

of the accounting standards and unfaithful disclosures are serious; and 

(e)  In addition, whether the delisting is necessary for the soundness of the KOSDAQ 

Market and investor protection. 

(3) In  a case  where a  common stock-listed corporation had made a spin-off to  convert to  a 
shareholdings company but has not completed the conversion to a shareholdings company, the 
causes under [§56(1)15 through 18] of the Regulation shall not apply. (Amended on December 
9, 2022; July 9, 2025) 

(4) In cases where the business year of a common-stock-listed corporation is less than six (6) 
months due to a change in the fiscal year, etc., this business year shall not be included when 
applying the causes  for the operating loss pursuant  to  [§56(1)15 and 16] of the Regulation. 
(Amended on December 9, 2022; July 9, 2025) 

§61-2. Exclusion from Listing Maintenance Review   

(1) In the case of determining whether a corporation is subject to listing maintenance review 
or not pursuant to [§57(1)] of the Regulation, the Exchange may exclude the corporation in 
cases where the concerned cause is found after elapsing five (5) years from the occurrence of 
the  cause  of  listing  maintenance  review.  In  such  cases,  the  time  when  the  cause  of  listing 
maintenance  review  shall  be  based  on  the  time  when  the  behaviors,  etc.  relating  to  the 
concerned cause are finished. 

(2) Notwithstanding paragraph (1) above, in cases where the Exchange deems that the cause of 
listing maintenance review has material impact to the listing eligibility of a common stock-
listed  corporation,  it  may  decide  to  have  the  corporation  be  subject  to  listing  maintenance 
review. 

[December 9, 2022] 

§62. Procedures of Listing Maintenance Review   

(1)  The  Exchange  shall  hold  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  (referring  to  the  Market 
Committee in the case of proviso to [§57(3)] of the Regulation) within twenty (20) days (based 
on  business  days;  hereinafter  the  same  shall  apply  in  this  paragraph)  from  the  date  of 
notification pursuant to [§57(2)] of the Regulation. Provided that, in cases where a common-
stock-listed corporation submits an improvement plan within fifteen (15) days from the date of 
receiving  the  notification  pursuant  to  [§57(2)]  of  the  Regulation,  the  Corporate  Review 
Committee shall be held within twenty (20) days from the date of submitting the improvement 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
plan.   

(2) [Deleted on July 9, 2025] 

(3) In case of granting an improvement period through the deliberation and resolution of the 
Corporate Review Committee  under the main sentence of [§57(3)] of the Regulation  or the 
Market Committee under the proviso to [§57(5)] of the Regulation, the improvement period 
may not exceed one (1) year unless there is a special reason: (Amended on February 27, 2025; 
July 9, 2025) 

1.  [Deleted on July 9, 2025] 

2.  [Deleted on July 9, 2025] 

(4) In cases when the improvement period granted pursuant to paragraph (3) has ended, the 
relevant common-stock-listed corporation shall submit following documents to the Exchange 
within  fifteen  (15)  days  (based  on  business  days)  after  the  end  of  the  improvement  period. 
Provided that, in cases where the relevant common-stock-listed corporation applies before the 
end of the improvement period pursuant to [§57(7)3] of the Regulation, the documents shall be 
submitted on the date of application: 

1.  An improvement plan implementation statement; 

2.  A written confirmation on the outcome of implementation of the improvement plan 
issued by experts in the relevant fields such as lawyers, certified public accountants, 
appraisers, etc.; and 

3.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the review of implementation 

of the improvement plan. 

(5)  The  Exchange  shall  hold  the  Corporate  Review  Committee  or  the  Market  Committee 
pursuant to [§57(4) and §57(6)] of the Regulation within twenty (20) days (based on business 
days) from the date of submitting the documents under paragraph (4) unless there is a special 
reason. In this case, the Corporate Review Committee or Market Committee held may grant an 
additional  improvement  period  of  up  to  three  months  in  any  of  the  following  cases,  and 
paragraph (4) and the main sentence of this paragraph shall apply to the deliberation procedure 
after the end of the improvement period. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

1.  In the case where it is clearly recognized that there will be implementation of important 
parts of the improvement plan, such as change of the largest shareholder, paid-in capital 
increase, etc.; and (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

2.  In  the  case  where  a  court  ruling  or  decision  that  has  a  significant  impact  on  the 
implementation of the improvement plan is scheduled and it is necessary to confirm it. 
(Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(6)  During  the  improvement  period,  the  Exchange  may  inspect  the  implementation  of  the 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
improvement plan by reviewing an annual report, semi-annual report, quarterly report, etc. 

(7) Pursuant to [§57(8)] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall notify the relevant common-
stock-listed corporation of the result of deliberation and resolution in writing within three (3) 
days (based on business days) from the date of deliberation and resolution of the Corporate 
Review Committee or the Market Committee. 

(8) Notwithstanding paragraphs (1) and (5), in cases where an event that may have a significant 
effect on the result of the deliberation, such as where court judgments or decisions on lawsuits, 
submission  of  audit  reports,  etc.,  is  scheduled  to  occur  after  the  period  during  which  the 
Corporate Review Committee or the Market Committee is to be held pursuant to paragraphs 
(1) or (5), the Exchange may extend the period within twenty (20) days (based on business 
days). 

(9) The occurrence of a    formality condition for delisting under [§54] of the Regulation shall 
not affect the procedures of listing maintenance review under [§57] of the Regulation and the 
objection against delisting under [§58] of the Regulations. (February 27, 2025) 

(10)  The  representative  of  the  concerned  common-stock-listed  corporation  may  attend  the 
meeting of Corporate Review Committee or the Market Committee and express his/her opinion. 

(11) The Exchange shall organize the Corporate Review Committee with specialists from the 
academia, legal and accounting fields who are able to conduct the deliberation of the listing 
maintenance review in an objective manner. In such cases, the details of the operation of the 
Corporate Review Committee shall be separately specified by the Exchange. 

§63. Procedures of Objection against Delisting by Listing Maintenance Review   

(1) “Documents stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§58(1)] of the Regulation shall refer 
to the following documents: 

1.  Application for objection in [Annex 28]; 

2.  Improvement plan to resolve the cause for delisting; 

3.  Opinion letters of experts, such as lawyers, certified accountants, appraisers, etc. in the 

fields; and 

4.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary in relation to an objection. 

(2) The Exchange shall hold  the Market  Committee pursuant  to  [§58(2)] of the Regulation, 
unless there is a special reason, within twenty (20) days (based on business days) from the date 
of  receiving  the  objection  under  [§58(1)]  of  the  Regulation  to  deliberate  and  decide  on  the 
matters specified in each of the following subparagraph: 

1.  Whether to delist the concerned stock; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
2.  Feasibility of the improvement plan, whether to grant the improvement period, and if 

granted, the length of improvement period; and 

3.  Whether to suspend the trading of concerned stock and if suspended, the period of trade 

suspension. 

(3)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  holds  the  Market  Committee  pursuant  to  [§58(2)]  of  the 
Regulation, it shall grant the representative of the concerned common-stock-listed corporation 
an opportunity to state his/her opinion. 

(4) In the case of granting an improvement period through the deliberation and resolution of 
the Market Committee pursuant to [§58(2)] of the Regulation, the improvement period may 
not exceed six (6) months unless there is a special reason, and the total period of improvement 
granted pursuant to [§62(3)] may not exceed one (1) year in total. (Amended on February 27, 
2025; July 9, 2025; March 31, 2026) 

(5) In cases where the improvement period granted pursuant to paragraph (4) has expired, the 
relevant  common-stock-listed  corporation  shall  submit  the  following  documents  to  the 
Exchange within fifteen (15) days (based on business days) after the end of the improvement 
period 

1.  An improvement plan implementation statement; 

2.  A written confirmation on the outcome of implementation of the improvement plan 
issued by experts in the relevant fields such as lawyers, certified public accountants, 
appraisers, etc.; and 

3.  Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the review of implementation 

of the improvement plan. 

(6) The Exchange shall hold the Market Committee within twenty (20) days (based on business 
days) from the date of receiving the documents under paragraph (5) unless there is a special 
reason. In this case, the Market Committee held may grant an additional improvement period 
of up to three (3) months if any of subparagraphs in §62(5)] apply, and paragraph (5) and the 
main sentence of this paragraph shall apply to the deliberation procedure after the end of the 
improvement period. (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

(7) Notwithstanding paragraphs (2) and (6), in cases where an event that may have a significant 
effect  on  the  result  of  the  deliberation,  such  as  court  judgments  or  decisions  on  lawsuits, 
submission  of  audit  reports,  etc.,  is  scheduled  to  occur  after  the  period  during  which  the 
Corporate Review Committee or the Market Committee is to be held pursuant to paragraphs 
(2) and (6), the Exchange may extend the period within twenty (20) days (based on business 
days). 

(8)  During  the  improvement  period,  the  Exchange  may  inspect  the  implementation  of  the 
improvement plan by reviewing an annual report, semi-annual report, quarterly report, etc. 

(9)  A  common-stock-listed  corporation  may  not  file  another  objection  to  the  decision  on 
delisting under paragraphs (2) through (4) of [§58] of the Regulation. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(10) The Exchange shall notify the relevant common-stock-listed corporation of the result of 
deliberation and resolution in writing within three (3) days (based on business days) from the 
date of deliberation and resolution of the Market Committee pursuant to paragraphs (2) through 
(4) of [§58] of the Regulation. 

CHAPTER Ⅲ. LISTING AND LISTING MANAGEMENT OF OTHER SECURITIES 

Section 1. Foreign Stocks, etc. 

§64. Preliminary Listing Review, etc. of Foreign Stocks   

(1) The  application for preliminary listing review of foreign  stocks, etc.  and supplementary 
documents pursuant to [§60(2)] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 1].   

(2)  The  application  for  initial  listing  of  foreign  stocks,  etc.  and  supplementary  documents 
pursuant to [§60(2)] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 2]. 

§65. Exception to Mandatory Holding for Initial Listing of Foreign Stocks, etc.   

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§61(1)1] of the Regulation 
shall refer to cases falling under any of subparagraphs of [§23(1)]. In such cases, the provision 
of [§23(2)] shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(2) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§61(1)2] of the Regulation 
shall refer to cases falling under any of subparagraphs of [§23(3)].   

(3) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§61(1)3] of the Regulation 
shall refer to cases falling under any of subparagraphs of [§23(4)] (excluding paragraph (2).) 

(4) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§61(1)4] of the Regulation 
shall refer to cases falling under any of subparagraphs of [§23(5)] (excluding paragraph (2).) 

(5) The disparate ratio between the acquisition price and the public offering price pursuant to 
the proviso to [§61(1)5] of the Regulation shall be calculated by the method specified in each 
subparagraph of [§23(6)]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§66. Methods of Applying Review Requirements for Initial Listing of Foreign Stocks, 
etc.   

“Cases  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  main  sentence  of  [§62(1)1(a)(i)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to cases falling under [§26(1)].   

§67. Special Cases for Foreign Technology Growth Companies 

(1)  “Cases  where  technology  and  growth  potential  are  recognized  in  accordance  with  the 
Enforcement  Rules”  in  the  former  part  other  than  each  subparagraph  of  [§63(1)]  of  the 
Regulation shall refer to cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Where  assessments  on  technology,  etc.  shall  be  conducted  by  two  (2)  specialized 
assessment  institutions  within  six  (6)  months  before  the  application  date  for 
preliminary listing review and the assessment results shall be all grade A or higher; or 

2.  Where  the  base  market  capitalization  is  KRW  one  (1)  trillion  or  more,  and 
technological  skill  or  growth  potential  is  recognized  through  qualitative  review 
requirements pursuant to [§62(1)6] of the Regulation. 

(2) “Requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” under [§63(1)2] of the Regulation shall 
refer  to  all  of  the  following  requirements.  Provided  that,  the  requirements  in  each  of  the 
following subparagraphs shall not apply to a listing sponsor who is not a managing underwriter 
pursuant to the Regulation on Securities Underwriting Business, etc.: (Amended on February 
14, 2022; March 9, 2023; Amended on December 28, 2023) 

1.  There shall be a record  of having  sponsored the listing of an innovative technology 
company within the past three (3) years from the date of application for preliminary 
listing review. Provided that, this provision shall not apply in cases where the Exchange 
deems it inevitable due to a sudden change in market situations or economic conditions; 
and 

2.  The KOSDAQ-listed foreign corporation or the foreign holding company located in 
Korea whose listing was sponsored within the past three (3) years (based on the date 
of  application  for  preliminary  listing  review)  shall  not  have  a  record  of  being 
designated as an investment attention issue or an administrative issue pursuant to the 
Regulation, or a cause of delisting due to formality review or a cause of delisting as a 
result of listing maintenance review shall not have occurred within two (2) years after 
the listing. 

§68. Application Documents for Listing Change and Supplementary Listing of Foreign 
Stocks, etc.   

The application for listing change or supplementary listing of foreign stocks, etc. pursuant to 
[§65(1)] of the Regulation and supplementary documents shall be stipulated in [Annex 5]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§69. Designation of Investment Attention Issues and Administrative Issues and Delisting 
of Foreign Stocks, etc. 

(1) The timings of designation as an investment attention issue and release from the designation 
pursuant to [§66] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 9]. 

(2) The  timings  of  designation  as  an  administrative  issue  and  release  from  the  designation 
pursuant to [§67] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 10]. 

(3)  Notwithstanding  [§83(2)],  in  the  case  of  applying  the  causes  for  designation  as  an 
administrative issue and delisting due to formality review, foreign currency shall be converted 
into Korean currency according to the base exchange rate that was determined and published 
in accordance with the Foreign Exchange Transaction Regulation as of the end of the latest 
business  year  and  applied.  Provided  that,  in  cases  where  [§52(1)2(h)&(i)  of  the  Regulation 
applies mutatis mutandis pursuant to [§66(1)] of the Regulation, the equity capital at the end 
of  semiannual  period  shall  be  calculated  based  on  the  base  exchange  rate  determined  and 
published  at  the  end  of  semiannual  period  in  accordance  with  the  Foreign  Exchange 
Transaction Regulation. (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

(4) In cases where the causes subject to listing maintenance review applied to a common-stock-
listed corporation apply mutatis mutandis pursuant to [§68(1)] of the Regulation, “a foreign 
holding company located in  Korea” in  [§61(1)4(e) and §61(1)4(f)] shall be construed  as “a 
foreign holding company.” 

Section 2. Stocks of Special Purpose Acquisition Companies 

§70. Application for Preliminary Listing Review of Stocks of Special Purpose 
Acquisition Companies 

(1)  The  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  of  stocks  of  special  purpose  acquisition 
companies  and  supplementary  documents  pursuant  to  [§69(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be 
stipulated in [Annex 1]. 

(2) The  application  for  initial  listing  of  stocks  of  special  purpose  acquisition  companies  in 
[§69(1)] of the Regulation and supplementary documents shall be stipulated in [Annex 2]. 

(3) Pursuant to the part other than each subparagraph of [§70(1)9] of the Regulation, special 
purpose acquisition companies shall set the essential matters to be included in the articles of 
incorporation set forth in [Annex 13] in their articles of incorporation. 

(4)  In  accordance  with  [§70(1)10]  of  the  Regulation,  shareholders,  etc.  of  special  purpose 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
acquisition companies shall agree to the matters in each of the following subparagraphs as of 
the date of application for preliminary listing review: 

1.  The  details  that  shareholders,  etc.  as  of  the  application  date  of  preliminary  listing 
review will not exercise their voting rights pursuant to Article 522 of the Commercial 
Act  with  respect  to  the  stocks,  etc.  (including  the  stocks  acquired  by  exercising  the 
rights such as conversion rights granted to the relevant stocks, etc.) acquired prior to 
the initial public offering of stocks of the special purpose acquisition company, or will 
exercise  their  votes  in  accordance  with  the  proportion  of  pros  and  cons  (including 
abstention and invalidity) without affecting the details of the resolution made by the 
number of stocks obtained by subtracting the number of stocks held by the shareholders, 
etc. from the number of stocks (including the number of stocks voted in writing) held 
by the shareholders participated in the general meeting of shareholders by delegating 
their voting rights to the Korea Securities Depository; 

2.  The details that the shareholders, etc. as of the application date for preliminary listing 
review will not exercise appraisal rights pursuant to Article 522-3 of the Commercial 
Act; 

3.  The details that the shareholders, etc. as of the application date for preliminary listing 
review will, in cases where the special purpose acquisition company is dissolved as it 
falls  under  any  of  the  items  of  Article  1-4-2(5)2  of  the  Regulations  on  Financial 
Investment Business established by the Financial Services Commission, comply with 
the methods and the procedures specified in  the  articles of incorporation  in  relation 
with the return of money deposited or trusted with deposit institutions, etc.; and 

4.  The details that the shareholders etc. will perform their duties of compensation for the 
damage occurred due to  the violation of the agreement pursuant to subparagraphs 1 
through 3. 

§71. Application Documents on Listing Change and Supplementary Listing of Stocks of 
Special Purpose Acquisition Companies 

The  application  for  listing  change  or  supplementary  listing  of  stocks  of  special  purpose 
acquisition companies pursuant to [§71(1)] of the Regulation and supplementary documents 
shall be stipulated in [Annex 5].   

§72. Designation of Stocks of Special Purpose Acquisition Company as Administrative 
Issue   

(1) With respect to the designation as an administrative issue and release from such designation 
due  to  a  failure  to  meet  the  qualifications  for  officers  under  [§72(2)1]  of  the  Regulation,  a 
special purpose acquisition company shall appoint an officer or in cases where its officer was 
disqualified, submit a confirmation on whether the qualifications for officers are met. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) With respect to the designation as an administrative issue due to stock distribution not up 
to standards under [§72(2)2] of the Regulation, a special purpose acquisition company shall 
submit the summarized register of shareholders in [Annex: Form No. 30] and documents that 
are deemed necessary by the Exchange  within five (5) days  from  the statutory deadline for 
submission  of  annual  reports.  In  such  cases,  the  special  purpose  acquisition  company  may 
submit them via the electronic disclosure system under [§54(1)] of the Disclosure Regulation. 

(3) The timings of designation as an administrative issue and release from such designation 
pursuant to [§72(4)] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 10]. 

§73. Delisting of Stocks of Special Purpose Acquisition Companies 

(1) “Causes specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to [§73(1)] of the Regulation 
shall refer to the cause specified in [§61(1)3(c)].   

(2)  “A  corporation  that  has  special  interests  specified  in  the  Enforcement  Rules”  in 
[§73(2)9(a)(iv)] of the Regulation shall refer to a corporation falling under any of the following 
subparagraphs: 

1.  A  financial  investment  company  prescribed  in Article  6(4)14(c)  of  the  Enforcement 

Decree of the Act; 

2.  Shareholders, etc. (excluding financial investment companies under subparagraph 1; 
hereinafter the same shall apply in this paragraph) of the special purpose acquisition 
company as of the application date for preliminary listing review; 

3.  A  company  of  which  major  shareholder  under Article  9(1)  of  the Act  is  the  person 

falling under any of the following items: 

(a)  Financial  investment  companies  under  paragraph  (1)  (including  the  officers  and 
employees of the concerned financial investment company who had performed or 
are performing the work related to the establishment and operation of the concerned 
special purpose acquisition company and their spouses and lineal ascendants and 
descendants); 

(b) Shareholders, etc. as of the application date for preliminary listing review under 
paragraph (2) (in cases where the concerned shareholder, etc. is a legal entity, the 
officers  of  the  concerned  legal  entity,  their  spouses,  and  lineal  ascendants  and 
descendants  shall  be  included  and  in  the  case  of  individuals,  their  spouses,  and 
lineal ascendants and descendants shall be included); and 

(c)  Officers  and  employees  of  the  concerned  special  purpose  acquisition  company 
(including  the  spouses  and  lineal  ascendants  and  descendants  of  the  concerned 
officers and employees). 

4.  A company in which a person falling under any of items of subparagraph 3 holds 5/100 

or more of the total number of outstanding shares; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
5.  a financial investment company under subparagraph 1 or major shareholders such as 
the shareholders,  etc. as  of the application date for preliminary listing review under 
subparagraph 2 (limited to cases where the concerned shareholders are a legal entity: 
hereinafter the same shall apply in this Article), and affiliated companies pursuant to 
the Monopoly Regulation and Fair Trade Act (hereinafter referred to as “the affiliated 
company” in this Article); and 

6.  The relevant special purpose acquisition company, the financial investment company 
noted in subparagraph 1, shareholders, etc. as of the application date for preliminary 
listing  review  noted  in  subparagraph  2,  and  a  company  that  currently  serves  as  an 
employee or has held a concurrent position within the past two (2) years. 

(3) In determining the number of shares held in paragraph (2)4, the number of shares noted in 
each of the following subparagraphs shall be included: 

1.  The number of shares that may be issued subsequent to the exercise of rights of stocks, 

etc.; 

2.  The  number  of  shares  held  by  the  affiliated  companies  of  the  financial  investment 

company noted in paragraph (2)1; and 

3.  The number of shares held by the affiliated companies of the shareholders, etc. as of 

the application date for preliminary listing review noted in paragraph (2)2. 

§74. Preliminary Listing Review for Listing after Merger 

The application for preliminary listing review and the supplementary documents pursuant to 
[§74] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 1]. 

§75. Review Requirements for Listing after Merger, etc. 

(1) “Case where the Exchange deems it necessary in the Enforcement Rules” in [§75(1)1(a)] 
of the Regulation shall refer to cases where requirements under the front part of [§26(2)] are 
met, in this case, the latter part of [§26(2)] shall apply mutandis mutatis. [July 9, 2025] 

(2) “Requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§75(4)1(d)] of the Regulation shall 
refer to requirements in following subparagraphs:   

1.  A  company  shall  not  have  received  any  disciplinary  measures  from  the  Financial 
Services  Commission  or  the  Exchange  during  the  past  one  (1)  year  due  to   
noncompliance  with  the  financial  laws  and  regulations  or  the  regulations  of  the 
Exchange; and 

2.  In  addition,  it  is  deemed  that  the  realization  of  the  public  interest  and  protection  of 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
investors are not undermined. 

(3) “Requirements stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in [§75(4)2(c)] of the Regulation shall 
refer to requirements in following subparagraphs: 

1.  The corporation that is a target of merger shall satisfy all of the following items: 

(a)  The sales amount shall  be at least  KRW 10 billion and there shall be operating 

profits in the latest business year; 

(b) There shall be a recommendation from the M&A professional institution, which 
has registered the trade name of the corporation that is a target of merger in the 
KRX M&A intermediary network; and 

(c)  The corporation that is a target of merger shall not engage in the businesses that 
are deemed to undermine the balanced development of national economy and the 
function  of  efficient  financing  of  the  capital  market  or  to  run  counter  to  good 
morals and other social orders. 

2.  A special purpose acquisition company shall have no record of having been subject to 

listing maintenance review over the past two (2) years. 

(4) The review requirements for listing after merger of a special purpose acquisition company 
shall be determined based on the application date for preliminary listing review of listing after 
merger. 

(5) A listing specification noted in [§75(6)] of the Regulation shall refer to [Annex: Form No. 
41]. 

(6)  “The  application  for  listing  after  merger  and  the  supplementary  documents  shall  be 
submitted to the Exchange in accordance with the Enforcement Rules” in the former part of 
[§76(1)2] of the Regulation shall refer to the submissions of the application for listing after 
merger in [Annex Form No. 3] and the supplementary documents pursuant to [Annex No. 2-2] 
through the listing sponsor within one (1) year after the registration of the merger. [February 
14, 2022] 

(7) “The requirements specified in the Enforcement Rules” in the latter part of [§76(1)2] of the 
Regulation shall refer to the requirements in [§26(3)]. [February 14, 2022] (Amended on April 
29, 2022) 

(8) Pursuant to the latter part of [§76(2)] of the Regulation, in cases where the applicant for 
listing after merger fails to meet the requirements in paragraph (7), the listing may be deferred 
until the relevant cause is resolved. [February 14, 2022] (Amended on July 9, 2025) 

§76. Mandatory Holding for Listing after Merger 

(1) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to subparagraph 2 of [§77] of 
the Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(3)]. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(2) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to subparagraph 3 of [§77] of 
the Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(4)]. 

(3) “Cases stipulated in the Enforcement Rules” in the proviso to subparagraph 4 of [§77] of 
the Regulation shall refer to the cases falling under any of the subparagraphs of [§23(5)]. 

Section 3. Different Classes of Stocks   

§77. Application for Preliminary Listing Review of Different Classes of Stocks 

(1)  The  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  of  different  classes  of  stocks  (including 
foreign  different  classes  of  stocks;  hereinafter  the  same  shall  apply  in  this  Section)  and 
supplementary documents pursuant to [§78] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 1]. 

(2)  The  application  for  initial  listing  and  supplementary  documents  of  different  classes  of 
stocks pursuant to [§78] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 2]. 

§78. Review Requirements for Initial Listing of Different Classes of Stocks 

“The criteria specified in the Enforcement Rules” in subparagraph 7 of [§79] of the Regulation 
shall refer to the cases falling under any of the following subparagraphs:   

1.  Where the relevant different classes of stocks could be abused as a means of defending 

the management rights of existing shareholders; 

2.  Where  the  interests  of  shareholders  is  infringed  due  to  the  imbalance  between  the 
equity investment and corporate governance power which should be proportional to the 
equity investment; 

3.  Where there is no sufficient financial resource for dividend payment or repayment; and 

4.  Other cases that are deemed to be contradictory to the realization of public interests 

and the protection of investors. 

§79. Application Documents for Listing Change and Supplementary Listing of Different 
Classes of Stocks 

The application and supplementary documents for listing change and supplementary listing of 
different classes of stocks pursuant to [§80] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 5].   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
§80. Designation as Administrative Issue and Delisting of Different Classes of Stocks 

(1) With respect to the insufficient number of shareholders under [§81(1)2] of the Regulation, 
the  method  of  applying  the  stock  distribution  not  up  to  standards  to  common  stocks  under 
[§55(1)] shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(2) With respect to the shortfall in market capitalization pursuant to [§81(1)4] and [§82(1)4] of 
the Regulation, the method of applying the shortfall in market capitalization to common stocks 
under [§51] shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(3) With respect to the shortfall in trading volume pursuant to [§81(1)5] of the Regulation, the 
method of applying the shortfall in market capitalization to common stocks under [§54(1) and 
§5(3)] shall apply mutatis mutandis. 

(4) The timings of designation as an administrative issue and release from such designation for 
different classes of stocks pursuant to [§81(1)] of the Regulation shall be stipulated in [Annex 
10]. 

Section 4. Subscription Warrants and Subscription Right Certificates   

§81. Application Documents for Initial Listing of Subscription Warrants and 
Subscription Right Certificates 

The  application  for  initial  listing  and  supplementary  documents  of  subscription  warrants  or 
subscription  right  certificates  pursuant  to  [§83(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  stipulated  in 
[Annex 2].   

§82. Application Documents on Listing Change of Subscription Warrants and 
Subscription Right Certificates   

The application for listing change and supplementary documents of subscription warrants or 
subscription  right  certificates  pursuant  to  [§84(1)]  of  the  Regulation  shall  be  stipulated  in 
[Annex 5]

CHAPTER Ⅴ. SUPPLEMENTARY PROVISIONS 

§83. Submission of Documents of Foreign Companies 

(1) Pursuant to [§87] of the Regulation, documents to be submitted by foreign companies shall 
be prepared in Korean language. Provided that, in cases where the Exchange deems it necessary, 
the attached documents may be written in English, and in such cases, a summary in Korean 
shall be attached. 

(2) Pursuant to [§87] of the Regulation, in the details of the documents submitted by foreign 
companies, matters regarding the amount shall be expressed in Korean currency. In such cases, 
it  shall  be  the  amount  converted  into  Korean Won  on  the  basis  of  the  basic  exchange  rate 
determined and published pursuant to the Foreign Exchange Transaction Regulation as of the 
base date of the financial information. 

§84. Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

Pursuant to [§88(2)] of the Regulation, the imposition criteria, the fee rate, the payment timing, 
the  exemption  criteria,  and  other  necessary  matters  of  listing  fees  and  annual  dues  shall  be 
stipulated in [Annex 14]. 

§85. Criteria for Industry Classification 

(1) Pursuant to [§89] of the Regulation, the Exchange shall classify industries by business types 
and  codes  specified  in  [Annex  11]  based  on  the  Korean  Standard  Industrial  Classification 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Korean Standard Industrial Classification”) published by the 
Commissioner of Statistics Korea in accordance with the Statistics Act. 

(2) The industry classification in paragraph (1) shall be carried out by the following methods: 

1.  In  cases  where  a  company  is  engaged  in  two  (2)  or  more  businesses,  its  industry 
division shall be the business yielding the largest sales amount. Provided that, in cases 
where the Exchange deems it necessary, it may be classified into the business yielding 
the highest added value; 

2.  In cases where the classification method specified in the subparagraph 1 is difficult to 
apply, the factors such as the number of employees and facilities shall be taken into 
consideration in determining the industry classification; 

3.  In  cases  where  it  is  difficult  to  classify  the  industrial  division  because  its  business 
details are not clear, it shall be classified under the other sector of similar industry; and 

4.  In the case of a holding company, if the proportion of the sales of a specific industry 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
sector is 50/100 or more on the consolidated financial statements, it shall be classified 
into the relevant industry. Provided that, the holding company may submit documents 
such as the management plans concerning the industry classification, and the Exchange 
may make the industry classification by comprehensively considering the realization 
of public interests and protection of investors, etc. 

(3)  In  cases  where  a  KOSDAQ-listed  corporation  falls  under  any  of  the  following 
subparagraphs, the industry classification of the corporation shall be changed. Provided that, 
no change in the industry classification shall take place if the Exchange deems that the industry 
reclassification is unnecessary in view of such factors as the history and business forecast of 
the  concerned  corporation  and  the  change  of  sub-sector  within  the  same  sector  may  not  be 
made: 

1.  Case where the reclassification of industrial division is necessary as a result of a change 

in the Korea Standard Industrial Classification; 

2.  Case where the main business has been changed due to a merger, spin-off, acquisition 

or transfer of business, etc.; 

3.  Case where the level of sales ratio for main products has changed for the past two (2) 
business years in a row, and the growth within the existing industrial division cannot 
be expected;   

4.  Case where there was a significant change in the level of sales ratio of main products 
in  the  latest  one  (1)  business  year  due  to  the  reorganization  of  business  structure,  a 
change  of  main  business,  etc.,  and  the  Exchange  deems  that  the  reclassification  is 
necessary upon receiving the request for industry reclassification from the concerned 
listed corporation; 

5.  Case where the industrial classification has been changed by the laws; and 

6.  Other cases where the reclassification of industry is deemed necessary. 

(4) The timing of reclassifying the industry sectors of KOSDAQ-listed corporations shall be 
each of the following subparagraphs: 

1.  Case of subparagraphs 1, 5 and 6 of paragraph (3): The time when the relevant fact has 

been confirmed; 

2.  Case of subparagraph 2 of paragraph (3): The time when the document proving that the 
main business has been changed as a result of the concerned merger, spin-off. business 
acquisition/transfer, etc. was submitted; and 

3.  Case of subparagraphs 3 and 4 of paragraph(3): The first trading day of the fifth (5th) 
month counted from the month following the month which includes the fiscal closing 
date  of  the  KOSDAQ-listed  corporation.  Provided  that,  if  a  KOSDAQ-listed 
corporation  fails  to  submit  its  annual  report  by  the  statutory  deadline  due  to  cases 
falling under each subparagraph in [§52(1)], the timing of industry reclassification for 
the corporation and the submission deadline of review materials required for industry 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
classification may be separately determined by the Exchange. 

(5)  The  Exchange  shall  classify  the  industries  of  KOSDAQ-listed  foreign  companies  by 
applying paragraphs (1) through (4) mutatis mutandis. Provided that, the Exchange may change 
the  time  of  industry  reclassification  and  the  submission  deadline  for  materials  required  for 
industry classification in consideration of the submission deadline for annual report under the 
laws of the home country of KOSDAQ-listed foreign companies. 

(6) The Exchange may request KOSDAQ-listed corporations to provide the materials needed 
for industry reclassification. 

(7)  KOSDAQ-listed  corporations  shall  submit  the  materials  necessary  for  the  industry 
classification under subparagraphs 3 and 4 of paragraph (3) to the Exchange by the statutory 
submission deadline for annual reports. 

§86. Opinion Gathering   

The opinion gathering pursuant to [§90] of the Regulation shall be governed by the provisions 
of  [§5]  of  the  Internal  Regulations  Management  Regulation  and  [§6]  of  the  Regulations 
Management Regulation. 

. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
ADDENDA 
(Regulation No. 1990, October 27, 2021)   

§1. Regulation on the Enforcement of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation     

The Wholly Amended Regulation of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, Regulation No. 
1977, shall become effective on November 1, 2021. Provided that, the amended provisions of 
[§2(1)1(f)(ii)],  the  latter  part  of  [§69(2)],  the  proviso  to  [§70(1)9(d)(iii)],  the  proviso  to 
[§73(2)9(c)] and [§76(1)2] shall be effective from February 15, 2022. 

§2. Effective Date 

These  Enforcement  Rules  shall  become  effective  on  November  1,  2021.  Provided  that,  the 
amended provision of [Annex 8] shall be effective from May 2, 2022.   

§3. Applicable Case concerning Listing Sponsors of Technology Growth Companies   

The amended provisions of [§28(2)] and [§67(2)] shall apply starting from the corporation that 
requests a preliminary listing review after the effective date of these Enforcement Rules.   

§4.  Applicable  Case  concerning  Improvement  Period  Granted  Due  to  Delisting  by  Audit 
Opinion 

The amended provision of [§60(13)] shall apply starting from the corporation that is granted 
an improvement period after the effective date of these Enforcement Rules.   

§5. General Interim Measures   

Applications, requests, determinations, procedures and other actions pursuant to the previous 
Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation at the time these Enforcement 
Rules  enter  into  force  shall  be  deemed  to  have  been  conducted  in  accordance  with  these 
Enforcement Rules.   

§6. Interim Measures concerning Designations of Administrative Issues and Release therefrom 
for Different Classes of Stocks   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) In the cases of different classes of shares listed as of October 1, 2020, notwithstanding the 
amended provisions of subparagraph 2 (iii) and (iv) in [Annex 10], the number of listed stocks 
and the market capitalization in the following table shall apply in lieu of the number of listed 
stocks  under  the  amended  provisions  of  subparagraph  2  (iii)  in  [Annex  10]  and  the  market 
capitalization under amended provisions of subparagraph 2 (iv) in [Annex 10] until September 
30, 2022.

(2) The  number  of  days  satisfying  the  market  capitalization  pursuant  to  [§33-6(1)4]  of  the 
previous  Regulation  (referring  to  the  Regulation  before  the  Partial  Amendment  to  the 
Enforcement Rules of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, Regulation No. 1865) at the time 
when  the  Partial  Amendment  to  the  Enforcement  Rules  of  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulation, Regulation No. 1865, entered into force shall be construed as the number of days 
in accordance with the amended provisions of the Partial Amendment of the Enforcement Rules 
of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, Regulation No. 1865. 

§7. Interim Measures for Selection Criteria of Corporate Insolvency Risks 

In accordance with the proviso to [§2], the provisions of [Annex 3] of the previous Regulation 
(referring  to  the  Regulation  before  the  Partial  Amendment  to  the  Enforcement  Rules  of 
KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, Regulation No. 1896) shall apply before the amended 
provisions of [Annex 8] enter into force.   

§8. Interim Measures for Assessments, etc. of Specialized Assessment Institutions 

(1) The amended provisions of [§2(6)1] and [§9] of the Partial Amendment to the Enforcement 
Rules  of  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation,  Regulation  No.  1951,  shall  apply  from  the 
assessment of a specialized assessment institution pursuant to [§9] of the same Enforcement 
Rules after April 26, 2021.   

(2) The amended provision of [§2(6)2] of the Partial Amendment to the Enforcement Rules of 
KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, Regulation No. 1951, shall apply from the corporation, 
which requests a preliminary listing review after April 26, 2021. 

§9. Relation with Other Regulations 

In cases when other regulations, enforcement rules and guidelines cited the provisions of the 
previous “Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation” at the time when 
these  Enforcement  Rules  have  become  effective,  it  shall  be  deemed  that  the  concerned 
provisions of these Enforcement Rules have been cited in  lieu of the previous provisions if 
there is a corresponding provision among these Enforcement Rules.

5 shall be “[§33] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation”.

5 (limited to a case where the cause for dissolution is a adjudication of bankruptcy), 10, 11 of

Market”) and subparagraphs 1, 2, 3, 4, 5 (limited to a case where the cause for dissolution is a

§4. Applicable Case concerning Timing of Designation and Release of Investment Attention

§5. Applicable Case concerning Timing of Designation and Release of Administrative Issue

§6. Interim Measure concerning Timing of Designation and Release of Administrative Issue 

(1) With regard to the timing of release from the designation as an administrative issue for a 
corporation that was decided to be subject to listing maintenance review due to the reason of 
[§56(1)3(i)] of the previous Rules, the previous Rules shall apply notwithstanding the amended 
provisions of [Annex No. 10]. 

(2) With regard to the timing of release from the designation as an administrative issue for the 
corporation of which reason for delisting by formality review was incurred based on half-year 
period pursuant to the previous rules of [§54(1)8(b),(c) and(d)], the previous Rules shall apply 
notwithstanding the amended provisions of [Annex No. 10].

part as follows:

2(4)], the proviso to [§16(3)], the proviso to the part other than each subparagraph of [§17-
2(2)], the proviso to [§17-3(1)], the proviso to [§18-2], and the proviso to the part other than 
each  subparagraph  of  [§21-2(3)]  shall  be  “[§56(1)3(j)]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulation".

effective date of these Regulations, the suspended procedures shall not be resumed until the 
formality conditions for delisting are resolved.

(Regulation No. 2426 / March 31, 2026)

§2. Case of Application concerning Improvement of Listing Maintenance Review Procedure

[Annex No. 1] Documents for Application for Preliminary Listing Review 
(Amended on February 14, 2022; April 29, 2022; March 9, 2023; December 28, 2023; March 16, 2026) 

Documents for Application for Preliminary Listing Review 

(Pertaining to [§9, §13, §22, §36, §64, §70, §74, §77, §82-2, and §82-6] of the Enforcement Rules) 

1. Initial listing   

(a) Common stocks 

(1) Application for preliminary listing review separately determined by the Exchange 
(2) Financial documents for an applicant for initial listing: 

a) Individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and auditor’s audit 

reports thereof; 

b) Following additional documents in cases where the auditor was designated during the relevant   
business year pursuant to Paragraph (6)1 of Article 14 of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on   
External Audit of Stock Companies, Etc.: 
i) Individual and consolidated financial statements for the latest quarterly or semi-annual 

business period of the relevant business year; and, 

ii) Audit reports of the designated auditor on the financial statements in i) above. 

c) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements and the auditor’s review reports   

thereof for the relevant business year; 

d) In cases where applying for the requirement of [§28(1)2(b)(iii)] of the Regulation, following   

additional documents: 
i) Individual and consolidated financial statements for the business year prior to the latest 

business year; and, 

ii) Auditor’s audit reports on the financial statements in i) above. 

(3) A certified copy of the corporate register   
(4) Articles of incorporation 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(5) Shareholders’ register as of the end of the latest business year (in cases where the register is 
closed after the end of the latest business year, it shall be as of the closing date; the same shall 
apply hereinafter) 

(6) A copy of the agreement for transfer agent services entered into with a transfer agent (hereinafter 

referred to as the “transfer agreement”)   
(7) Following documents on mandatory holding: 

a) Written confirmation on mandatory holding by person subject to mandatory holding; and 
b)  Documents  issued  by  the  KSD  to  certify  the  mandatory  holding  by  the  person  subject  to 

mandatory holding 

(8) Certification on issuance and registration 
(9) A copy of the minutes of the board of directors on the approval for listing 
(10)  Documents  separately  determined  by  the  Exchange  in  relation  with  the  review  of  internal 

control conducted by the listing sponsor 
(11) Opinion letter of the main creditor bank 
(12) Written confirmation on the status of investments of stakeholders 
(13)  Written  confirmation  on  the  non-existence  of  parties  in  special  relationship,  including  the 

affiliates 

(14) Documents proving the completion of an education course operated by the Exchange for the 

support of listing. However, this may be exempted for a large corporation. 

(15) Annual report of the previous business year or the documents equivalent thereof, in the case of 

an  applicant  for  listing  which  satisfies  the  share  distribution  requirements  pursuant  to 
[§28(1)1(c)] of the Regulation 

(16) Following additional documents in the case of a foreign holdings company in Korea: 

a) Consolidated financial statements and auditor’s audit reports thereof for the latest business 

year that include all the foreign affiliates; 

b) Latest quarterly or semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements and auditor’s   

review reports thereof for the relevant business year; 

c) Foreign affiliates’ individual and consolidated financial statements and audit reports thereof; 

and 

d) Written report on the operation of internal accounting management system of foreign affiliates 

in [Annex Form No. 34] pursuant to [§20(1)] of the Enforcement Rules. 

(17) Following additional documents in the case of a venture company: 

a)  Venture company  pursuant to  [§2(1)38(a) or  §2(1)38(b)]  of the  Regulation: Certificate  for 
venture company issued pursuant to [§25] of the Act on Special Measures for Promotion of 
Venture Businesses; and 

b)  Venture  company  pursuant  to  [§2(1)38(c)]  of  the  Regulation:  Certificate  for  technical 
innovation-oriented small and medium enterprises issued pursuant to [§13] of the Enforcement 
Decree of the Act on Technology Innovation of Small and Medium Enterprises. 

(18) Following additional documents in the case of a technology growth company: 

a) Innovative technology company: Following documents:   

i) Cases where a specialized assessment institution has taken an assessment pursuant to 

[§28(1)1(a)(iii)] of the Enforcement Rules: Marketability statement in [Annex Form No. 9]   

and a recommendation letter from the designated advisor in [Annex Form No. 11]; and 

ii) Other cases: Marketability statement in [Annex Form No. 9]. 
b) Business model company: Business model company evaluation report in [Annex Form No. 
10]. 

(19) Following additional documents in the case of a prompt-transfer company pursuant to [§31(1)]   

of Regulation: 
a) Prompt-transfer company pursuant to [§31(1)3(f) of the Regulation: Recommendation letter   
in [Annex Form No. 11] from the designated advisor and a report on corporate continuity in 
[Annex Form No. 10-2]; and 

b) Other cases: Recommendation letter in [Annex Form No. 11] from the designated advisor. 

(20) Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the preliminary listing review. 

Notes: 

(1) The financial statements in [(2)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  Financial  statements  refer  to  the  statement  of  financial  position,  income  statement  and 
comprehensive  income  statement,  cash  flow  statement,  statement  of  changes  in  equity,  and 
supplementary  schedules,  and  semi-annual  financial  statements  refer  to  semi-statement  of 
financial  position,  semi-annual  income  statement  and  semi-annual  comprehensive  income 
statement, and supplementary schedules; 

(b) Consolidated financial statements, quarterly and semi-annual consolidated financial statements 
and auditor’s audit and review reports thereof shall be submitted by those companies with a 
subsidiary only; 

(c) The documents referred to in [(2)a)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i)  In  cases  where  the  applicant’s  auditor  was  designated  by  the  Securities  and  Futures 
Commission pursuant to [§14(6)1] of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on External Audit 
of  Stock  Companies,  Etc.  the  auditor’s  audit  report  shall  refer  to  the  audit  report  of  the 
designated auditor; and 

(ii) In cases where the accounts are not closed for the latest business year, following documents 
may be submitted first and the documents referred to in [(2)a)] may be submitted after the 
account closing: 

a)  Individual  and  consolidated  financial  statements  of  the  business  year  prior  to  the  latest 
business year and auditor’s audit report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the audit opinion 
is unqualified; and 

b) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and 
the  auditor’s  review  report  thereof.  In  this  case,  it  is  limited  that  the  review  opinion  is 
unqualified. 

(iii) In cases where one business year has not been lapsed after the establishment or conversion 
of the foreign holdings company in Korea, the document in [(2)a)] may be replaced by the 
statement of financial position as of the establishment or conversion and written confirmation 
of review thereof.   

(d)  In  cases  where  the  listing  applicant  submitting  the  documents  pursuant  to  [(2)b)]  has  not 
prepared the individual and consolidated financial statements in accordance with the K-IFRS 
for  the  latest  business  year,  the  individual  and  consolidated  financial  statements  shall  be 

 
prepared in accordance with the K-IFRS for the latest business year and the auditor’s or the 
designated auditor’s audit report shall be submitted additionally. 

(e) Those documents referred to in [(2)c)] may not be submitted in a case which falls under any of 

the followings: 

(i) In cases where it has not been 45 days since the end of the semi-annual business period of the 

relevant business year; or 

(ii) In cases where the listing applicant submitted the semi-annual or the third quarter individual 

and consolidated financial statements and the designated auditor’s audit report thereof. 

(2) The documents in [(7)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  In  cases  where  the  listing  applicant  falls  under  any  of  the  subparagraphs  in  [§32(2)]  of  the 

Regulation, the documents in [(7)] may not be submitted; 

(b) The documents in [(7)a)] shall state the matters as follows: 

(i)A statement that the person subject to mandatory holding of the shares, etc. will hold the shares, 
etc. for the mandatory holding period and will not withdraw or establish or remove the right of 
pledge on the shares, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary. 

(ii)The method of disclosure in case where there occurs an event of accounts transfer, establishment 
and removal of a right of pledge, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. held by the person 
subject  to  mandatory  holding  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  and  the  method  of 
handling  the  case  where  the  mandatory  holding  is  impossible  because  the  shares,  etc.  are 
provided security, etc. 

(iii)A statement that the applicant will not raise any objection against the disclosure by the 

listing sponsor as to the fact where, during the period of mandatory holding, the person 

subject to mandatory holding makes accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a right 

of pledge, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. 

(c)The documents referred to in [(7)b)] may be submitted within three days (based on business days) 

after the day of notice of the result of the preliminary listing review. 

(3) The documents in [(8)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  In  cases  where  the  shares,  etc.  issued  by  the  listing  applicant  have  not  been  electronically 
registered, the certification on issuance and registration in [(8)] may be temporarily replaced by 
specimens of all denominations of the stock certificate, a document issued by a transfer agent to 
certify the issuance of share certificate, or a certificate of entry into the depositor’s account book. 

(b) The listing applicant who makes a primary offering or secondary distribution of shares after 

filing the application for preliminary listing review may submit the certification on issuance and   

registration in [(8)] within 20 days after submitting the initial listing application. 

 
 
 
(4) The documents in [(15)] may be submitted after the closing of accounts in a case where the account 

are not closed for the latest business year. 

(5) The documents in [(16)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a) The documents in [(16)b)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i) In cases where it has not been 45 days since the end of the quarterly or semi-annual period of 

the relevant business year, the documents in [(16)b)] may not be submitted. 

(ii) In cases where the Exchange deems it necessary considering the establishment place,   

accounting environment, history of listing on a foreign exchange, etc., the documents in [(16)b)] 
shall be replaced by quarterly or semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements 

and auditor’s audit report thereof. 

(b) The documents in [(16)c and d)] may not be submitted in the cases of a foreign subsidiary that 
falls under any of each    subparagraph of [§20(2)].(c) Of the documents in [(16)d)], written 
report on the operation of internal accounting management system shall describe the operation 
of internal accounting management system for the period of at least three months prior to the 
preliminary listing review application 

(b) Foreign stocks, etc. (excluding different classes of foreign stocks) 

(1) Application for preliminary listing review separately determined by the Exchange 
(2) Financial documents for an applicant for initial listing 

a) Individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and auditor’s audit   

reports thereof 

b) Individual and consolidated financial statements for the latest quarterly or semi-annual 
business period of the relevant business year and the auditor’s review reports thereof 

(3) Written report on the operation of internal accounting management system in [Annex Form No. 

34] pursuant to [§20(1)] of the Enforcement Rules 

(4) Shareholders’ register as of the end of the latest business year (in cases where the register is 
closed after the end of business year, it shall be as of the date of the closure; the same shall apply 
hereinafter) 

(5) Written confirmation on mandatory holding by person subject to mandatory holding 
(6) Articles of incorporation which reflects the matters required to be entered into pursuant to [Annex 

Form No. 12] 

(7) A certified copy of the corporate register   
(8) A copy of the minutes of the board of directors on the approval for listing 
(9) Written confirmation on the status of investments of stakeholders 
(10)  Written  confirmation  on  the  non-existence  of  parties  in  special  relationship,  including  the 

affiliates 

(11) Certification on issuance and registration 

 
 
 
(12) A copy of the agency agreement entered into with a transfer agent for the matters such as the 

methods of exercising the rights of beneficial shareholders

[Annex Form No. 36]
