a) Documents proving that the applicant is listed on the foreign exchange 
b) Documents proving the trading activities for the latest one (1) year at the listed foreign 

securities markets 

(21) Following additional documents in the case of a foreign holdings company: 

a) Consolidated financial statements and auditor’s audit reports thereof which include all the 

foreign affiliates 

b) Individual and consolidated financial statements of foreign affiliates and audit reports thereof 
c) Written report on the operation of internal accounting management system of foreign affiliates 

in [Annex Form No. 34] pursuant to[§20(1)] of the Enforcement Rules 

d) Certified copies of the corporate register of foreign affiliates 

(22) Other documents the Exchange deems necessary for the preliminary listing review. 

Notes: 

(1) The financial statements in [(2)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  Financial  statements  refer  to  statement  of  financial  position,  income  statement  and 
comprehensive  income  statement,  cash  flow  statement,  statement  of  changes  in  equity,  and 
supplementary schedules, and semi-annual financial statements refer to semi-annual statement 
of  financial  position,  semi-annual  income  statement  and  semi-annual  comprehensive  income 
statement, and supplementary schedules. 

(b) Consolidated financial statements, quarterly and semi-annual consolidated financial statements 
and auditor’s audit and review reports thereof shall be submitted only by those companies with a 
subsidiary.  However,  in  a  case  where  the  listing  applicant  adopted  IFRS  or  US  GAAP,  the 
applicant shall submit consolidated financial statements, quarterly and semi-annual consolidated 
financial statements and auditor’s audit and review reports thereof. 

(c) The documents in [(2)a]] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i) In cases where the accounts are not closed for the latest business year, following documents 
may  be  submitted  first  and  the  documents  referred  to  in][(2)a)]  may  be  submitted  after  the 

 
 
account closing. 

a)  Individual  and  consolidated  financial  statements  of  the  business  year  prior  to  the  latest 
business year and auditor’s audit report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the audit opinion 
shall be unqualified. 

          b) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and 
the auditor’s review report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the review opinion shall be 
unqualified. 

(ii) In cases where one business year has not been lapsed after the establishment or conversion of 
the foreign holdings company, the documents are replaced by the statement of financial position 
as of the establishment or conversion and written confirmation of audit review thereof. 

(d) Documents in][(2)b)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i) In cases where it has not been 45 days since the end of the quarterly or semi-annual business 

period of the relevant business year, the documents in [(2)b]] may not be submitted. 

(ii)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  considering  the  establishment  place, 
accounting environment, history of listing on a foreign exchange, etc., the documents in][(2)b)] 
shall be replaced by quarterly or semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements 

and auditor’s audit report thereof 

(2) Of the documents in [(3)], the written report on the operation of internal accounting management 
system shall describe the operation of internal accounting management system for the period of at least 
three months prior to the preliminary listing review application. 

(3) The documents in [(5)] shall state the matters as follows: 

(a) A statement that the person subject to mandatory holding of the shares, etc. will hold the shares, 
etc. for the mandatory holding period and will not withdraw or establish or remove the right of 
pledge on the shares, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary. 

(b) The method of disclosure in case where there occurs an event of accounts transfer, establishment 
and removal of a right of pledge, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. held by the person 
subject  to  mandatory  holding  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  and  the  method  of 
handling  the  case  where  the  mandatory  holding  is  impossible  because  the  shares,  etc.  are 
provided security, etc. 

(c) A statement that the applicant will not raise any objection against the disclosure by the listing 
sponsor  as  to  the  fact  where,  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  the  person  subject  to 
mandatory  holding  makes  accounts  transfer,  establishment  and  removal  of  a  right  of  pledge, 
sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. 

(4) In cases where it is impossible to submit the document in [(7)] due to the laws of the home country, 
it may be replaced by a document proving the fact. 

 
 
 
 
(5) The documents in [(11)] shall be based on the following standards: 

  (a)  In  cases  where  the  shares,  etc.  issued  by  the  listing  applicant  have  not  been  electronically 
registered, the certification on issuance and registration in [(11)] may be temporarily replaced 
by specimens of all denominations of the stock certificate, a document issued by a transfer agent 
to certify the issuance of share certificate, or a certificate of entry into the depositor’s account 
book. 

(b) The listing applicant who makes a primary offering or secondary distribution of shares after filing 
the  application  for  preliminary  listing  review  may  submit  the  certification  on  issuance  and 
registration in [(11)] within 20 days after submitting the initial listing application. 

(6) The documents in [(12)] may be submitted at the time of application of the initial listing in the case 
where  the  listing  applicant  makes  the  primary  offering  or  the  secondary  distribution  after  the 
application of the preliminary listing review. 

(7) The documents in [(21)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  The  documents  ]n  [(21]a)  and  b)]  may  not  be  submitted  in  cases  where  the  foreign  holdings 

company adopted IFRS or US GAAP. 

(b) The documents ]n [(21)b) and c)] may not be submitted in cases of a foreign subsidiary that falls 

under any of each subparagraphs of [§20(2)]. 

(c)  Of  the  documents  in  [(21)c)],  the  written  report  on  the  operation  of  internal  accounting 
management system shall describe the operation of internal accounting management system for 
the period of at least three months prior to the preliminary listing review application. 

(d) In cases where it is impossible to submit the document referred to in [(21)d)] due to the laws of 

the home country, it may be replaced by a document proving the fact.

to

Notes: 

(1) The financial statements in [(2)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a) Financial statements refer to statement of financial position, income statement and comprehensive 
income  statement,  cash  flow  statement,  statement  of  changes  in  equity,  and  supplementary 
schedules,  and  semi-annual  financial  statements  refer  to  semi-annual  statement  of  financial 
position, semi-annual income statement and semi-annual comprehensive income statement, and 
supplementary schedules. 

(b) Consolidated financial statements, semi-annual consolidated financial statements, and auditor’s 

audit or review reports thereof shall be submitted only by companies with subsidiaries. 

(c) The documents referred to in [(2)a)] shall be based on the following standards: 

i) In cases where the applicant’s auditor was designated by the Securities and Futures Commission 
pursuant  to  [§14(6)1]  of  the  Enforcement  Decree  of  the  Act  on  External  Audit  of  Stock 
Companies, Etc. the auditor’s audit report shall refer to the audit report of the designated auditor. 

ii) In cases where the closing of accounts is not finalized for the latest business year, following 
documents may be submitted first and the documents referred to in [(2)a)] may be submitted 
after the account closing. 

a) Individual and consolidated financial statements of the business year prior to the latest   

business year and auditor’s audit report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the audit   

opinion shall be unqualified. 

b) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and 
the auditor’s review report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the review opinion shall be 
unqualified. 

(d) In cases where the listing applicant submitting the documents pursuant to [(2)b)] has not prepared 
the individual and consolidated financial statements in accordance with the K-IFRS for the latest 

 
 
business  year,  the  individual  and  consolidated  financial  statements  shall  be  prepared  in 
accordance  with  the  K-IFRS  for  the  latest  business  year  and  the  auditor’s  or  the  designated 
auditor’s audit report shall be submitted additionally. 

(e)Documents in [(2)c)] may not be submitted in the case that falls under any of the followings: 

i) In cases where it has not been 45 days since the end of the semi-annual business period of the 

relevant business year; or 

ii) In cases where the listing applicant submitted the semi-annual or the third quarter individual 

and consolidated financial statements and the designated auditor’s audit report thereof. 

(2) The documents referred to in [(4)b)] may be submitted within three (3) days (based on business days) 

after the day of notice of the result of the preliminary listing review. 

(5)  The documents mentioned in (15) and (16) shall be submitted only when applying for  eligibility 

review for listing after merger pursuant to [§2(1)1(f)(ii)] of the Regulation. 

(6)  The  document  in  (15)  may  be  temporarily  replaced  with  the  specimens  of  the  issued  stock 
certificates  (referring  to  standardized  securities  pursuant  to  the  Regulation  on  Handling 
Standardized  Securities,  etc.;  the  same  shall  apply  hereinafter),  or  a  document  issued  by  the 
transfer agency to prove the issuance of stock certificates or a certificate of entry into depositor’s 
account book in cases where the stocks issued by a listing applicant have not been electronically 
registered. In such cases, the certificate of issuance and registration may be submitted by the date 
of application for listing after merger. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex No. 2] Documents for Application for Initial Listing   
(Amended on March 16, 2026) 

Documents for Application for Initial Listing 

(Pertaining to [§25, §64, §70, §77, §81] §82-2], and §82-6] of the Enforcement Rules) 

1. Common stocks, different classes of stocks, stocks of a special purpose acquisition company 

(1) Application for initial listing in [Annex Form No. 3] 
(2) Documents for application for preliminary listing review in [Annex No. 1] 
(3) Certificate on issuance and registration 

(4) Documents issued by the KSD to prove mandatory holding by the person subject to mandatory   

holding 

(5) Listing agreement 
(6) Written affirmation on the fulfillment of obligations   
(7) Summary tables of shareholders or details of subscription and allotment of shares 
(8) Written confirmation relating to IR conference 
(9) Written affirmation on mandatory holding of stocks, etc. by listing sponsor and documents   

Issued by the KSD proving the mandatory holding in accordance with [§13(5) & §26(1)5] of   
the Regulation 

(10) Documents proving the payment of subscription of stocks 
(11) In the case of a special purpose acquisition company, following additional documents: 

a) Written confirmation on funds’  deposit and trust issued by deposit institutions, etc. (refers to 
the institutions publicly notified by the Financial Services Commission pursuant to [§1-4-2(2)] 
of the Regulations on Financial Investment Business) for the funds deposited or trusted 
b) Written confirmation of the total amount of issuance of the shares, etc. owned by financial 
investment companies pursuant to [§6(4)14(c)] of the Enforcement Decree of the Act 
(12) Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the preliminary listing review. 

Notes: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(1) The documents in [(3)] may be submitted within 20 days after the date of submitting the application 
for initial listing in the case of a listing applicant who makes the primary offering or the secondary 
distribution after the application of preliminary listing review. 

(2) The documents in [(iv)] means the certification of mandatory holding issued by the KSD as to the 
mandatory holding of stocks, etc. for which electronic registration has completed pursuant to the 
Act  on  Electronic  Registration  of  Stocks,  Corporate  Bonds,  etc.  However,  in  a  case  where  the 
securities are not subject to electronic registration pursuant to [§25(1)] of the Act on Electronic 
Registration  of  Stocks,  Corporate  Bonds,  etc.,  the  documents  shall  be  replaced  by  a  certificate 
issued by the KSD to prove the custody of concerned stocks, etc. 

(3)  In  cases  where  deemed  inevitable  by  the  Exchange,  those  documents  in  [(4)  to  (12)]  may  be 

submitted by the day immediately prior to the date of initial listing. 

(4) The documents in [(8)] shall not be submitted in the case where the listing applicant is a special 

purpose acquisition company. 

(5) The documents in [(10)] shall be submitted only in a case where the company made the primary 

offering or the secondary distribution after the application of preliminary listing review.

securities are not subject to electronic registration pursuant to [§25(1)] of the Act on Electronic 
Registration  of  Stocks,  Corporate  Bonds,  Etc.,  the  documents  shall  be  replaced  by  a  certificate 
issued by the KSD to prove the custody of concerned stocks, etc. 

(3) In cases where deemed inevitable by the Exchange, documents in [(4) to (14)] may be submitted by 

the day immediately prior to the date of initial listing. 

(4) The documents in [(10)] shall be submitted only in a case where the company made the primary 

offering or the secondary distribution after the application of preliminary listing review. 

(5) The documents in [(13)] shall be replaced by a document proving the fact in the case where the 

submission of the document is impossible due to the laws of the home country. 

3. Subscription warrants 

(1) Application for initial listing in [Annex Form No. 38] 
(2) Certificate on issuance and registration 
(3) A certified copy of the corporate register   

(4) Other documents the Exchange deems necessary   

4. Subscription rights 

(1) Application for initial listing in [Annex Form No. 39] 
(2) A copy of the minutes of the board of directors on the resolution for the issuance of new shares 
(3) Form of the subscription rights 
(4) Certificate on issuance and registration 
(5) Other documents the Exchange deems necessary   

5.  Business  development  investment  company  stocks  land  business  development  investment  trust 

beneficiary certificates 

(1) Application for initial listing separately determined by the Exchange 
(2) Application documents for preliminary listing review under [Annex No. 1] 
(3) Certificates on issuance and registration 
(4) Documents proving registration with the Financial Services Commission 
(5) Prospectus 
(6) Listing agreement under [Annex No. 4] 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(7) Documents proving payment of share capital or trust principal, etc. 
(8) Written confirmation on mandatory holding under [Annex No. 12] 
(9) Other documents the Exchange deems necessary for the listing review 

 
 
[Annex No. 2-2] Application Documents for Listing after Merger   
[February 14, 2022] (Amended on December 9, 2022) 

Application Documents for Listing after Merger 

(Pertaining to [§75] of the Enforcement Rules) 

(1) Listing Application in [Annex Form No. 3] 
(2) Documents for Application for preliminary listing review in [Annex No. 1] 
(3) Certificate of issuance and registration 
(4)  A  document  issued  by  the  KSD  to  prove  the  mandatory  holding  of  the  person  subject  to 

mandatory holding 

(5) Listing contract 
(6) Indemnity report on fulfillment of obligations 
(7)    A certified copy of the registration of incorporation 
(8) Schedule for issuance of new stocks 
(9) Minutes of general meetings of shareholders   
(10) A copy of transfer agency service contract 
(11 Summary Table of Shareholders in [Annex Form No. 30] 
(12) Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for listing review.   

Notes: 

(1) The document in (4) shall refer to the mandatory holding certificate issued by the Korea Securities 
Depository concerning the mandatory holding of stocks, etc., which have been electronically registered 
pursuant to the Act on Electronic Registration of Stocks, Bonds, etc. Provided that, in cases where the 
stocks, etc. are not subject to electronic registration pursuant to Article 25(1) of the Act on Electronic 
Registration of Stocks, Bonds, etc., a certificate issued by the Korea Securities Depository may be in 
substitution for the mandatory holding certificate to prove the deposit of the relevant stocks, etc. 

(2) The documents in (4) through (12) may be submitted by the day before the listing after merger in 
cases where the Exchange deems it unavoidable. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex No. 3]    Documents for Backdoor Listing Review   
(Amended on March 9, 2023) 

Documents for Backdoor Listing Review 

(Pertaining to [§32]) 

(1) Report on backdoor listing separately determined by the Exchange 
(2) Financial documents for the backdoor listing target company 

a) Individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year and auditor’s audit 

reports thereof. 

            b)  Following  additional  documents  in  cases  where  the  auditor  was  designated  during  the 

relevant   

business year pursuant to [§14(6)1] of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on External Audit 
of Stock Companies, Etc. 
i)  Individual  and  consolidated  financial  statements  for  the  latest  quarterly  or  semi-annual 

business period of the relevant business year, and, 

ii) Audit reports of the designated auditor on the financial statements of ① 

c) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements of the relevant business and the 

auditor’s review reports thereof. However, in the case where the backdoor listing target 
company is a foreign company, the latest quarterly or semi-annual individual and 
consolidated financial statements for the current relevant business year and the auditor’s 
review reports thereof shall be submitted. 

(3) A certified copy of the corporate register of the backdoor listing target company 
(4)  Articles  of  incorporation  of  the  backdoor  listing  target  company  (In  the  case  of  a  foreign 
company, it shall reflect the matters required to be entered into the articles of incorporation in 
accordance with [Annex No. 12] 

(5) Shareholders’ register of the backdoor listing target company as of the end of the latest business 
year (in cases where the register is closed after the end of business year, it shall be as of the date 
of the closure; the same shall apply hereinafter) 

(6) A  copy  of  the  agreement  for  transfer  agent  services  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  the  “transfer 

contract)that the backdoor listing target company entered into with a transfer agent 

(7) Following documents on mandatory holding: 

a) Written confirmation on mandatory holding by person subject to mandatory holding; and 
b)  Documents  issued  by  the  KSD  to  certify  the  mandatory  holding  by  the  persons  subject  to 

mandatory holding. 

(8) Certification on issuance and registration of the backdoor listing target company 
(9) A copy of the minutes of the board of directors of the backdoor listing target company on the 

approval for listing 

 
 
 
 
(10)  Documents  separately  determined  by  the  Exchange  in  relation  with  the  review  of  internal 

control of the backdoor listing target company conducted by the listing sponsor   

(11) Opinion letter of the main creditor bank of the backdoor listing target company 

(12) Written confirmation on the status of investments by stakeholders of the backdoor listing target 

company 

(13)  Written  confirmation  on  the  non-existence  of  parties  in  special  relationship,  including  the 

affiliates, of backdoor listing target company 

(14) Documents proving that the backdoor listing target company completed an education course 
operated by the Exchange for the support of listing. However, this may be exempted for a large 
corporation 

(15)  Following  additional documents  in  the  case  where  the  backdoor  listing target  company  is  a 

foreign holding company located in Korea: 

a) Consolidated financial statements that include all the foreign affiliates for the latest business 

year and auditor’s audit reports thereof; 

b) Quarterly and semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements for the relevant 
business year and the auditor’s review reports thereof. However, this applies only in the 
case where 45 days has lapsed after the end of the quarterly or semi-annual business 
period; 

c) Individual and consolidated financial statements of foreign affiliates and audit reports thereof; 

and 

d) Written report on the operation of internal accounting management system of foreign affiliates 

in [Annex Form No. 34]. 

(16)  Following  additional documents  in  the  case  where  the  backdoor  listing target  company  is a 

venture company: 

a) Venture company pursuant to [§2(1)38(a) or §2(1)38(b)] of the Regulation: Venture 
company certificate issued pursuant to [§25] of the Act on Special Measures for the Promotion 
of Venture Businesses; and 
b) Venture company pursuant to [§2(1)38(c)] of the Regulation: Certificate for technical 
innovation-oriented small and medium enterprises issued pursuant to [§13] of the Enforcement 
Decree of the Act on Technology Innovation of Small and Medium Enterprises. 

(17)  Following  additional  documents  in  the  case  where  the  backdoor  listing  target  company  is  a 

foreign company: 
a) Written report on the operation of internal accounting management system pursuant to [Annex 

Form No. 34]; 

b) A copy of the agency agreement entered into with a transfer agent for the matters such as the 

methods of exercising the rights of beneficial shareholders; 
c) A copy of the agreement for appointment of the listing agent; 
d) Lawyer’s legal opinion; 
e) Comfort letter of auditor in [Annex Form No. 35]; 
f) Written affirmation on fulfillment of obligations by the representative director in [Annex Form   

No. 36]; and 

g) In the case of a foreign company listed on a foreign securities market, documents proving   
that the company is listed on the foreign exchange and documents proving the trading   

 
activities for the latest one (1) year at the listed foreign exchange. 

(18)  Following  additional  documents  in  the  case  where  the  backdoor  listing  target  company  is  a 

foreign holdings company: 
a) Consolidated financial statements that include all the foreign affiliates and auditor’s audit   

reports thereof; 

b) Individual and consolidated financial statements of foreign affiliates and audit reports thereof; 
    and 
c) Internal accounting management system operation report of [Annex Form No. 34] for 

foreign subsidiary; and 

d) A certified copy of the corporate register of the foreign affiliates. However, this may be   
replaced by a document proving the fact in cases where it is impossible to submit the   
document due to the laws of the home country. 

(19) Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the preliminary listing review 

Notes: 

(1) The financial statements in [(2)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a)  Financial  statements  refer  to  statement  of  financial  position,  income  statement  and 
comprehensive  income  statement,  cash  flow  statement,  statement  of  changes  in  equity,  and 
supplementary schedules, and semi-annual financial statements refer to semi-annual statement of 
financial position, semi-annual income statement and semi-annual comprehensive income statement, 
and supplementary schedules. 

(b) Consolidated financial statements, quarterly and semi-annual consolidated financial statements 
and  auditor’s  audit  and  review  reports  thereof  shall  be  submitted  by  only  backdoor  listing 
target companies with subsidiaries. However, in  the case where the backdoor listing target 
company is a foreign company that adopted IFRS or US GAAP, the applicant shall submit only 
consolidated  financial  statements,  quarterly  and  semi-annual  consolidated  financial 
statements, and auditor’s audit and review reports thereof. 

(c) The documents in [(2)a)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i) In cases where the auditor was designated by the Securities and Futures Commission pursuant 
to [§14(6)1] of the Enforcement Decree of the Act on External Audit of Stock Companies, Etc. 
the auditor’s audit report shall refer to the audit report of the designated auditor; and 

(ii) In cases where the closing of accounts is not finalized for the latest business year, following 
documents  may  be  submitted  first  and  the  documents  in  [(2)a)]  may  be  submitted  after  the 
account closing; 

            a) Individual and consolidated financial statements of the business year prior to the latest 
business year and auditor’s audit report thereof. In this case, it is limited that the audit opinion 
is unqualified; and 

            b) Semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements of the latest business year 
and the auditor’s review report thereof. In this case,  it is limited that the review opinion  is 
unqualified. 

(d) In cases where the backdoor listing target company submitting the documents pursuant to [(2)b)] 
has not prepared the individual and consolidated financial statements in accordance with the K-

 
 
IFRS for the latest business year, the individual and consolidated financial statements shall be 
prepared  in  accordance  with  the  K-IFRS  for  the  latest  business  year  and  the  auditor’s  or  the 
designated auditor’s audit report shall be submitted additionally. 

(e) The documents in [(2)c)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(i) In cases where it falls under any of the followings, the documents referred to in [(2)c)] may not 
be submitted:   

            a)  In  cases  where  it  has  not  been  45  days  since  the  end  of  the  semi-annual  or  quarterly 
business period of the relevant business year (limited to the case where the backdoor listing 
target company is a foreign company); or 

            b) In cases where the backdoor listing target company submitted the semi-annual or third 
quarter individual and consolidated financial statements and the designated auditor’s audit 
report thereof. 

(ii) In cases where the backdoor listing target company is a foreign company and the Exchange 
deems  it  necessary  considering  the  establishment  place,  accounting  environment,  history  of 

listing on a foreign securities market, etc., the applicant shall submit auditor’s audit report of 

quarterly or semi-annual individual and consolidated financial statements. In this case, it is 
limited that the relevant audit opinion is unqualified. 

(2) The documents in [(3)] may be replaced by a document proving the fact in cases where the backdoor 
listing target company which is a foreign company is not possible to submit the documents due to 
the laws of the home country. 

(3) The documents in [(7)a)] shall include the following matters: 

(a) A statement that the person subject to mandatory holding of the shares, etc. will continue to hold 
the shares, etc. for the mandatory holding period and will not withdraw or establish or remove the 
right of pledge on the shares, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary; 

(b) Method of disclosure in case where there occurs an event of accounts transfer, establishment and 
removal of a right of pledge, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. held by the person subject to 
mandatory  holding  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  and  method  of  handling  the  cases 
where it is impossible to make the mandatory holding because the shares, etc. are provided security, 
etc.; and 

(c) A statement that the applicant will not raise any objection against the disclosure by the listing 
sponsor  as  to  the  fact  where,  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  the  person  subject  to 
mandatory holding makes accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a right of pledge, sales, 
withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. 

(4) The documents in [(8)] may, in cases where the shares, etc. issued by the backdoor listing target 
company  have  not  been  electronically  registered,  be  temporarily  replaced  by  specimens  of  all 
denominations of the stock certificate issued (refers to the uniform stock certificate prescribed in 
the Securities Handling Regulations; the same shall apply hereinafter) and a document issued by a 
transfer agent to certify the issuance of share certificate, or a certificate of entry into the depositor’s 

 
 
 
account book. 

(5) The documents in [(15)] shall be based on the following standards: 

(a) The documents in [(15)a)] shall be the statement of financial position and the auditor’s review 

report thereof as of the establishment or conversion into a holdings company in cases where the 
company is a foreign holding company located in Korea with business operation history less than 
one (1) business year after the establishment or conversion; 

(b) In cases where the Exchange deems it necessary considering the company’s establishment place, 

accounting environment, history of listing on a foreign exchange, etc., the documents in [(15)b)] 

shall include the auditor’s audit report on the quarterly and semi-annual consolidated financial 

statements; and 

(c) The documents in [(15)c) and d)] may not be submitted in cases of a foreign subsidiary that falls 

under any of subparagraphs of [§20(2)]. 

(6) The documents in [(18)b) and c)] may not be submitted in cases of a foreign subsidiary that falls 

under any of subparagraphs of [§20(2)].

of the Enforcement Rules)

etc.:

the fact in the case of a paid-in capital increase through the third party allotment.

(9) In the case of listing change or supplementary listing due to a change of company name, stock 

split, merger, etc., documents proving such event 

(10) Following additional documents in the case of a special purpose acquisition company’s issuance

(b) Written confirmation of the total amount of issuance of the shares, etc. owned by financial 

investment companies   

(11) Other documents that the Exchange deems necessary for the listing review 

Notes: 

(1) The documents for the application for listing change or supplementary listing shall be submitted 
with  the  Exchange  five  (5)  trading  days  prior  to  the  scheduled  date  of  listing  change  and 
supplementary listing. However, documents that fall under any of the followings shall be submitted 
by the day prescribed below: 

(a) Documents in [(3)]: The application for the issuance of the document can be submitted first and 

then, the concerned document shall immediately be submitted as soon as prepared; 

(b)  Documents  in  [4)]:  Within  20  days  after  the  date  of  the  application  for  listing  change  or 

supplementary listing; 

(c)  Documents  in  [(6)]:  By  the  previous  day  of  the  date  of  the  application  for  listing  change  or 

 
 
 
 
supplementary listing; and 

(d) Documents in [(7) and (10)]: Without delay after completion of the subscription payment. 

(2) The documents in [(2)] shall follow the followings: 

    (a)  Where  the  same  document  is  submitted  in  the  disclosure  related  to  the  listing  change  and 

supplementary listing, the documents referred to in [(2)] may not be submitted; 

    (b) If the document in [(2)] was corrected, only the final document may be submitted; and 

    (c) Only the part related to the application for the listing change and supplementary listing among 

the documents in [(2)] may be separately submitted.   

(3) Only the part related to the application for the listing change and supplementary listing among the 

documents in [(3)] may be separately submitted. 

(4) Documents in [(5)] shall be submitted only when mandatory holding under this Regulation, etc. 

applies. In such case, the documents in [(5)] shall state the following matters: 

(a) A statement that the person subject to mandatory holding of the shares, etc. will continue to hold 
the shares, etc. for the mandatory holding period and will not withdraw or establish or remove 
the right of pledge on the shares, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary; 

(b) Method of disclosure in case where there occurs an event of accounts transfer, establishment and 
removal of a right of pledge, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the shares, etc. held by the person subject 
to mandatory holding during the period of mandatory holding, and method of handling the cases 
where  it  is  impossible  to  make  the  mandatory  holding  because  the  shares,  etc.  are  provided 
security, etc.; and 

(c) A statement that the applicant will not raise any objection against the disclosure by the listing 
sponsor  as  to  the  fact  where,  during  the  period  of  mandatory  holding,  the  person  subject  to 
mandatory holding makes accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a right of pledge, sales, 
withdrawal, etc. 

(5) The documents in [(7)(b)] shall follow the followings: 

(a) Among Documents in [(7)b], the details of use of the funds refers to the use details, plan, etc. of 
the funds raised through the concerned paid-in capital increase. In this case, if there are pre-paid 
payment,  provisional  payment,  lending  of  money,  lending  of  securities,  investment  of  equity 
capital (including the acquisition of stocks, etc. or equity certificates issued by other company) 
for those who acquired the new shares through the paid-in capital increase through the allotment 
to a third party, the details and the plan shall be included.   

(b) The KOSDAQ-listed corporation that belongs to the premier company category as of the date of 

issuance of the new shares may not submit the documents in [(7)b)]. 

(6) The documents in [(8)] shall be submitted only in cases where there is a change of capital such as 

capital reduction and reverse stock split. 

(7) As  a  case  of  issuing  securities  overseas  to  those  other  than  residents  (excluding  the  investment 
dealing companies acquiring the concerned securities through an underwriting agreement relating 
to the issuance of the securities) pursuant to the Foreign Exchange Transaction Act, in the case of 
applying  for  listing  of  new  share  that  are  issued  by  the  exercise  of  rights  on  conversion  rights, 
subscription right, etc. which are attached to the securities or issued as underlying securities, in the 
case  where  the  relevant  securities  are  DRs,  within  one  (1)  year  after  the  issuance,  following 

documents shall be submitted in addition:   

(a)In  cases  of  exemption  of  securities  registration  or  exemption  of  submission  of  securities 

registration, documents confirming the fact; and,   

(b) Documents proving the mandatory holding that the shares shall not be subject to sales, accounts 
transfer, establishment and removal of pledge, withdrawal, etc. unless the Exchange deems it 

necessary  pursuant  to  [§16]  of  the  Regulation,  by  putting  the  new  shares  under  mandatory 

holding  with  the  KSD,  which  are  issued  through  exercise  of  rights  on  conversion  right, 
subscription right, etc. attached to the relevant securities or issued as underlying securities in 
the case where the relevant securities are DRs, within one (1) year after the issuance,. 

(9) In cases of applying for listing change and supplementary listing of foreign stocks, etc. and foreign 

different classes of stocks, following standards are applied: 

(a) The documents in [(3)] means the documents on registration for the issuance of new shares. 
However, in cases where it is impossible to submit the document due to the laws of the home 
country, it can be replaced by written document proving the fact. 

(b) The documents in [(5) and (6)] may be replaced with the written confirmation of mandatory 

holding entered into the listing sponsor.

[Annex No. 6]    Qualitative Criteria for Preliminary Listing Review 
(Amended on September 27, 2022; December 28, 2023; July 9, 2025; November 24, 2025) 

Qualitative Criteria for Preliminary Listing Review 

(Pertaining to [§27]) 

1. Corporate sustainability   

Corporate sustainability shall be recognized in terms of business status, financial condition, technical 
capability, growth potential, and other management environments of a corporation. 

(a) Standard companies 

Review items 

Focal points for review 

 Industrial growth potential and trend such as industrial growth cycle, market 
size, competitive situation, entry barrier, etc.   
 Regulatory environment of industries at home and abroad, and effects of the 
government policy     
 Change factors of sales amount and profits of the past, and possibility of 
increase in sales and profits in the future   
 Possibility of maintaining business relationship with major customers and of 
securing new customers 
 Size of sale credit and inventory assets, and appropriateness of management 
system thereof 
 Level of financial stability compared to the industrial group and competing 
companies 
 Liquidity status considering the size and trend of cash flow from the business 
operation 
 Possibility of deterioration of financial status due to contingent liabilities 
 Technological competitiveness such as intellectual property, level of technical 
professionals, degree of technological perfection and competitive advantage   
 Competitiveness in commercialization of technology held or under 
development 
 Rationality of corporate growth strategy and business plan for growth 
  Possibility  of  expanding  business  by  strengthening  competitiveness  of  main 
products and entering new businesses 
Rationality of the use of funds raised by public offering and possibility of growth 
by the influx of funds 
 Impact that lawsuits or legal conflicts relating to patent, management right, 
etc., if any, may have on corporate management   
 Impact that management’s expertise such as level of experience and capital 
participation by management may have on corporate growth 

Business 
situations 

Financial 
conditions 

Technology 

Growth 
potential 

Other 
management 
environments 

 
 
 
 
(b) Companies with no realized profit   

Review items 

Focal points for review 

 Industrial growth potential and trend such as industrial growth cycle, market 
size, competitive situation, entry barrier, etc.   
 Regulatory environment of industries at home and abroad, and effects of the 
government policy     
 Size and trend of loss, and validity* of the cause of the loss 
* Losses caused by structural problems such as overall decrease in sales, or 

incurred in the process of growth for R&D, expansion of production facilities, 
etc. 

 Possibility of expansion of transactions with main customers, and possibility 
to turn profitable through securing new customers, etc. 
 Size of sale credit and inventory assets, and appropriateness of management 
system thereof 
 Level of financial stability compared to the industrial group and competing 
companies 
 Size of decrease in cash flow from losses and whether or not to secure 
liquidity considering the trend of future growth 
 Possibility of deterioration of financial status due to contingent liabilities 
 Differentiated business models compared to competitors and competitiveness 
of the business models (in the areas of production of services and products, sales 
distribution, etc.) 
 Corporate growth strategies and rationality of business strategy* for growth 
*Recruitment of personnel, planning of facility investment, securing of patent 

rights, etc. 

 Status of outside investors’ assessment of corporate growth potential and the 
basis for the assessment 

*Including status of financing from external investors 
  Possibility  of  expanding  business  by  strengthening  competitiveness  of  main 
products and entering new businesses 
Rationality of the purpose of use of funds (facility expansion, etc. to secure 
growth potential) and effect of influx of funds raised by public offering 
 Impacts that lawsuits or legal conflicts relating to patent, management right, 
etc. may have on corporate management   
 Influence of management’s expertise and capital participation on corporate 
growth 
 Whether the system for investor protection such as granting of put-back 
options is sufficient 

Business 
situations 

Financial 
conditions 

Growth 
potential 

Other 
management 
environments 

※  If the Exchange deems it necessary given the business structure of the companies-with-no-profit, it 

may be possible to apply both the qualitative criteria for standard companies and those for companies 
with no realized profit simultaneously. 

 
 
 
 
(c) Technology growth companies 

Review items 

Focal points for review 

 Industrial growth potential and trend such as industrial growth cycle, market 
size, competitive situation, entry barrier, etc.   
 Possibilities of entering or expanding existing markets and creating new 
markets 
 Possibilities of maintaining existing customers or securing new customers 
 Regulatory environment of industries at home and abroad, and effects of the 
government policy 
 Influence of internal competence such as management’s knowledge and 
experience on business continuity and future growth 
 Innovative technology companies1) 
 Completeness of technology including stage of development, self-reliance, 
difficulty of imitation, etc. 
 Competitive advantage in terms of technological differentiation, level R&D, 
size and appropriateness of R&D investment, status of possessing intellectual 
property rights, etc. 
 Level of technological workforce, such as technological expertise, 
technological management ability, etc.   
 Competitiveness in commercialization of technology 
 Business model companies 
 Completion of business models in terms of degree of commercialization, 
realization of sales, etc. 
 Competitive advantage in terms of differentiation of business models, 
position in the market, etc. 
 Whether human and material resources essential to business are secured 
 Rationality of business plans, including workforce and facility investment 
plans for corporate growth, securing intellectual property rights, etc. 
 Rationality of the purpose of use of funds raised by public offering and the 
effect of influx of the funds 
 Possibility of realizing revenue including sales and operating income within a 
certain period after listing 
 Impacts that lawsuits or legal conflicts relating to patent, management right, 
etc. may have on corporate management   
 Impact that the contingent liabilities arising from the terms of major contracts 
related to business operation, etc. may have on management 

Business 
situations 

Technology/ 
Business 
feasibility 

Growth 
potential 

Other 
management 
environments 

Notes: 

(1) In cases where the outcome of the assessment for a domestic company (excluding foreign holding 
company  located  in  Korea)  conducted  by  specialized  assessment  institutions  is  a  grade  of  ‘AA’  or 
above,  the  review  items  of  ‘Technology/Business  feasibility’  shall  not  apply  thereto.  In  such  cases, 
when the overall assessment grades submitted by the specialized assessment institutions are different 
from each other, the higher grade shall be the final assessment grade, but, in the case where even one 
assessment institution has rated ‘BBB’ or lower, the lower assessment grade shall be the final grade. 

※  If  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  considering  the  business  structure  of  the  technology  growth 

companies, it may be possible to apply both the qualitative criteria for ordinary companies and those 
for technology growth companies simultaneously. 

 
 
2. Transparency and stability of the business management   

Transparency  and  stability  of  the  business  management  shall  be  recognized  in  light  of  corporate 
governance, internal control system, disclosure system, trading with interested parties, stock trading 
before listing, etc. of a corporation. 

Review items 

Focal points for review 

Corporate 
governance 

Internal 
control system 

Corporate 
disclosure 

Trading with 
interested 
parties   

Stock trading 
before listing   

Management 
stability   

 Whether the decisions on important matters are made autonomously by 
establishing independent corporate governance structure. 
 In cases where there is an unlawful act by the management, the impact that such 
act may have on corporate management. 
 Whether there is a history of significant actions by the largest shareholder or the 
management that are against the interests of the listing applicant. 
 Level of establishment and operation of internal control system such as the 
regulation on the operation of the board of directors, etc.   
 Whether there are any important errors or unusual matters confirmed through 
accounting audit or tax investigation 
 In the case of a holding company, the appropriateness of establishment and 
operation of management systems of its subsidiaries with regard to appointment 
of executives, business performance reporting, conclusion of business 
management contract, etc. 
 Whether it has human resources, internal control procedures such as accounting 
regulations, etc. and accounting systems, established and operated to produce 
reliable accounting data. 
 Whether work force and organization are constructed in order to perform the 
disclosure duties stipulated in relevant laws and regulations (in case where the 
largest shareholder is a paper company, the disclosure duties relating to the 
material business matters of the paper company shall be included.) 
 Whether the disclosure system to prevent the usage of material undisclosed 
information is established. 
 Whether the background, conditions, procedures, etc. for trading with the 
interested parties comply with relevant laws and regulations. 
 Fairness of conditions of the trading with the interested parties compared to the 
trading with a third person   
 Possibility of infringing the interests of shareholders in light of the necessity of 
stock trading before listing, legality of procedures, appropriateness of trading 
price, etc. 
 Whether there is any trading using undisclosed information 
 Whether the largest shareholder, etc. (in the case of a paper company, a de facto 
controlling stockholder shall be included) holds stable amount of shares   
 In the case of technology growth companies, whether the stability of 
management is maintained until profit realization 
 If there are disputes over management rights, the impact that such disputes may 
have on corporate management. 
 Whether it is possible to maintain the continuity of corporate management 
considering the change of management, restructuring of business, etc. in the case 
where the largest stockholder is changed 
 If there is a secondary offering, the appropriateness of the secondary offering in 
terms of the demand for financing, retaining of management control, etc. of the 

 
 
 
listing applicant. 

3. Protection of investors 

It  shall  be  recognized  that  the  realization  of  public  interests  and  the  protection  of  investors  are  not 
harmed.   

Review items 

Focal points for review 

Public interests 
and investor 
protection   

 Whether the application for preliminary listing review and the attached 
documents contain any false statement or presentation of a material fact or 
omits to state or present a material fact. 
 In case where the largest shareholder or the management has ever sold or 
taken over management rights of a listed corporation, whether the market 
integrity was impeded in such processes or not. 
 In the case where a listing applicant is a corporation established through the 
spin-off (including business transfer, contribution in kind, etc; the same 
hereinafter) by a corporation listed on the KOSDAQ market or a corporation 
that lists its stocks on the KOSPI market, whether it is recognized that the 
parent corporation (referring to the parent company under Article 342-2(1) of 
the Commercial Act) of the listing applicant has made its best efforts to protect 
shareholders, such as collection of shareholders’ opinions and communication 
with shareholders, etc. 
 In the case where a re-listing applicant applies for re-listing after spin-off, 
whether it is recognized that efforts to protect minority shareholders of the 
newly-established corporation or the surviving corporation after the spin-off, 
such as collection of shareholders’ opinions, communication with 
shareholders, dividend policy, retirement of treasury stocks, etc., have been 
faithfully implemented, and whether the continuity of the surviving 
corporation is recognized after the split-off 
 In addition, any likelihood of infringing the realization of public interests and 
the protection of investors. 

※  This requirement may not apply if the parent company is changed or the core business sector of the 
listing applicant is changed after the spin-off. 

 
 
 
 
. 

[Annex No. 7]    Qualitative Criteria for Preliminary Listing Review by Industry 
(Corporate Continuity) 
(Amended on December 28, 2023; December 30, 2025)

(Pertaining to [§27]) 

1. Deep tech industry(1)(2)

Notes: 

Focal points for review 
The importance of national economic aspects of main technologies, such as 
their impact on related industries and contribution to the creation of new 
technologies and new industries. 
Innovativeness based on originality and differentiation of the main business. 
Ability to carry out business based on main technologies and whether the 
government has certified innovation.(3) 
Feasibility of technology in view of rationality of the main technology and 
completeness of development stages.   
 Competitiveness in commercializing the main technology and possibility of 
commercialization of main products.   
Possibility of maintaining technological capability based on expertise of the 
main technology and R&D capability, etc. 
Whether  the  business  plan  is  reasonable,  including  investment  plans  for 
human  resources  and  facility  for  the  growth  of  company  and  securing 
intellectual property rights. 
Growth potential of the business, including rationality of the main business 
and completeness for profit-realization, etc. 
Potential of business expansion, including possibilities of business derivation 
and linking with other industries. 
· Impact on corporate management in the event of a lawsuit or dispute related 
to patents, management rights, etc. 
· Effect  of contingent liabilities on management according to the terms and 
conditions of major contracts related to business. 

(1)  Subparagraph  1  applies  to  corporations  that  possess  national  strategic  technology  under  the 
Special Act on Fostering of National Strategic Technology or national high-tech strategic technology 
under  the  Act  on  Special  Measures  for  Strengthening  and  Protecting  Competitiveness  of  National 
High-tech Strategic Industries and operate technology in the relevant field as their main business. 
Provided that in the case of corporations that also fall into the bio industry under subparagraph 2, the 
standards of subparagraph 2 may be applied. 

(2) In the  case  where  a company  with no  realized profit  applies  for  preliminary  listing  review,  the 
review  item  of  ‘Technology’  in  subparagraph  1  shall  not  apply,  but  the  review  item  of  ‘Financial 
conditions’  for  ‘Companies  with  no  profit’  under  the  Qualitative  Criteria  in  [Annex  No.  6]  shall 
additionally apply. 

 
 
 
(3) It shall refer to cases where, as a case of the Financial Services Commission's designation as an 
innovative financial service pursuant to the Special Act on Financial Innovation Support or a similar 
case thereto, the case has been certified for innovation in technology in accordance with relevant laws 
and regulations. .

[Annex No. 8] Criteria for Identification of Corporate Insolvency Risks

each variable as below which have significant influences on corporate insolvency.

(1) Criteria refer to the standard value for judging whether each variable has a significant effect on the 
symptoms of insolvency. The value of the variable of the criteria shall be 1 in cases where it satisfies 
the criteria or 0 where it does not satisfy the criteria. However, for those variables without a criterion,

(2) It shall include the case where the audit opinion is  “unqualified”, but the uncertainty about the 
survival as a going concern is stated in the audit report as a special note. 

2. The Exchange shall calculate comprehensive measurement values of insolvency risks via the 
method  below  in  accordance  with  the  insolvency  scores  measured  by  variable  for  the 
KOSDAQ-listed corporations and designate investment attention issues by taking into account 
whether or not the comprehensive measurement values surpass the comprehensive threshold 
value(1).   

Method of calculating comprehensive measurement value of corporate insolvency risks(2) 

Insolvency score (z) = ∑ (value of variable by each value x weight by variable) – 4.494 

Comprehensive measurement value on insolvency risk = ez  ÷  (1 + ez) 

Notes: 
(1) The comprehensive threshold value shall be 0.7. 
(2) e means the natural constant (the base of the natural logarithm). 

3.  The  Exchange  shall  notify  the  KOSDAQ-listed  corporation  that  was  designated  as  an 
investment  attention  issue  of  the  result  of  designation  and  the  relevant  variables  for 
identification of insolvency risks, etc.

Notes: 
(1)  The  audit  report  or  review  report  in  [1)  to  4)]  refers  to  the  audit  report  or  review  report  filed 
pursuant to [§6(1)2(e)(i) or (ii)] of the Disclosure Regulation. In this case, in cases where there is a 
corrected report, the issue shall be designated as or released from an administrative issue on the day 
following the day of the corrected report. 

(2)  )  In  cases  where  an  issue  is  determined  to  maintain  listing  status  (including  the  cases  of  being 
excluded  from  listing  maintenance  review;  hereinafter  the  same)  after  it  went  through  the  listing 
maintenance review to which it was subject because it was designated as an investment attention issue 
due to a cause of [2) through 4)], the issue concerned shall be released from the designation as an 
investment attention issue under the concerned cause though the time for the release to be determined 
from 1) through 4) has not arrived. In such cases, the date of the release from the investment attention 
issue designation shall be the next day of the date when the listing maintenance is determined. 

(3) [1) to 13)] apply to corporations which listed common stocks. 

(4) [1) to 15)] apply to KOSDAQ-listed foreign corporations. 

(5) [3) to 7), 10) to 13) and 16) to 22)] apply to SPACs.
