International and foreign organizations 

 
 
 
[Annex No. 12]    Matters Required to be Entered in Articles of Incorporation of 
Foreign Companies 

Matters Required to be Entered in Articles of Incorporation of Foreign Companies 

1. General meeting of stockholders   

(a)  Time for convocation 

(1)  The  general  meeting  of  stockholders  shall  be  composed  of  the  ordinary  general  meeting  of 
stockholders and the extraordinary general meeting of stockholders   

(2) An ordinary general meeting of stockholders shall be convened within four (4) months after the 
end of every business year. 

(3) An extraordinary general meeting of stockholders shall be convened when there is a resolution of 
the board of directors, a request for convocation by shareholders who hold at least 3/100 of the total 
number of outstanding stocks or by shareholders who continued to hold at least 15/1,000 of the total 
number of outstanding stocks for more than six (6) months, or a request for convocation by the auditor 
or the audit committee, or a court order.   

(b) Convocation procedure (notice and announcement) 

When convening a general meeting of shareholders, a company shall inform shareholders of the date, 
time, place, and purpose of the meeting at least two (2) weeks prior to the date set for such general 
meeting in writing or in an electronic form.   

(c) Matters subject to special resolution   

(i) The  matters  falling  under  any  of  followings  shall be  determined  by  a  special  resolution  at  the 
general meeting of shareholders.   

ⓐ  Change  of the articles of  incorporation, merger and  spin-off,  stock  split,  dissolution,  capital 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
reduction, transfer of the entire or important part of business, taking over of the entire business of 
another corporation; and 

ⓑ  In the case of a foreign holding company (including foreign holding companies incorporated in 
Korea),  a  merger,  spin-off,  dissolution,  and  liquidation  or  change  of  structure  of  its  subsidiary 
company,  transfer  and  takeover  of  the  entire  or  an  important  part  of  business  of  its  subsidiary 
company,  issuance  of  new  shares  of  subsidiary  company  through  the  third-party  allotment,  and 
disposal of stocks of the subsidiary company. 

(ii) Special resolution at a general meeting of shareholders shall be adopted by the affirmative votes 
of at least 2/3 of voting rights of the stockholders present at the meeting and at least 1/3 of the total 
outstanding stocks. However, in cases where a foreign holding company (including foreign holding 
companies incorporated in Korea) falls under any of the followings cases or amends its articles of 
incorporation due to any of the following cases, a special resolution shall be made with at least 3/4 of 
the number of voting rights of the stockholders present at the meeting and at least 2/3 of the total 
number of outstanding stocks: 

ⓐ  Case where the foreign holding company sells the entire or part of the shares of a major foreign 
subsidiary corporation and, as a result, the major foreign subsidiary corporation loses its position 
as a foreign subsidiary company of the foreign holding company; and   

ⓑ  Case where a major foreign subsidiary corporation is suspended from actual business activities 
due to the transfer of the entire or an important part of its business. 

(d) Place of the meeting 

The general meeting of shareholders shall be held at the place of the principal office or of the stock 
exchange where the company is listed. 

(e) General meeting of stockholders of certain classes of stocks 

(i) In case where a corporation issued certain classes of stocks and stockholders of a certain class of 
stocks are damaged due to the special provisions for each class of stocks, amendment of the articles 
of incorporation, stock swap, stock transfer, merger, spin-off, merger subsequent to spin-off, etc., a 
resolution adopted by a general meeting of stockholders of such specific class of stocks is required 
for effecting such events in addition to the resolution at the general meeting of stockholders. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(ii) A resolution of a general meeting of stockholders of certain classes of stocks shall be adopted by 
the affirmative votes of at least 2/3 of the voting rights of the stockholders present at the meeting and 
of 1/3 of the total number of outstanding stocks of such class. 

(iii) Provisions relating to a general meeting of stockholders shall apply mutatis mutandis to a general 
meeting of stockholders of different classes of stocks except for the special classes of stocks including 
non-voting different class of stocks.   

2. Directors 

(a) Number of directors and appointment of outside directors   

(i) The number of directors of this company shall be more than 3 but less than  ○, and the number 
of outside directors shall be more than 1/4 of the total number of directors (for a corporation of which 
total amount of assets is KRW 2 trillion or more as of the end of the latest business year, it shall be 
more  than  three  (3)  and  the  half  of  the  total  number  of  directors).  However,  in  case  where  a 
corporation has been listed in the qualified foreign stock market for more than three (3) years, the 
number of outside directors shall be one (1) or more.   

(ii)  In  case  where  an  outside  director  candidate  recommendation  committee  is  established,  the 
committee shall recommend candidates for outside directors from among the persons satisfying the 
qualifications specified in the relevant laws of home country. 

(iii)  The  details  for  recommendation  and  examination  of  qualifications  of  candidates  for  outside 
directors shall be determined by the outside director candidate recommendation committee. 

(b) Remuneration for directors   

The amount of remuneration and severance pay of directors shall be determined by a resolution at the 
general meeting of stockholders unless such amount is specified in these articles of incorporation.   

(c) Minutes of board of directors and inspection rights of stockholders 

(i) Minutes shall be prepared with regard to the proceedings of a board of directors’ meeting.   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(ii) The agenda items, summary of the proceedings and outcomes thereof, and opponents and grounds 
for their opposition shall be entered in the minutes, and directors and auditors present at the meeting 
shall sign their names and affix their seals or signatures thereon. 

(iii) Stockholders may request either to inspect or copy the minutes of the board of directors’ meeting 
during business hours.   

(iv) This company may  reject shareholders’ requests for  inspecting  or  copying  the  minutes of the 
board of directors’ meeting with an explanation of grounds therefor.   

(d) Release from directors’ liability to company 

A director’s liability for damages to the company occurred by may be absolved by the consent of all 
stockholders. 

3. Auditors or audit committee 

[Case of appointing an auditor] 

(a) Number of auditors and appointment   

(i) Number of auditors of a company shall be at least one (1) but less than  ○. In such cases, if the 
total amount of assets of the corporation is KRW 100 billion or more as of the end of the latest business 
year, at least one (1) of the auditors shall be a standing auditor.   

(ii)  Auditors  shall  be  appointed  at  a  general  meeting  of  shareholders,  and  the  resolutions  for 
appointing auditors shall be adopted separately from those for appointing directors.   

(iii) A resolution to appoint an auditor shall be adopted by the affirmative votes of majority of the 
stockholders present at the meeting and of at least 1/4 of the total number of outstanding stocks   

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(b) Term of office 

The  term  of  office  of  an  auditor  shall  expire  upon  the  closing  of  an  ordinary  general  meeting  of 
stockholders convened in respect of the last period for the settlement of accounts within three (3) years 
after his/her inauguration. 

(c) Appointment of an auditor to fill up a vacancy   

If there is a vacancy of an auditor, the position shall be filled through appointment at a general meeting 
of shareholders. However, in case where the number of auditors in office satisfies the requirement on 
the number of auditors specified in these articles of incorporation and the vacancy does not hinder the 
performance of duties of auditor(s), the vacancy may be left unfilled.   

(d) Duties of auditors 

(i) Auditors shall audit accounting and business of a company. 

(ii) Auditors may attend and state their opinions at the board of directors’ meeting. 

(iii) Auditors  may  request  the  board  of  directors  to  convene  an  extraordinary  general  meeting  of 
stockholders by presenting a written statement specifying the subject matter of the meeting and the 
grounds for the convocation. 

(iv) The auditor of the parent company may request its subsidiary company to report on its business 
if it is necessary for carrying out his/her duties. In such cases, if a subsidiary fails to make a report 
without delay or it is required to verify the contents of such reports, the auditor of the parent company 
may investigate the business affairs of the subsidiary company and the status of its property. 

(v) The appointment of an external auditor shall be approved by the auditor.   

(e) Audit record 

Auditors shall prepare a record of audit. A summary of auditing process and the outcomes thereof shall 
be recorded in the audit record and the auditors who have carried out such audit shall write their names 
and affix their seals or signatures thereon. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(f) Remuneration and severance pay for auditors   

The amount of remuneration and severance pay to be received by auditors shall be determined by a 
resolution  at  a  general  meeting  of  stockholders  if  such  amount  is  not  specified  in  these  articles  of 
incorporation. In such cases, a resolution for determining the amount of remuneration and severance 
pay for an auditor shall be adopted separately from those for directors. 

[Case of establishing an audit committee] 

(A corporation of which total amount of assets is KRW 2 trillion or more as of the end of the latest 
business year shall establish an audit committee.) 

(a) Composition of an audit committee   

(i) This company shall establish an audit committee in lieu of auditors. 

(ii) The audit committee shall consist of at least three (3) directors. Provided that the ratio of outside 
directors shall exceed 2/3 (the majority of members in case where a corporation has been listed for 
more  than  three  (3)  years  on  the  recognized  overseas  securities  market)  of  the  total  number  of 
members. 

(iii) The audit committee shall, from among its members, elect a member to represent the committee 
as chairperson, by its own resolution. In such cases, the chairperson shall be an outside director.   

(b) Duties of the Audit Committee 

(i) The audit committee shall audit accounting and business of a company. 

(ii) The audit  Committee may request  the  board of directors to convene  an  extraordinary  general 
meeting  of  stockholders  by  presenting  a  written  statement  specifying  the  subject  matter  of  the 
meeting and the grounds for the convocation. 

(iii) When necessary for carrying out its duties, the audit committee may request a subsidiary for a 
report on its business. In such cases, if the subsidiary fails to immediately make the report or it is 
necessary to verify the contents of the report, the audit committee may inspect the business affairs 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
and the status of property of the subsidiary. 

(iv) An audit committee shall give its approval when it comes to appointing an external auditor. 

(v) An  audit  committee  shall  handle  other  matters  delegated  by the  board  of  directors  than  those 
stated in (1) through (4) above.   

(c) Audit record 

The audit committee shall prepare a record of audit. The summary of audit process and the outcomes 
thereof shall be recorded in the audit record and auditors who have carried out such audit shall write 
their names and affix their seals or signatures thereon. 

4. Subscription rights 

(i) Each shareholder shall be entitled to the allotment of new shares in proportion to the number of 
shares which he/she holds. 

(ii) Notwithstanding the preemptive subscription rights of stockholders, the company may make an 
allotment  of  new  stocks  to  other  persons  than  stockholders  through  a  resolution  of  the  board  of 
directors in the case of each of followings: 

a. ··········   

b. ··········   

c. ·········· 

(iii)  In  case  where stockholders  give  up  or  forfeits  his/her  subscription  rights  or  where fractional 
stocks are created in allotting new stocks, the method of handling such matters shall be decided by a 
resolution of the board of directors.   

5. Stockholders’ rights to inspect books of account     

(i) Any shareholder who holds shares representing at least three (3) percent of the total outstanding 
shares or at least 10/10,000 of the total outstanding shares since six (6) months before may demand, 
in writing stating the grounds therefor, the inspection or copying of the books of account and related 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
documents. 

(ii) The company shall not reject the demand made by a shareholder unless it proves that such demand 
is improper. 

6. Reporting of audit report to regular general meeting of shareholders   

(i) The company shall receive an audit report audited by an external auditor one (1) week before an 
ordinary general meeting of shareholders and report it to shareholders at the ordinary general meeting 
of shareholders. 

(ii) Financial statements shall be prepared according to the accounting standards (referring to changed 
accounting standards in case where the Exchange approved the change of the accounting standards) 
selected at the time of the initial listing of stocks on the Exchange 

7. Exceptions in applying the matters to be stated in the articles of incorporation   

In cases where the matters required to be stated in the articles of incorporation are inconsistent with 
those in relevant laws and regulations of the home country of the foreign corporation or of the foreign 
stock market where stocks of a foreign corporation are listed (including regulations or guidelines of the 
stock exchange concerned), the matters that the Exchange deems necessary may be stated differently in 
the articles of incorporation. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex No. 13] Matters Required to be Entered in Articles of Incorporation of SPACs 

Matters Required to be Entered in Articles of Incorporation   
of Special Purpose Acquisition Companies 
(Pertaining to [§70] of Enforcement Rules) 

1. Business objective 

The sole business objective of this Corporation shall be to merger with another company (hereinafter 
referred to as “the merger target company”) after listing issued stocks on the KOSDAQ market of the 
Korea Exchange established pursuant to Article 373 of the Financial Investment Services and Capital 
Markets Act.   

2. Stocks   

(a) Duty on deposit (trust) of funds   

At least 90/100 of the funds raised by issuing stocks (excluding the stocks issued before the initial 
public  offering)  shall  be  deposited  (or  entrusted)  with  the  securities  finance  companies  (or  trust 
companies) prescribed in Article 1-4-2(2) of the Regulations on Financial Investment Business by the 
next business day of the payment due date for the stocks.   

(b) Restrictions on withdrawal of and prohibition of security provision with deposited funds 

This  Corporation  shall  not  withdraw  the  funds  or  provide  security  with  the  funds  deposited  (or 
entrusted) at the securities finance companies (or trust companies) (including interests or dividends; 
the  same  hereinafter)  before  the  completion  of  registration  of  the  merger  with  the  merger  target 
company. However, when it is inevitable for the operation of this Corporation and falling under any 
of the followings, the funds deposited (or entrusted) may be withdrawn:     

(1) Case of withdrawing within the amount necessary for purchasing stocks to exercise the appraisal 
rights pursuant to [§165-5] of the Act; and 

(2) Case of paying the funds deposited (or entrusted) to stockholders, subsequent to dissolution of 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
this Corporation.   

(c) Paid-in capital increase by third-party allotment   

In case where, after listing its stocks on the KOSDAQ market of the Korea Exchange, this Company issues new 
stocks to be allocated to the persons other than the existing stockholders, it shall obtain in advance the resolution 
of the general meeting of shareholders pursuant to Article 434 of the Commercial Act.   

3. Prohibition on borrowing and issuance of debt securities 

(a) Prohibition on borrowing 

This  Corporation  is  prohibited  from  borrowing  funds  from  others,  guaranteeing  debt,  or  providing 
security for others.   

(b) Prohibition on issuance of debt securities 

This Corporation shall not issue debt securities. However, it can issue convertible bonds or bonds with 
warrant under Article 513 or 516-2 of the Commercial Act before the initial offering of stocks to list 
the stocks on the KOSDAQ market of the Korea Exchange. 

4. Mergers 

(a) Merger target company 

(i)  The  merger  value  of  the  merger  target  company  calculated  in  accordance  with  each  of 
subparagraphs under Paragraph (1) of Article 176-5 of the Enforcement Decree of the Act or the total 
assets of the merger target company based on the statement of financial position as of the end of the 
latest business year shall be 80/100 or more of the funds deposited (or entrusted). In such cases, if 
there are a multiple number of merger target companies, it shall be based on the aggregate amount of 
the merger values or the total assets of individual merger target company. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(ii) No negotiation shall be on the process for determining the merger target company or no company 
shall  be  potentially  determined as  the  merger target company  before  the initial public  offering  of 
stocks.   

* In case where the merger target company is a venture corporation under [§2(1)38] of the KOSDAQ 
Market Listing Regulation, it shall be written that the venture company concerned is the merger 
target company.   

(b) Restrictions on merger   

(i) This  Corporation  shall not merge  in  the manner of  consolidation  of  corporations prescribed  in 
Article  542  of  the  Commercial  Act,  and  when  merging  with  an  unlisted  corporation  under 
Article9(15)4  of  the Act,  the  merger  shall  not  be  conducted  in  the  manner  that  this  Corporation 
becomes  the  non-surviving  company  as  a  result  of  the  merger  except  for  the  listing  after  merger 
pursuant to [§2(1)1(f)(ii)] of the Regulation. 

(ii) This Corporation shall not merger with the companies falling under any of followings: 

  Persons  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “stockholders,  etc.  before  IPO”)  who  have  purchased  the 
securities  (including  those  related  to  non-voting  stocks;  hereinafter  referred  to  as  “stocks,  etc.”) 
under each item of Subparagraph 1 of Article 139 of the Enforcement Decree of the Act before the 
initial offering of stocks of this Corporation. 

A  company  where  the  stockholders,  etc.  before  IPO  of  this  Corporation  or  the  persons  falling 
under any of followings are the large shareholders prescribed in Subparagraph 6 of Article 2 of the 
Act on Corporate Governance of Financial Companies [the “financial companies” shall be construed 
as “KOSDAQ-listed corporations” and the “outstanding voting shares (including equities; hereafter 
the same shall apply)” shall be construed as “outstanding shares”; the same hereinafter] or hold 5/100 
or more of the total issued and outstanding stocks:   

ⓐ  As the executives and employees of an investment dealing company for equity securities under 
Article 6(4)14(c) of the Enforcement Decree of the Act, which belongs to the stockholders, etc. 
before IPO of this Corporation, the persons who have performed or are performing tasks related to 
the establishment, operation, etc. of this Corporation and their spouses and lineal ascendants and 
descendants; 

ⓑ  Executives of a corporation who belong to the stockholders, etc. before IPO of this Corporation, 
and their spouses and lineal ascendants and descendants; 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
ⓒ  Individuals who belong to the stockholders, etc. before IPO of this Corporation, their spouses 
and lineal ascendants and descendants; and 

ⓓ  Executives and employees of this Corporation, and their spouses and lineal ascendants and 
descendants. 

  The  large  shareholders  prescribed  in  Subparagraph  6  of  Article  2  of  the  Act  on  Corporate 
Governance  of  Financial  Companies  and  the  affiliated  companies  prescribed  in  the  Monopoly 
Regulation and Fair Trade Act of the stockholders, etc. before IPO of this Corporation, and   

 Corporations of which executives and employees hold or have held within the latest two (2) years 
concurrent positions with this Corporation or the stockholders, etc. before IPO. 

(iii) When calculating the number of stock holdings noted in (2)b above, the number of stocks that 
may  be  issued  through  the  exercise  of  the  rights  of  stocks  falling  under  any  of  items  under 
Subparagraph 1 of Article 139 of the Enforcement Decree of the Act shall be  included, and when 
calculating the number of stocks of the stockholders, etc. before IPO, the number of stocks held by 
the affiliated companies of the concerned stockholders shall be included.   

5. Officers 

(a) Qualifications of officers 

Any person falling under any of Subparagraphs of Articles 5 and 6 of the Act on Corporate Governance 
of Financial Companies may not become an executive of this Corporation, and an executive shall lose 
his/her position if he/she falls hereunder after taking the position. 

(b) Number of directors   

The number of outside directors of this Corporation shall be at least 1/4 of the total number of directors.   

(c) Duty of executives and employees 

Executives and employees of this Corporation shall not reveal or offer any information which can help 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
specify or assume the merger target company before a merger.   

6. Dissolution of this Corporation and return of deposited (or entrusted) funds   

(a) Dissolution of this Corporation 

When falling under any of following cases, this Corporation shall be dissolved.   

(1) Case where this Corporation fails to list its stocks on the securities market within 90 days from 
the deadline for payment for the stocks issued by the IPO.   

(2) Case where this Corporation fails to complete the registration of merger with the merger target 
company within 36 months after the deadline for payment for the stocks issued through the IPO.   

(3)  Case  where  the  stocks  of  this  Corporation  were  delisted  pursuant  to  the  listing  regulations 
prescribed in Article 390 of the Act before the registration of merger with the merger target company 
is completed. 

(b) Return of the funds deposited (or entrusted) 

In case where this Corporation is dissolved by falling under the causes for dissolution noted in (a) 
above, the funds (including interests or dividends) deposited (or entrusted)  at the securities finance 
companies (or trust companies) shall be paid back to the stockholders according to their holding ratios. 
However, in case where the stockholders, etc. before IPO have given up their rights to request for a 
return of funds relating to the stocks, etc. purchased before the IPO of stocks of this Corporation, the 
repayment shall be made according to the holding ratios of the stocks excluding those purchased prior 
to the IPO. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
[Annex No. 14]    Listing Fees and Annual Dues 
(Amended on February 14, 2022; April 29, 2022; September 27, 2022, December 9, 2022; July 9, 2025; March 
16, 2026)

1 billion shall be rounded up. 

6. In case where an applicant for listing change submits several applications for listing change on a

as a single case.

2. Annual Dues 

(a) Stocks, foreign stocks, DRs of foreign stocks, and different classes of stocks     

Annual Dues 

(Amounts less than KRW 100 shall be discarded) 

1. Annual dues paid regularly: On the basis of average total market capitalization of the previous year, 
the amount determined by applying the fee rate noted below. 

2. Annual dues paid irregularly: The amount determined by prorating the annual dues for the concerned 
year calculated by applying the average total market capitalization as of the decision date of de-listing 
and the rate shown in the table below by the number of days from the first day to the day before the de-
listing date of the year which includes the de-listing date.   

Average total market 
capitalization   

(in KRW billion)

Notes: 

1. When calculating the annual dues paid regularly, in case of initial listing or re-listing, it shall be 
the amount determined by prorating the amount calculated according to the method shown in the table 
above  by  the  number  of  days  from  the  initial  listing  date  or  re-listing  date  to  the  last  day  of  the 
concerned year. 

2.  In  the  case  of  initial  listing  and  re-listing,  the  average  total  market  capitalization  shall  be  the 
average total market value of the concerned number of days. 

3.  The  average  total  market  capitalization  shall  be  determined  by  aggregating  the  market 
capitalizations of common stocks and class shares issued by the concerned listed corporation.   

4. When determining the fees per KRW 1 billion, the amount less than KRW 1 billion shall be rounded 
up.   

5. The average total market capitalization shall be determined by averaging the market value listed. 
In such cases, if the trading is suspended, the market capitalization of the day immediately preceding 
the trading suspension date shall be regarded as the market capitalization of the trading suspension 
date.

1/3 of the fees determined pursuant to subparagraph(a) 

(Amounts less than KRW 100 shall be discarded) 

Note:   

1. The average market capitalization of subscription rights certificates shall be the amount calculated 
by multiplying the closing price on the day before the listing date of underlying stock of concerned 

 
 
subscription rights certificate by the number of certificates to be listed. In such cases, if the trading is 
suspended, the market capitalization of the day immediately preceding the trading suspension date 
shall be regarded as the market capitalization of the trading suspension date. 

  2. In the case of business development investment trust beneficiary certificates, the average market capitalization 

shall be deemed as the average trust principal amount.   

3. Payment Time of Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

(a)  Listing Fees 

Fees for preliminary listing review 
Listing fees 

Payment Time 
At the time of application for preliminary listing review 
At the time of listing application 

  Note: Re-listing fees may be paid by the listing date. 

(b)  Annual Dues 

Regular payments 

Irregular payments 

Payment Time 
The annual dues of the immediately preceding year for the stocks listed 
as at the end of the immediately preceding year shall be paid by the end 
of January each year.   
In case where securities are delisted, the annual dues for the period 
from the first day of the year which includes the concerned delisting 
date to the previous day of delisting date shall be paid before the 
delisting date of the securities concerned.   

4. Exemption from Payment of Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

The Exchange may exempt the listing fees and annual dues that fall under any of followings. 

(a) Listing fees and annual dues falling under any of the followings as of the payment dates. 

(i) Listing fees and annual dues for listing change and supplementary listing of KOSDAQ-listed 
corporations falling under [§56(1)6] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; 

(ii) Supplementary listing fees, listing change fees and annual dues of the stocks (including different 
classes of stocks), DRs of foreign stocks and subscription warrants issued by the KOSDAQ-listed 
corporations who are under the rehabilitation procedures pursuant to the Debtor Rehabilitation and 
Bankruptcy Act (in the case of foreign stocks and DRs of foreign stocks, it shall refer to the relevant 
laws of home countries). 

(b) Annual dues falling under any of the followings as of the imposition dates. 

(i) In case where a corporation is delisted during the period for regular payments or within three (3) 
months  after  the  payment  period  ended  (including  the  case  where  the  causes  for  delisting  have 
occurred, while excluding the case of being delisted after the improvement period was granted), the 
amount of annual dues for the period from the first day of the year which includes such delisting 
date to the previous day of the delisting date. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(ii) In case where a corporation is delisted pursuant to [§54(1)2] and [§54(1)3] (limited to the cases 
of dissolution pursuant to Subparagraphs 5 and 6 of Article 227 of the Commercial Act), or [§54(1)6] 
of the Regulation, the amount of annual dues for the period from the first day of the year which 
includes the delisting date to the previous day of the delisting date. 

(iii) In cases where a KOSDAQ-listed corporation has a liquidity provision agreement stipulated in 
[§12-3(1)]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Business  Regulation  for  the  year  that  is  the  base  for  the 
calculation of annual dues, the amount of annual dues prorated on a daily basis for the period of 
liquidity provision (the amount less than KRW 100 shall be discarded). 

(c) In the case of the designated corporations that meet the requirements specified in [§26(5)], fees for 
preliminary listing review and listing fees (excluding fees for listing change and supplementary listing). 

(d) The fees for listing review for different classes of stocks falling under [§78(2)] of the Regulation. 

(e) The fees for listing change of subscription rights certificates pursuant to [§44(2)] and Paragraphs 
(2) and (3) of [§84] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation. 

(f) Listing fees and annual dues for subscription rights certificates. 

(g) The  fees  for  preliminary  listing  review  and  listing  fees  (excluding  fees  for  listing  change  and 
supplementary listing, but including fees for listing change and supplementary listing subsequent to 
the listing after merge under [§2(1)1(f)] of the Regulation) of the companies falling under [§2(1)41], 
[§2(1)39]  and  [§75(2)]  of  the  Regulation.  However,  the  provisions  of  this  Item  shall  not  apply  to 
foreign companies (including foreign holding companies located in Korea). 

(h) The annual dues (based on the regular payment in January each year) for the period of three (3) 
consecutive business years which include the business year in which the dates of initial listing and 
listing after merger of the companies falling under [§2(1)41], [§2(1)39] and [§75(2)] of the Regulation 
fall.  However,  the  provisions  of  this  Item  shall  not  apply  to  foreign  companies  (including  foreign 
holding companies located in Korea). 

(i)  In  the  case  of  initial  listing  and  listing  after  merger  of  a  KONEX-listed  corporation,  fees  for 
preliminary listing review and listing (excluding fees for listing change and supplementary listing, but 
including fees for listing change and supplementary listing subsequent to the listing after merge under 
[§2(1)1(f)] of the Regulation). 

(j) In the case of initial listing and listing after merger of a KONEX-listed corporation on the KOSDAQ 
Market, the annual dues (based on the regular payment in January each year) for the period of three 
(3) consecutive business years which include the business year to which the date of initial listing or 
listing after merger of the company belongs. 

(k) In addition, the listing fees and annual dues that the Exchange deems it necessary to exempt for 
the purpose of market administration, etc. 

5. Other Matters relating to Listing Fees and Annual Dues 

(a) Notification of payment and measures against non-payment 

 
 
 
(i) With regard to the payment of annual dues, the Exchange shall notify the listed corporations of 
such fact by the day two (2) weeks before the due date for the regular payments and by the day one 
(1) week before the delisting date for the irregular payments.   

(ii) In cases where a listed corporation fails to pay the annual dues within three (3) months after the 
due  date,  the  Exchange  may  file  actions  such  as  request  for  an  order  of  payment  against  the 
concerned corporation. Provided that this provision shall not apply to issuers of delisted securities. 

(b) Refund 

The Exchange shall refund the listing fees to the corporation of which listing application was rejected. 
However, the fees for preliminary listing review shall not be refundable once the preliminary listing 
review process has commenced.

[Annex Form No.4] Listing Agreement 

Listing Agreement (Domestic Companies Excluding SPACs)   

______  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Company”)  enters  into  this  Agreement  with  the  Korea  Exchange 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Exchange”) as per the following terms and conditions to list and trade the stocks 
issued by the Company on the KOSDAQ market. 

Article 1 (Observance of Laws and Regulations) The Company shall observe faithfully the following laws and 
regulations, which are currently enforced, may be established and amended from time to time in the future with 
respect to the operation of the KOSDAQ market. 

1.  The Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act, the Enforcement Decree and the Enforcement 

Rules of the same Act; 

2.  The KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

3.  The KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

4.  The KOSDAQ Market Disclosure Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; and 

5.  Other matters such as standards, guidelines and policies set forth by the Exchange or the parties that are 

authorized by the Exchange in relation to KOSDAQ-listed corporations. 

Article 2 (Cooperation with respect to investigation of abnormal transactions) In cases where the Exchange deems 
it necessary with respect to the investigation of abnormal transactions of listed stocks, it may request the Company, 
in writing or via wired and/or wireless communications, to submit copies of materials related to the process of 
creation of material corporate information (minutes of the board of directors, contracts, etc.) including the time of 
generation  of  the  information,  list  of  officers  and  employees,  personal  information  on  major  insiders,  list  of 
shareholders, etc., and in such cases, the Company shall reply faithfully to the request. 

Article  3  (Maintaining  corporate  continuity  and  ensuring  management  transparency)  The  Company  shall  not 
conduct such activities as unfair fund transactions with the largest shareholder and the related persons that may 
significantly impede maintaining the independence and the nature as a going-concern of the Company and shall 
ensure the transparency of management through refurbishing of articles of association and regulations, faithful 
performance  of  directors’  duties,  transparent  accounting  practices,  fair  auditing,  proper  disclosure,  holding 
investor  relations  sessions,  prohibiting  unfair  inside  transactions,  protecting  shareholders’  rights  and  interests, 
improving corporate governance and etc. 

Article 4 (Measures) In cases where the Exchange deems it necessary for the effective implementation of this 
Agreement,  it  may  request  the  Company  for  necessary  matters,  in  writing  or  wired  and/or  wireless 
communications, such as submission of related data or reports and interviews with persons involved, and in this 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
case, the Company shall respond immediately to the request as long as there are no  special reasons which are 
acknowledged by the Exchange. 

Article 5 (Effect for successor) This Agreement shall be effective for the person who succeeds the status of the 
Company or the Exchange. 

Article 6 (Agreement on jurisdiction) It is agreed upon that all disputes that may arise in relation to this Agreement 
shall be finally settled by the court with the jurisdiction over the location of the KOSDAQ Market Division. 

Article 7 (Holding IR sessions) 

(1)  The  Company  shall  hold  investor  relations  sessions  regarding  business  performance,  business  plan  and 
prospect (hereinafter referred to as the “IR sessions”) at least once a year during two (2) years from the initial 
listing date. However, in cases where the period from the date of listing to the end of the year which includes the 
listing date is shorter than two (2) months, this shall apply starting with the year following the year which includes 
the listing date. 

(2) When providing related information to an unspecified number of investors at investor relations sessions, the 
Company shall maintain the fairness and objectivity. 

Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

Name and signature/seal of the representative director: 

Name and signature/seal of the chairperson of KRX: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Listing Agreement (Foreign Companies Excluding Foreign-listed Foreign Companies) 

______  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Company”)  enters  into  this  Agreement  with  the  Korea  Exchange 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Exchange”) as per the following terms and conditions to list and trade the stocks 
issued by the Company on the KOSDAQ market. 

Article 1 (Observance of Laws and Regulations) The Company shall observe faithfully the following laws and 
regulations, which are currently enforced, may be established and amended from time to time in the future with 
respect to the operation of the KOSDAQ market. 

1. The Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act, the Enforcement Decree and the Enforcement 
Rules of the same Act; 

2. The KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

3. The KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

4. The KOSDAQ Market Disclosure Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; and 

5. Other matters such as standards, guidelines and policies set forth by the Exchange or the parties that are 
authorized by the Exchange in relation to KOSDAQ-listed corporations. 

Article 2 (Cooperation with respect to investigation of abnormal transactions) In cases where the Exchange deems 
it necessary with respect to the investigation of abnormal transactions of listed stocks, it may request the Company 
or the disclosure agent, in writing or via wired and/or wireless communications, to submit copies of materials 
related to the process of creation of material corporate information (minutes of the board of directors, contracts 
etc.) including the time of generation of the information, list of executives and employees, personal information 
on major insiders, list of shareholders, etc., and in such cases, the Company or the disclosure agent shall reply 
faithfully to the request. 

Article 3 (Maintaining corporate continuity and ensuring management transparency)   

(1) The Company shall not conduct such activities as unfair fund transactions with the largest shareholder and the 
related persons that may significantly impede maintaining the independence and the nature as a going-concern of 
the Company and shall ensure the transparency of management through refurbishing of articles of incorporation 
and regulations, faithful performance of directors’ duties, transparent accounting practices, fair auditing, proper 
disclosures,  holding  investor relations  sessions,  prohibiting  unfair  inside  transactions,  protecting  shareholders’ 
rights and interests, improving corporate governance and etc. 

(2) The Company shall apply the same type of accounting standards as that applied at the time of listing, and in 
cases where the Company intends to change this, it shall obtain an approval from the Exchange. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) In cases where the Company has listed its shares by applying the requirements for initial listing of foreign 
holding company under [§62] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, the subsidiary under [§2(1)27] of the 
KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation  shall  maintain  the  position  as  a  subsidiary  after  listing.  However,  this 
provision shall not apply to the case where the Exchange authorizes in advance. 

Article 4 (Measures) 

(1) In cases where the Exchange deems it necessary for the effective implementation  of this Agreement, it may 
request  the  Company  or  the  disclosure  agent  for  necessary  matters,  in  writing  or  wired  and/or  wireless 
communications, such as submission of related materials or reports and interviews with persons involved, and in 
such  cases,  the  Company  shall  reply  immediately  to  the  request  as  long  as  there  are  no  special  reasons 
acknowledged by the Exchange. 

(2) The Exchange may delist the Company in the case where it deems the investor protection is severely affected 
as the Company fails to comply with the provisions of paragraphs (2) and (3) under Article 3 above.   

Article 5 (Change of listing agent and disclosure agent) In cases where the listing agent or disclosure agent is 

changed after the conclusion of this Agreement, the Company shall notify the Exchange of such fact. 

Article 6 (Effect for successor) This Agreement shall be effective for the person who succeeds the status of the 
Company or the Exchange. 

Article 7 (Agreement on jurisdiction) It is agreed upon that all disputes that may arise in relation to this Agreement 
shall be finally settled by the court with the jurisdiction over the location of the KOSDAQ Market Division. 

Article 8 (Efforts to provide corporate information)   

(1) The  Company shall have offices located in Korea and be  furnished with human resources and facilities to 
provide corporate information. However, the same shall not apply in cases where it has a related company under 
Article 21(1) of the Act on External Audit located in Korea, and the Exchange deems that the related company 
can perform the relevant businesses affairs on behalf of the Company. 

(2)  The  Company  shall  hold  investor  relations  sessions  regarding  business  performance,  business  plan  and 
prospect at least once per half-year during two (2) years from the initial listing date at the time of closing accounts 
(including semi-annual closings). However, in cases where the period from the date of listing to the end of the 
year which includes the listing date or the remaining period of the half-year is shorter than two (2) months, this 
shall apply starting with the half-year following the half-year which includes the listing date. 

(3)The Company shall appoint at least one (1) Korean outside director who has an address or residence in Korea. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

Name and signature/seal of the representative director: 

Name and signature/seal of the chairperson of KRX: 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Listing Agreement (Foreign-listed Foreign Companies) 

______  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the  Company”)  enters  into  this  Agreement  with  the  Korea  Exchange 
(hereinafter referred to as “the Exchange”) as per the following terms and conditions to list and trade the stocks 
issued by the Company on the KOSDAQ market. 

Article 1 (Observance of Laws and Regulations) The Company shall observe faithfully the following laws and 
regulations, which are currently enforced, may be established and amended from time to time in the future with 
respect to the operation of the KOSDAQ market. 

1. The Financial Investment Services and Capital Markets Act, the Enforcement Decree and the Enforcement 
Rules of the same Act; 

2. The KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

3. The KOSDAQ Market Business Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; 

4. The KOSDAQ Market Disclosure Regulation and the Enforcement Rules of the same Regulation; and 

5. Other matters such as standards, guidelines and policies set forth by the Exchange or the parties that are 
authorized by the Exchange in relation to KOSDAQ-listed corporations. 

Article 2 (Cooperation with respect to investigation of abnormal transactions) In cases where the Exchange deems 
it necessary with respect to the investigation of abnormal transactions of listed stocks, it may request the Company 
or the disclosure agent, in writing or via wired and/or wireless communications, to submit copies of materials 
related to the process of creation of material corporate information (minutes of the board of directors, contracts 
etc.) including the time of generation of the information, list of executives and employees, personal information 
on major insiders, list of shareholders, etc., and in such cases, the Company or the disclosure agent shall reply 
faithfully to the request. 

Article 3 (Maintaining corporate continuity and ensuring management transparency)   

(1) The Company shall not conduct such activities as unfair fund transactions with the largest shareholder and the 
related persons that may significantly impede maintaining the independence and the nature as a going-concern of 
the Company and shall ensure the transparency of management through refurbishing of articles of incorporation 
and regulations, faithful performance of directors’ duties, transparent accounting practices, fair auditing, proper 
disclosures, holding investor relations activities, prohibiting unfair inside transactions, protecting shareholders’ 
rights and interests, improving corporate governance and etc. 

(2) The Company shall apply the same type of accounting standards as that applied at the time of listing, and in 
the case where the Company intends to change this, it shall obtain an approval from the Exchange. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(3) In cases where the Company has listed its shares by applying the requirements for initial listing of foreign 
holding companies pursuant to [§62] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, the subsidiary under [§2(1)27] 
of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation shall maintain the position as a subsidiary after listing. However, this 
provision shall not apply to the case where the Exchange authorizes in advance. 

Article 4 (Measures) 

(1)  In  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  for  the  effective  implementation  of  this Agreement,  it 

Exchange  may request the Company or the  disclosure  agent for necessary matters, in writing or wired and/or 

wireless communications, such as submission of related materials or reports and interviews with persons involved, 

and in such cases, the Company shall reply immediately to the request as long as there are no special reasons 

acknowledged by the Exchange. 

(2) The Exchange may delist the Company in cases where it deems the investor protection is severely affected as 
the Company fails to comply with the provisions of paragraphs (2) and (3) under Article 3 above.   

Article 5 (Change of listing agent and disclosure agent) In cases where the listing agent or disclosure agent is 

changed after the conclusion of this Agreement, the Company shall notify the Exchange of such fact. 

Article 6 (Effect for successor) This Agreement shall be effective for the person who succeeds the status of the 
Company or the Exchange. 

Article 7 (Agreement on jurisdiction) It is agreed upon that all disputes that may arise in relation to this Agreement 
shall be finally settled by the court having the jurisdiction over the location of the KOSDAQ Market Division. 

Article 8 (Holding IR sessions)   

(1)  The  Company  shall  hold  investor  relations  sessions  regarding  business  performance,  business  plan  and 
prospect (hereinafter referred to as the “IR sessions”) at least once per half-year during two (2) years from the 
initial listing date at the time of closing accounts (including semi-annual closings). However, in cases where the 
period from the date of listing to the end of the year which includes the listing date or the remaining period of the 
half-year is shorter than two (2) months, this shall apply starting with the half-year following the half-year which 
includes the listing date. 

(2) When providing related information to an unspecified number of investors at investor relations sessions, the 
Company shall maintain the fairness and objectivity. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

Name and signature/seal of the representative director: 

Name and signature/seal of the chairperson of KRX:

[Annex Form No.14]    Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding   
(Amended on February 14, 2022; February 17, 2022; April 29, 2022; December 28, 2023; March 16, 2026) 

Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding of Stocks, etc. (Initial Listing, etc.) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,  
mm/dd/yyyy 

                              Date: 

I and the related persons (hereinafter referred to as “the party undersigned”) hereby affirm that we will 
keep the following promises as the persons subject to mandatory holding falling under the provisions 
of [§26], [§61], [§69] and [§77] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation in relation to initial listing 
of             

  Co. Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as “the Company”) on the KOSDAQ market. 

1. The party undersigned will mandatorily hold the stocks, etc. issued by the Company (referring 
to the securities under [§2(1)10] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and including bonus 
stocks to be issued pursuant to [§3] of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing 
Regulation;  the  same  hereinafter),  which  are  owned  by  the  party  undersigned  as  of  the  day 
preceding the date of application for listing (hereinafter referred to as “listing application date”) 
under  [§27],  [§60],  [§69]  and  [§76]  of  the  KOSDAQ Market  Listing  Regulation,  as  detailed  in 
subparagraph  5,  except  for  the  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  that  it  is  inevitable,  such  as 
fulfillment  of  obligations  according  to  statues  and  M&As,  etc.  and  will  not  make  the  accounts 
transfer,  establishment  and  removal  of  a  pledge  right,  sales,  withdrawal,  etc.  of  the  stocks,  etc. 
unless the Exchange deems it necessary, during the mandatory holding period.   

2.  The  party  undersigned  will  make  mandatory  holding,  accounts  transfer,  establishment  and 
removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned 
during  the  mandatory  holding  period  only  through  the  listing  sponsor,  who  is  a  managing 
underwriter pursuant to the Regulation on Securities Underwriting Business, etc. (limited to one 
(1) managing underwriter in cases where there are more than one (1) managing underwriter) among 
  Securities Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as “the listing sponsor”) and 
listing sponsors,   
will follow the methods and procedures for mandatory holding, account transfer, establishment and 
removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the relevant stocks, etc. as stipulated in the 
“agreement  on  the  provision  of  largest  shareholder’s  affirmation”  entered  into  between  the 
Company and the listing sponsor. 

3. The party undersigned will not raise any objection to the publication as a market notice by the 
listing sponsor of the facts if the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a pledge right, 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
sales,  withdrawal, etc.,  of the  stocks, etc.  owned  by  the  party  undersigned are made  during  the 
mandatory holding period. 

4.  The  party  undersigned  will  promise  to  faithfully  respond  to  the  request  of  the  Exchange  to 
confirm the fact in cases where the party undersigned, as the persons subject to mandatory holding 
of stocks, etc. violates relevant regulations by presale contract, etc., and not to raise any objection 
to any measures to be taken by the Exchange.   

5. Details of stocks, etc. under mandatory holding by persons subject to mandatory holding

related persons, professional investors, venture capitals, general corporations, individual investors, others, 
etc.  In  the  case  of  unlisted  corporations,  please  add  “(unlisted)”.  (e.g.)  (unlisted)  largest  shareholder, 
(unlisted) related person, etc. 

(2)  Please specify the type of securities under custody  such as common shares,  different class  of shares 
(convertible different class of shares, etc.), preferred shares (convertible and redeemable preferred shares, 
etc.), convertible bonds, bonds with subscription rights, subscription warrants, etc. 

(3)  Please  specify  the  number  of  shares  in  case  of  stocks  and  the  number  of  shares  to  be  converted  or 
redeemed in case of equity-linked bonds and specify the face amount of the bonds in Note column, and in 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
the case of stock options, please write down the number of stocks to be acquired by exercising the stock 
options. 

(4) Please specify the reasons for mandatory holding by classifying them into ‘mandatory holding pursuant 
to KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation’ (referring to the mandatory holding due to initial listing, merger, 
stock swap, business acquisition, asset acquisition, investment in-kind and change of the largest shareholder 
by  the  third  party  share  allotment)  and  ‘others’  (referring  to  the  capital  increase  by  private  placement, 
etc.).(In cases where there are two or more reasons for mandatory holding for the same stocks, please specify 
those reasons separately.) 

(5) In cases where the different class of stocks have different terms from those of common stocks, the details 
shall be described as a footnote.

Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding of Stocks, etc. (Supplementary Listing) 
(Pertaining to [§39], [§68] and [§71] of the Enforcement Rules) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,  
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

I and the related persons (hereinafter referred to as “the party undersigned”) hereby affirm that we will 
keep the following promises as the persons subject to mandatory holding falling under the provisions 
of [§44], [§65], and [§71] of  the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation in relation to supplementary 
listing of                Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as “the Company”) on the KOSDAQ market. 

1. The party undersigned will mandatorily hold the stocks, etc. issued by the Company (referring to 
the securities under [§2(1)10] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and including the bonus 
stocks issued pursuant to [§3] of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; 
the same hereinafter), which are owned by the party undersigned among those stocks, etc. subject to 
the  supplementary  listing  pursuant  to  [§44],  [§65],  and  [§71]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulation, as detailed in subparagraph 5, except for the cases where the Exchange deems that it is 
inevitable, such as fulfillment of obligations according to statutes and M&As, etc., and will not make 
the  accounts  transfer,  establishment  and  removal  of  a  pledge  right,  sales,  withdrawal,  etc.  of  the 
stocks, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary, during the mandatory holding period.   

2.  The  party  undersigned  will  comply  with  the  related  regulations  concerning  the  method  of 
disclosing the fact in the case of mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the persons subject to mandatory 
holding  and  the  method  of  handling the matter in the  event  that the mandatory holding  becomes 
impracticable due to the provision of the relevant stocks, etc. as collateral, etc. 

3. The party undersigned will make mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal 
of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned during 
the mandatory holding period only through the listing sponsor,   
Ltd. 
(hereinafter    referred to as “the listing sponsor”) and will not raise any objection to the publication 
as a market notice by the listing sponsor of the facts if the account transfer, establishment and removal 
of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the relevant stocks, etc. are made.

Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding of Stocks, etc. (Backdoor Listing) 
(Pertaining to [§34] of the Enforcement Rules) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,  
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

I and the related persons (hereinafter referred to as “the party undersigned”) hereby affirm that we, as 
the persons subject to mandatory holding pursuant to [§36] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, 
will  comply  with  the  following  matters  in  relation  to  the  backdoor  listing,  etc.  through  the  M&A 
between the      “A” company (hereinafter “the Company”), a KOSDAQ-listed corporation, and  “B”   
company (hereinafter “the backdoor listing target company”), an unlisted corporation,. 

. 

1.  The  party  undersigned  will  mandatorily  hold  the  stocks,  etc.  issued  by  the  Company  and  the 
backdoor listing target company (referring to the securities under [§2(1)10] of the KOSDAQ Market 
Listing Regulation and including the bonus stocks issued pursuant to [§3] of the Enforcement Rules 
of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; the same hereinafter), which are owned by the party 
undersigned  and  subject  to  [§36]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing  Regulation,  as  detailed  in 
subparagraph  5,  except  for  the  cases  where  the  Exchange  deems  that  it  is  inevitable,  such  as 
fulfillment  of  obligations  according  to  statutes  and  M&As,  etc.,  and  will  not  make  the  accounts 
transfer, establishment and removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. unless 
the Exchange deems it necessary, during the mandatory holding period.   

2.  The  party  undersigned  will  comply  with  the  related  regulations  concerning  the  method  of 
disclosing the fact in the case of mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the persons subject to mandatory 
holding  and  the  method  of  handling the matter in the  event  that the mandatory holding  becomes 
impracticable due to the provision of the relevant stocks, etc. as collateral, etc. 

3. The party undersigned will make mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal 
of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned during 
the mandatory holding period only through the financial investment company licensed for investment 
dealing business (including underwriting business) and investment brokerage business for securities 
under Article 8 of the Act and will not raise any objection to the publication as a market notice by 
the financial investment company of the facts if the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the relevant stocks, etc. are made. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
                                                           
 
 
 
 
 
4. The party undersigned will promise to faithfully respond to the request of the Exchange to confirm 
the fact in cases where the party undersigned, as the persons subject to mandatory holding of stocks, 
etc.  violates  relevant  regulations  by  presale  contract,  etc.,  and  not  to  raise  any  objection  to  any   
measures to be taken by the Exchange.

Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding of Stocks, etc.   

(Mandatory Holding in Process of Backdoor Listing) 

(Pertaining to [§34] of the Enforcement Rules) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,  
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

I and the related persons (hereinafter referred to as “the party undersigned”) hereby affirm that, with 
respect to the backdoor listing through M&A between    “A”    Co., Ltd. (hereinafter “the Company”), 
a KOSDAQ-listed corporation, and  “B” Co., Ltd., an unlisted corporation, we will comply with the 
following matters as the persons subject to mandatory holding, who fall under the mandatory holding 
in the process of backdoor listing under [§37] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation. 

. 

1. The party undersigned will mandatorily hold the stocks, etc. issued by the Company (referring to 
the securities under [§2(1)10] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and including the bonus 
stocks issued pursuant to [§3] of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; 
the same hereinafter), which are owned by the party undersigned, in accordance with [§37(1)] of the 
KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, as detailed in subparagraph 5, except for the cases where the 
Exchange deems that it is inevitable in [§37(2)] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation , and 
will not make the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, 
etc. of the stocks, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary during the mandatory holding period.   

2.  The  party  undersigned  will  comply  with  the  related  regulations  concerning  the  method  of 
disclosing the fact in the case of mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the persons subject to mandatory 
holding  and  the  method  of  handling the matter in the  event  that the mandatory holding  becomes 
impracticable due to the provision of the relevant stocks, etc. as collateral, etc. 

3. The party undersigned will make mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal 
of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned during 
the mandatory holding period only through the financial investment company licensed for investment 
dealing business (including underwriting business) and investment brokerage business for securities 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
                                                           
 
 
 
 
 
 
under Article 8 of the Act, and will not raise any objection to the publication as a market notice by 
the financial investment company of the facts if the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the relevant stocks, etc. are made. 

4. The party undersigned will promise to faithfully respond to the request of the Exchange to confirm 
the fact in cases where the party undersigned, as the persons subject to mandatory holding of stocks, 
etc.  violates  relevant  regulations  by  presale  contract,  etc.,  and  not  to  raise  any  objection  to  any 
measures to be taken by the Exchange.

fulfillment of statutory obligations and M&As, etc., until the date of three (3) months [six (6) months 
for prompt transfer companies (one (1) year for prompt transfer companies under [§31(1)3(e) or (f)] 
of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation), and one (1) year for foreign companies (however, when 
six (6) months have elapsed since the listing date, the quantity up to 5/100 of the initial holdings may 
be  sold  every  month)]  from  the  date  of  listing  of  “A”;  and  will  not  make  the  accounts  transfer, 
establishment and removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the relevant stocks unless the 
Exchange deems it necessary during the relevant period.   

2. The undersigned will faithfully respond to the request of the Exchange to confirm the fact in cases 
where the undersigned violates relevant regulations by presale contract, etc., and will not raise any 
objection to any measures to be taken by the Exchange.

I, the undersigned, hereby affirm that I will comply with the following matters as the person subject to 
mandatory holding falling under[§26(1)5] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation in relation to the 
initial listing of                              Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as “A”) on the KOSDAQ Market.

within six (6) months before the application for preliminary listing review by “A” (based on the date 
of application for preliminary listing review) until the date of six (6) months [one (1) month if the 
“disparate ratio between the public offering price and the acquisition price” specified in [§23(6)] of 
the Enforcement Rules of KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation is lower than 50%] from the listing 
date of “A”, and will not make the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a pledge right, 
sales,  withdrawal,  etc.  of  the  relevant  stocks  unless  the  Exchange  deems  it  necessary  during  the 
relevant period.   

2. To faithfully respond to the request of the Exchange to confirm the fact in cases where I violate 
relevant regulations by presale contract, etc.; and not to raise any objection to any measures to be 
taken by the Exchange.

(3) It means the “disparate ratio between the public offering price and the acquisition price” specified in 
[§23(6)] of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, where the “acquisition price” 
means the average of the acquisition prices (in the case of stocks, etc. other than stock certificates such as 
convertible  bonds,  bonds  with  warrants,  etc.,  it  may  be  calculated  by  taking  into  account  the  number  of 
shares to be converted or listed, the exercise prices, etc. at the time of calculation of the acquisition price) of 
the stocks, etc. of the concerned corporation acquired by the listing sponsor within six (6) months before the 
date of application for preliminary listing review, weighted by the acquisition quantities; the “public offering 
price”    means the price stipulated in Article 5(1) of the Regulations on Securities Underwriting Business, 
Etc.; and the “disparate ratio between the public offering price and the acquisition price” refers to the ratio 
calculated by the following formula: 

Disparate ratio between the public offering price and the acquisition price   

= (Public offering price – Acquisition price)  ÷  Acquisition price  ×  100 

(4) In cases where the different class of stocks have different terms from those of common stocks, the details 
shall be stated as a footnote. 

Affirmed by; 

Name of Company: 

Name and seal of the representative director:  

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Written Affirmation on Mandatory Holding (Paper Company and Association, etc.) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,  

                                    Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

I and the related persons (hereinafter referred to as “the party undersigned”) hereby affirm that the party 
undersigned,    as  the  largest  shareholder  of                  company  (hereinafter  referred  to  as  “the 
Company”), a KOSDAQ-listed corporation, will comply with the following matters as a person subject 
to  mandatory  holding  falling  under  the  provisions  of  [§51(1)]  of  the  KOSDAQ  Market  Listing 
Regulation. 

1. The party undersigned will mandatorily hold the stocks, etc. (referring to the securities in [§2(1)10] 
of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and including the bonus stocks issued pursuant to [§3(1)] 
of the Enforcement Rules of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation; the same hereinafter) issued 
by the Company, which are owned by the party undersigned falling under [§51(1)] of the KOSDAQ 
Market Listing Regulation, as detailed in subparagraph 5 except for the cases where the Exchange 
deems it inevitable such as fulfillment of statutory obligations and M&As, etc., and will not make 
the  accounts  transfer,  establishment  and  removal  of  a  pledge  right,  sales,  withdrawal,  etc.  of  the 
stocks, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary during the relevant period. 

2.  The  party  undersigned  will  comply  with  the  related  regulations  concerning  the  method  of 
disclosing the fact in the case of mandatory holding, accounts transfer, establishment and removal of 
a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the person subject to mandatory 
holding  and  the  method  of  handling the matter in the  event  that the mandatory holding  becomes 
impracticable due to the provision of the relevant stocks, etc. as collateral, etc. 

3. The party undersigned will make the mandatory holding,    accounts transfer, establishment and 
removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned 
during  the  mandatory  holding  period  only  through  the  financial  investment  company  licensed  of 
investment dealing business (including underwriting business) and investment brokerage business 
for the securities under Article 8 of the Act, and will not raise any objection to the publication as a 
market notice by the listing sponsor of the facts if the accounts transfer, establishment and removal 
of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc., of the relevant stocks, etc. are made. 

4. The party undersigned will faithfully respond to the request of the Exchange to confirm the fact in 
cases  where  the  party  undersigned,  as  the  persons  subject  to  mandatory  holding  violate  relevant 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
regulations by presale contract, etc., and will not raise any objection to any measures to be taken by 
the Exchange.

of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation and including the bonus stocks issued pursuant to [§3(1)]

by the Company which are owned by the party undersigned, as detailed in subparagraph 5 except for 
the cases where the Exchange deems it inevitable such as fulfillment of statutory obligations and 
M&As, etc., in accordance with [§57(11)] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation, and will not 
make the accounts transfer, establishment and removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of 
the stocks, etc. unless the Exchange deems it necessary during the relevant period.

holding  and  the  method  of  handling the matter in the  event  that the mandatory holding  becomes

removal of a pledge right, sales, withdrawal, etc. of the stocks, etc. owned by the party undersigned 
during  the  mandatory  holding  period  only  through  the  financial  investment  company  licensed  of 
investment dealing business (including underwriting business) and investment brokerage business

market notice by the listing sponsor of the facts if the accounts transfer, establishment and removal

(Pertaining to [§32] of the Enforcement Rules) 

To Chairperson of Korea Exchange,   

“A” Corporation, the party undersigned, hereby confirms that there is no doubt of following information 
pursuant to [§34] and [§64] of the KOSDAQ Market Listing Regulation with respect to asset (equity 
securities issued by unlisted corporation) acquisition from an unlisted corporation or a KONEX-listed 
corporation  (hereinafter referred to  as  “the  unlisted  corporation,  etc.”  in this form)    and  the  capital 
increase by third-party allotment, and if any false fact is found, the corporation will make no objections 
to delisting, designation and release of administrative issue, etc. taken by the Exchange based on the 
regulations and enforcement rules of the KOSDAQ market. The corporation shall also indemnify any 
and all claims and damages which may arise in connection with the breach of confirmation duty.

corporation’s view but in case of listed corporation, (listed) shall be stated in front of type (for example, (listed) 
largest shareholder and (listed) specially related parties). 

(4)  Type  of  target  stocks  such  as  common  stock,  preferred  stock,  redeemable  convertible  preferred  stock, 
convertible bond, bond with subscription right and subscription warrant shall be stated. 

(5) Name of a corporation that issued stocks subject to mandatory holding. 

6) “Listing” in case the stock is listed on KOSDAQ market and otherwise it shall be “unlisted”. 

(7) Number of stock in case of stocks and number of stock to be issued by conversion or redemption in case of 
equity-linked bonds. 

(8) The starting date of mandatory holding but if the date is undecided, leave blank 

(9) The ending date of mandatory holding reason but if the date is undecided, leave blank (e.g., Oct. 1, 2010) 

(10) The period of mandatory holding shall be stated under reason for mandatory holding (1 year, 6 months,  1 
month, etc.)

Date of preparation:

Note for description 

1. Date of preparation shall be as of the record date for closing of the register of shareholders. 

2. A corporation listed on the KOSDAQ market that has issued class stocks shall submit a summary 

table of shareholders' lists for common stocks and class stocks, respectively. 

3. Ratio or shareholding ratio shall be written to two decimal places. 

4. Within the same category, list shareholders in the order of the number of stocks held. 

5. In the remarks column of the shareholder distribution in item 1 and    the shareholder distribution 
other than the largest shareholder, etc. in item 4, the relationship with the largest shareholder and the 
position in the corporation shall be stated. 

6. “The largest shareholder” means a person who falls under [§2(1)13(a)] of the Regulation. 

7. “Related person” means a person who falls under [§2(1)13(b)] of the Regulations. 

8. “The largest shareholder, etc.” refers to a person who falls under [§2(1)13] of the Regulation. 

9. “Major shareholder” refers to a person excluding the largest shareholder, specially related person, 
and  employee  stock  ownership  association  member  from  among  major  shareholders  under 
subparagraph  6(b)  of Article  2  of  the Act  on  Governance  of  Financial  Companies.  In  this  case, 
“financial company” shall be construed as “a corporation listed on the KOSDAQ market.” 

10. In the “Minority Shareholder” column, write down those excluding the employee stock ownership 

association from among those who fall under [§2(1)16] of the Regulations. 

11. “Other shareholder” refers to any shareholder who are not corresponding to the largest shareholder, 
specially related person, major shareholder, minority shareholder, and the employee stock ownership 
association. In this case, if there are more than 10 other shareholders, the number of shareholders 
shall be entered in the column of the name of other shareholders. 

12.  “Employee  stock  ownership  association”  refers  to  the  employee  stock  ownership  association 
established in accordance with the Framework Act on Labor Welfare. In this case, the number of 
employees in the employee stock ownership association should be written in the column of the name 
of  the  employee  stock  ownership  association,  the  date  of  birth  of  the  head  of  employee  stock 
ownership association in the column of the date of birth, and the stocks owned in the name of the 
head  of  employee  stock  ownership  association  and  its  share  ownership    in  the  columns  of  the 
number of stocks owned and shareholding ratio. 

13. “Non-floating stocks” refers to stocks under [§2(1)35] of the Regulations. 

14. “Foreign investor” refers to a foreign investor in a foreign-invested company 51/100 or more of 
which stocks are held by the Korean investors from among foreign-invested companies under the 
Foreign Investment Promotion Act.
