[Annex Form No.35]    Comfort Letter of External Auditor 

Comfort Letter of External Auditor 

(Pertaining to [§64] and [Annex No. 1] of the Enforcement Rules) 

To Listing Applicant,     
Date: mm/dd/yyyy 

xxxx  Accounting  Corporation  (hereinafter  “the  Auditor”)  has  audited  (reviewed)  the  financial 
statements of ___ Co., Ltd (hereinafter “the Company”) for the year that ended on December 31, 20XX 
and June 30, 20XX and confirm following matters in relation to the application for preliminary listing 
review of foreign stocks and/or DRs to be filed on [date] by the Company. 

1.  The Auditor maintains independence from the Company according to accounting audit standards of 

OOOO in relation to the accounting audit on the financial statements of the Company. 

2.  The Auditor, for the preparation of this letter, has implemented each of the confirmation procedure 
as requested by the Company only for the financial information items as attached and requested by 
the Company among the content included in the application for preliminary listing review for foreign 
stocks/DRs. The Auditor has not implemented any additional confirmation procedure for items that 
are not enumerated in the attachment. 

(1)  The Auditor has compared the amounts and explanations in the items that are included in the 
application for preliminary listing review for foreign stocks/DRs with the concerned amount and 
descriptions in the audit (review) report on the financial statements of 20xx, and verified that 
they correspond with each other. 

(2)  The  Auditor  has  recalculated  the  ratios  and  sums  that  are  included  in  the  application  for 
preliminary listing review for foreign stocks/DRs and verified the accuracy of the calculations. 

(3)  The Auditor has compared the amounts and explanations in the items that are included in the 
application for preliminary listing review for foreign stocks/DRs with the concerned explanations 
in  the  audit  (review)  report  on  the  financial  statements  of  20xx,  and  verified  that  the  former 
explanations do not include matters that are different from the descriptions or amounts in the 
audit (review) report. 

(4)  The Auditor  has  compared  the  amounts  in  the  items  that  are  included  in  the  application  for 
preliminary listing  review for  foreign  stocks/DRs  with  the  concerned  amount  in  the  accounts 
closing report and verified that they correspond with each other. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
                 
                                                                               
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
(5)  In cases where an amount that is not included in the audit (review) report and the Company’s 
accounts closing report but included in the application for preliminary listing review for foreign 
stocks/DRs, the Auditor has compared the amount with the Company’s internal documents such 
as  accounting  records  or  analysis  data  that  the  Company  turned  in  and  verified  that  they 
correspond with each other. For the accuracy and validity of the internal documents such as the 
analysis data provided by the Company, no review was made. 

The sufficiency of the verification procedure implemented by the Auditor is under the responsibility of 
the  Company,  the  recipient  of  this  letter.  The Auditor  expresses  no  opinion  on  whether  or  not  the 
verification  procedure  falls  under  the  purpose  intended  by  the  recipient,  and  in  addition,  as  the 
verification  procedure  implemented  by  the  Auditor  is  not  the  procedure  according  to  the  OOOO 
accounting  audit  standards  (local  country’s  accounting  audit  standards,  etc.),  opinion  thereon  is  not 
expressed. 

3.  For the preparation of this letter, the Auditor implemented procedures, during the period of from 
[date] to [date] (hereinafter “subsequent period”) that the recipient deemed necessary and requested 
and the requested procedures and results are as follows: 

(1)  The  Auditor  examined  the  minutes  of  general  shareholders  meeting  and  board  of  directors 
meeting during the subsequent period. And the Company’s personnel in charge of the minutes 
stated that  all  the  minutes said  above  are turned  in  without  any  omission. The  content  of the 
general shareholders meeting and board of directors meeting are as follows: 

< Excerpt of BOD minutes dated [date] > 

-  Resolution: approved OOOO 

(2)  The Company’s personnel in charge stated that the statement of financial positions or  income 
statement as of a date or during a period of after [date] was not prepared. The Auditor, in relation 
to this, has not implemented any review procedures during the period of from [date] to [date]. 

(3)  The Auditor has made inquiries to the Company’s personnel in charge about following material 
facts, etc. and, in relation to the material facts, verified major subsidiary books, chits, etc. tuned 
in by the recipient as per the subsequent period. 

- Dishonor of a note or a check issued   
- Suspension of business operation 
- Occurrence of a disaster or a major loss 
- Selling of a large amount of fixed asset 
- Filing of a lawsuit or occurrence of a dispute 
- Change of officers 
- Merger, split-off or merger after split-off (including physical split-off or merger after physical 
split-off), transfer or acquisition of business, resolution of major asset lease or management 
entrustment, etc. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
- Issuance of shares or bonds 
- Borrowing of a large amount or borrowing from overseas 
- Change of important accounting estimation 
- Occurrence of contingent liabilities or pre-arranged events 
- Occurrence of abnormal error corrections in previous period 
- Important changes in share ownership, long-term debt, operating capital, etc. 
- In cases of a holdings company, above matters on major subsidiaries   
- Other matters that are deemed important 

To the inquiries by the Auditor about the matters above, the Company’s personnel in charge stated that 
the matters above have not occurred during the subsequent period. 

< Matters stated > 

As the above procedure  has not been executed according to the accounting audit standards, opinion 
thereon is not expressed and opinion whether the procedure falls under the purpose of the procedure, 
intended  by  the  recipient  of  this  letter,  is  not  expressed.  If  the Auditor  had  implemented  additional 
procedures or accounting audit or review, other matters to be reported to the recipient might have been 
found. 

4.  The  responsibility  of  the  description in the  application  for  preliminary listing review  for  foreign 
stocks/DRs and of determination and verification of disclosure scope, etc. remains with the Company, 
the recipient of this letter. The Auditor’s responsibility is to implement verification procedures on 
the requested  matters  and issue  this letter.  In  addition,  issuance  of this letter  does  not replace  or 
exempt the recipient’s responsibility for the content of the application for preliminary listing review 
for foreign stocks/DRs and for determination and verification of disclosure scope, etc. 

5.  As  this  letter  is  for  the  recipient’s  information  purpose  only  in  relation  to  the  application  for 
preliminary listing review for foreign stocks/DRs for the listing on the KRX, perusal or use for other 
purposes are not allowed. 

6.  This letter was prepared for the purpose of use within Korea in connection with the listing of the 

Company on the KRX. Accordingly, use in any area other than Korea is not allowed.

※  The legal disputes arising in connection with this Affirmation shall be governed by the laws of the

company”)  under  the  Monopoly  Regulation  and  Fair  Trade Act  of  financial  investment 
company stated in item 1 or of a shareholder as of application date for preliminary listing 
review in item “2” (it is limited to a case where the shareholder concerned is a corporation; 
the same in this Article)   

6. Legal entity who holds dual position as executives or staff currently or during recent 2 
years  in  the  special  purpose  acquisition  corporation  concerned,  financial  investment 
company in item “1” or shareholder as of the application date for preliminary listing review 
in item “2” 

Note. In calculating the number of stocks in item “4”, the followings shall be included: 

1. Number of stocks that may be issued by exercises of rights of stocks, etc. 

2. Number of stocks held by affiliated companies of financial investment company in sub-item “1” of item “2” 
and of shareholder as of the application date for preliminary listing review in sub-item “2” of item “2”.

Note. 

 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
1. The number of stocks to be issued shall be classified and stated separately into total number of stocks to be 
issued and the number of stocks to be allocated to existing shareholders determined by the board of directors. 

2. The subscription date (period) shall be the subscription date (period) for existing shareholders.

of shareholders), the contents of articles of association (contents of general meeting of shareholders’ resolution) 
shall be stated and in case where the transfer of subscription rights is determined by the board of directors, the 
contents of the resolution shall be stated.     

4. The date of delisting shall  be  five  (5) days (based on trading day) before the date of subscription start for 
existing shareholders.
